### [1] [Resonance near a doubly degenerate embedded eigenvalue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08554)
*Hemant Bansal,Alok Maharana,Lingaraj Sahu*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 该论文将作者先前关于共振现象的研究扩展到双简并嵌入本征值（即重数为2的本征值）的情况，引入了微分拓扑技术（莫尔斯引理）来处理这一新情况，并获得了谱密度、逗留时间、散射截面和时间延迟等重要物理量的渐近结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将作者先前关于共振现象的研究扩展到双简并嵌入本征值（doubly degenerate embedded eigenvalues）的情况，解决该情况下出现的新困难，这些困难超出了先前方法的能力范围。

Method: 引入微分拓扑技术（differential topological technique），特别是莫尔斯引理（Morse Lemma），结合先前文献中的方法，研究拉普拉斯算子在L²(ℝ³)上的秩二自伴扰动（rank-two self-adjoint perturbations）。

Result: 获得了双简并嵌入本征值附近谱密度（spectral density）的渐近结果，能够轻松处理阈值本征值（threshold eigenvalue）情况，并分析了逗留时间（sojourn time）、散射截面（scattering cross-section）和时间延迟（time delay）的渐近行为。

Conclusion: 通过引入莫尔斯引理这一微分拓扑技术，成功解决了双简并嵌入本征值情况下的共振现象研究难题，获得了重要的物理量渐近结果，并能够处理阈值本征值这一特殊情况。

Abstract: This paper extends the study of resonance phenomenon initiated by the authors in~\cite{LS} to the case of doubly degenerate embedded eigenvalues (i.e. eigenvalue of multiplicity two). A fundamentally new concept is introduced to resolve the difficulties that arise in this study, beyond the methods of \cite{LS}. We apply a differential topological technique, namely the Morse Lemma, to study the present case. This allows us to understand rank-two self-adjoint perturbations of the Laplacian on $L^{2}(\mathbb{R}^{3})$, and along with methods of \cite{LS}, we obtain asymptotic results for the spectral density near a doubly degenerate embedded eigenvalue. Importantly, we are able to easily handle the threshold eigenvalue case.
  \par We also analyze important properties which explain such resonance phenomenon, viz., asymptotic behaviour of the sojourn time, scattering cross-section and time delay.

</details>

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Coexistence Regime and Thermal Crystallization in the cavity-mediated extended Bose-Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07121)
*Wei-Wei Wang,Jin Yang,Barbara Capogrosso-Sansone,Jian-Ping Lv,Chao Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 通过路径积分蒙特卡洛方法，研究了具有腔介导长程相互作用的扩展玻色-哈伯德模型在单位填充下的有限温度行为。研究发现超流态与电荷密度波态之间存在强一级相变，低温下存在亚稳态，高温下则出现热诱导结晶现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索扩展玻色-哈伯德模型（extended Bose-Hubbard model）在有限温度下的相行为，特别关注具有腔介导长程相互作用（cavity-mediated long-range interactions）的系统在超流态与电荷密度波态共存区域的温度演化特性。

Method: 采用路径积分蒙特卡洛（path integral-Monte Carlo）方法，研究单位填充条件下的扩展玻色-哈伯德模型。通过将系统初始化为超流态或电荷密度波态两种不同构型，分别探索其温度演化路径。

Result: 当系统从超流态初始化时，加热过程会逐渐抑制超流密度（superfluid density），形成正常流体（normal fluid）；进一步升温则出现热辅助的晶体序（crystalline order）形成，最终熔化回正常流体。而从电荷密度波态初始化的系统则显示密度序的平滑热熔化，无超流相干性重现。低温下亚稳态持续存在，高温下则发生热诱导结晶（thermally induced crystallization）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了扩展玻色-哈伯德模型在有限温度下的复杂相演化行为：超流态与电荷密度波态之间的强一级相变导致低温亚稳态，而高温下热诱导结晶现象的出现表明温度对系统序参量演化具有非单调影响。

Abstract: By means of path integral- Monte Carlo, we study the finite-temperature behavior of the extended Bose-Hubbard model with cavity-mediated long-range interactions at unit filling. At zero temperature, the system supports superfluid, Mott-insulating, supersolid, and charge-density-wave phases, with a strongly first-order transition between superfluid and charge density wave states characterized by a broad coexistence region. Focusing on this coexistence regime, we explore how the dominant order evolves with temperature. When the system is initialized in a superfluid state, the superfluid density is progressively suppressed upon heating, and a normal fluid is stabilized. Upon further increasing the temperature, a thermally assisted emergence of crystalline order occurs which eventually melts into the normal fluid. In contrast, simulations initialized in a charge-density-wave configuration display a smooth thermal melting of density order, with no reemergence of superfluid coherence. Overall, our results show that metastability persists at low temperatures, but ultimately disappears at higher temperatures, where thermally induced crystallization takes place.

</details>


### [3] [Fermi-pressure-assisted cavity superradiance in a mesoscopic Fermi gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08691)
*Francesca Orsi,Ekaterina Fedotova,Rohit Prasad Bhatt,Mae Eichenberger,Léa Dubois,Jean-Philippe Brantut*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究观测了介观费米气体中超辐射相变（superradiant phase transition）的非单调密度依赖性，发现当费米波矢与反冲波矢相当时阈值最小，揭示了费米压辅助有序化与泡利阻塞（Pauli blocking）之间的交叉行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索介观尺度（几十到几千个原子）的费米气体在强光-物质耦合（light-matter coupling）下的超辐射相变行为，特别是在宽密度范围内该相变阈值的变化规律。

Method: 实验方法采用高精细度光学腔（high-finesse cavity）中的$^6$Li原子费米气体，通过改变原子密度研究超辐射阈值的变化，并分析原子数依赖性和光子数标度关系。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）超辐射阈值随密度呈非单调变化，在费米波矢与反冲波矢（recoil wavevectors）相当时达到最小值；2）该最小值对应费米压辅助有序化与光子散射泡利阻塞之间的交叉；3）在特定参数下实现了具有自旋密度波（spin-density-wave）特性的有序相。

Conclusion: 结论表明该介观系统为研究强相干光-物质耦合下的少费米子体系提供了新平台，实验结果与理论预测良好吻合，揭示了费米统计在超辐射相变中的关键作用。

Abstract: We study the superradiant phase transition of a mesoscopic Fermi gas comprising between a few tens and a few thousand $^6$Li atoms in a high-finesse cavity across a wide range of densities. We observe a non-monotonic variation of the superradiant threshold as a function of density, with a minimum reached when the Fermi and recoil wavevectors are comparable. The minimum corresponds to a crossover between Fermi pressure-assisted ordering and Pauli blocking of photon scattering, in good agreement with theory. This interpretation is confirmed by a study of the atom-number dependence of the ordering threshold and photon number scaling. Lastly, we demonstrate the operation of our mesoscopic system in a regime where light-induced forces are opposite for the two spin components, leading to an ordered phase with a spin-density-wave character. Our system opens the perspective of studying few-fermion systems with strong and coherent light-matter coupling.

</details>

### [4] [Reply to the comment on "Instability of the ferromagnetic quantum critical point and symmetry of the ferromagnetic ground state in 2D and 3D electron gases with arbitrary spin-orbit splitting''](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06825)
*Dmitry Miserev,Daniel Loss,Jelena Klinovaja*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文是对D. Belitz和T. R. Kirkpatrick评论的回应，针对原论文中关于二维和三维电子气中任意自旋轨道分裂下铁磁量子临界点不稳定性和铁磁基态对称性的研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在回应D. Belitz和T. R. Kirkpatrick对作者先前论文的评论，澄清关于二维和三维电子气中铁磁量子临界点不稳定性和铁磁基态对称性研究的争议点。

Method: 采用回复评论的形式，针对评论中提出的质疑进行逐点回应和澄清，基于原论文的理论框架和分析方法。

Result: 通过回应澄清了原论文的观点，维护了关于铁磁量子临界点（ferromagnetic quantum critical point）不稳定性和铁磁基态（ferromagnetic ground state）对称性在二维和三维电子气中的结论。

Conclusion: 作者通过系统回应评论中的质疑，进一步巩固了原论文关于自旋轨道分裂（spin-orbit splitting）对铁磁量子临界点稳定性和铁磁基态对称性影响的理论分析。

Abstract: We reply on the comment of D. Belitz and T. R. Kirkpatrick on our article ``Instability of the ferromagnetic quantum critical point and symmetry of the ferromagnetic ground state in 2D and 3D electron gases with arbitrary spin-orbit splitting''.

</details>


### [5] [Flat Topological Nodal Lines in Heavy-Fermion Compound CeCoGe$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06966)
*Yuting Wang,Weikang Wu,Jianzhou Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论结合动力学平均场理论，揭示了重费米子材料CeCoGe₃作为拓扑节线Kondo半金属的原型特征，展示了强关联、非平庸拓扑与超导性的共存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索强电子关联、非常规超导性与对称性保护拓扑之间的相互作用，为重费米子材料CeCoGe₃中的奇异量子态提供理论基础。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）结合动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）计算，分析CeCoGe₃的关联电子结构与拓扑性质。

Result: 结果显示从高温非相干态到低温相干重准粒子的交叉转变，在25K时质量增强因子达52.6；电子关联、自旋轨道耦合与非中心对称I4mm晶体对称性共同稳定了费米能级10meV内的平拓扑节线。

Conclusion: CeCoGe₃被确立为拓扑节线Kondo半金属的原型材料，其强关联、非平庸能带拓扑与超导性的共存表明该材料是实现拓扑超导性的潜在候选体系。

Abstract: The interplay between strong electronic correlations, unconventional superconductivity, and symmetry-protected topology provides a fertile ground for discovering exotic quantum states. In this work, we investigate the correlated electronic structure and topological properties of the heavy fermion material CeCoGe$_3$ using density functional theory combined with dynamical mean-field theory calculations. Our results reveal a crossover from high temperature incoherent states to low temperature coherent heavy quasiparticles, accompanied by a mass enhancement of $m^*/m_{\text{DFT}}\sim 52.6$ at $T=25$ K. The interplay between electronic correlation, spin-orbit coupling and the noncentrosymmetric $I4mm$ crystal symmetry stabilize flat topological nodal lines within 10 meV of the Fermi level, which could contribute a significant density of states. The proximity of topological nodal lines to the Fermi surface suggests a potential role in mediating pressure induced unconventional superconductivity. Our work establishes CeCoGe$_3$ as a prototype topological nodal line Kondo semimetal. The coexistence of strong correlation, non-trivial band topology and superconductivity indicate CeCoGe$_3$ as a potential candidate for realizing topological superconductivity.

</details>


### [6] [Coherent-state ansatz for the Holstein polaron in one and two dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07290)
*Connor M. Walsh,Igor Boettcher,Frank Marsiglio*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究针对Holstein模型中电子-声子强耦合情况下极化子（polaron）基态描述的困难，提出了一种基于相干态（coherent states）变分波函数的半解析近似方法，在强耦合和弱耦合区域均表现出优异的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Holstein模型常作为固体中电子-声子相互作用和极化子形成的原型，但当声子频率较小且电子-声子耦合较强时，由于基态中存在大量声子，对Holstein极化子的精确描述变得困难。

Method: 提出了一种半解析近似方法，采用变分波函数（variational ansatz），其中电子周围环绕着以相干态形式存在的声子云（phonon clouds）。该方法在Lang-Firsov极限下变得特别简单且精确。

Result: 确定了该近似方法在偏离Lang-Firsov极限时的有效域，并进一步探索了去除声子云必须形成相干态要求后的改进效果。两种近似在强耦合下表现极好，在弱耦合下也表现出令人惊讶的良好性能。

Conclusion: 相干态变分波函数为极化子基态波函数提供了简单直观的图像，同时能够准确预测基态能量和有效质量（effective mass）。

Abstract: The Holstein model often serves as an archetype for electron-phonon interactions and polaron formation in solids. However, precise descriptions of the Holstein polaron are difficult when the phonon frequency is small and the electron-phonon coupling is strong, due to the presence of many phonons in the ground state. We present a semi-analytical approximation that consists of a variational ansatz with clouds of phonons surrounding the electron in the form of coherent states. This becomes particularly simple and exact in the Lang-Firsov limit. We determine the domain of validity away from this limit, and further explore the improvement achieved with a removal of the requirement that the phonon clouds form coherent states. Both approximations work extremely well at strong coupling, and both work surprisingly well also at weak coupling. The coherent-state ansatz provides a simple and intuitive picture of the polaron ground-state wavefunction, and in addition predicts accurate values for the ground-state energy and effective mass.

</details>


### [7] [Fractional Topological Phases, Flat Bands, and Robust Edge States on Finite Cyclic Graphs via Single-Coin Split-Step Quantum Walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07701)
*Dinesh Kumar Panda,Colin Benjamin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究首次在有限循环图上实现了完全幺正、非相互作用的离散时间量子行走中的分数量子拓扑相，通过单硬币分步循环量子行走协议发现了传统循环量子行走无法实现的拓扑现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索传统循环量子行走（cyclic quantum walk）动力学无法实现的拓扑现象，特别是在有限循环图上实现分数量子拓扑相（fractional topological phase），为小规模合成量子系统提供可实验实现的平台。

Method: 采用单硬币分步循环量子行走（SCSS-CQW）协议，通过步依赖参数（step-dependency parameter）和硬币旋转角（coin-rotation angle）控制准能谱（quasienergy spectra）、平带（flat bands）和拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）的工程化设计。

Result: 研究发现偶数和奇数位点循环图具有本质不同的能带结构，旋转平带仅出现在4n位点循环中；SCSS-CQW产生分数绕数±1/2（Zak相位±π/2），与传统量子行走的整数不变量形成鲜明对比，这些分数不变量导致非常规的体-边界对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）并支持超越常规整数拓扑分类的边缘态（edge states）。

Conclusion: 该方案仅需与演化时间无关的恒定数量探测器，为在小规模合成量子系统中实现分数拓扑、平带和受保护边缘态提供了最小资源消耗且实验可访问的平台，数值模拟显示这些态在动态和静态硬币无序以及相位保持扰动下保持稳定。

Abstract: We report the first realization of a fractional topological phase in a fully unitary, noninteracting discrete-time quantum walk implemented on finite cyclic graphs. Using a single-coin split-step cyclic quantum walk (SCSS-CQW), we uncover topological phenomena that are inaccessible within conventional cyclic quantum-walk dynamics. The protocol enables controlled engineering of quasienergy spectra, flat bands, and topological phase transitions through the step-dependency parameter and coin-rotation angle. We show that cyclic graphs with even and odd numbers of sites exhibit qualitatively different band structures, while rotational flat bands arise exclusively in $4n$-site cycles; a general analytic condition for their emergence is derived. The SCSS-CQW produces fractional winding numbers $\pm \frac{1}{2}$ (Zak phases $\pm \fracπ{2}$), in sharp contrast with the integer invariants of standard quantum walks. These fractional invariants lead to an unconventional bulk--boundary correspondence and support edge states beyond the usual integer topological classification. In the step-dependent protocol, transitions between distinct fractional winding sectors generate robust edge modes. Numerical simulations show that these states remain stable in the presence of both dynamic and static coin disorder as well as phase-preserving perturbations, while survival-probability analysis demonstrates their long-time persistence. Requiring only a constant number of detectors independent of the evolution time, the proposed scheme offers a minimal-resource and experimentally accessible platform for realizing fractional topology, flat bands, and protected edge states in small-scale synthetic quantum systems.

</details>


### [8] [Alleviating Projection-Space Sensitivity in DFT+U via Renormalized U](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07340)
*Manjula Raman,Kenneth Park*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过约束DFT计算揭示了DFT+U方法中有效库仑相互作用U_eff对投影空间尺寸的显著依赖性，并提出通过重新计算每个投影尺寸对应的U_eff值来消除计算结果的不一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管DFT+U方法显著改善了关联电子系统的描述，但其准确性严重依赖于输入参数，包括用于哈伯德修正的局部投影空间。使用不同投影尺寸的计算可能产生定量不同甚至发散的结果。

Method: 采用约束DFT（constrained DFT）计算研究金红石TiO₂和β-MnO₂中有效库仑相互作用U_eff对投影尺寸的依赖性，通过自洽计算分析不同投影尺寸下的U_eff变化。

Result: 随着投影尺寸增大，自洽计算的U_eff显著降低，降幅高达33%。这种趋势归因于通过轨道弛豫和增强屏蔽导致的库仑相互作用重整化（renormalization）。当使用针对每个投影尺寸重新计算的U_eff值时，晶格参数、电子结构和相对相稳定性在不同投影尺寸下变得一致。

Conclusion: 这些发现为缓解DFT+U计算中的投影尺寸依赖性提供了实用途径，通过针对特定投影尺寸重新计算U_eff参数，可以获得一致且可靠的计算结果。

Abstract: Although the DFT+U method significantly improves the description of correlated electronic systems, its accuracy is known to depend strongly on the input parameters including local projection space used for the Hubbard correction. As a result, calculations performed with different projection sizes can yield quantitatively different -- and sometimes divergent -- results. In this work, we investigate the dependence of the effective Coulomb interaction $U_{\mathrm{eff}}$ on projection size using constrained DFT calculations for rutile TiO$_2$ and $β$-MnO$_2$. We find that as the projection size increases, the self-consistently calculated $U_{\mathrm{eff}}$ decreases significantly -- by as much as $33$\%. This trend is attributed to renormalization of the Coulomb interaction through orbital relaxation and enhanced screening. When $U_{\mathrm{eff}}$ values recalculated for each projection size are employed, the results for lattice parameters, electronic structure, and relative phase stability become consistent across different projection sizes. These findings can provide a practical route to alleviate projection-size dependence in DFT+U calculations.

</details>


### [9] [Qubit discretizations of d=3 conformal field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07420)
*Hansen S. Wu,Ribhu K. Kaul*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出利用近期量子计算平台研究三维共形场论（conformal field theory）的标度维度（scaling dimensions），通过在多面体晶格上选择特定耦合参数，可从仅20个量子比特的系统中以数个百分点精度提取标度维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维共形场论是经典计算机难以解决的前沿问题，但可能通过量子模拟得到解决。论文旨在利用近期量子比特平台研究此类理论，为量子计算在量子场论领域的应用开辟新途径。

Method: 方法是在多面体晶格（polyhedral lattice）上选择量子多体问题的特定耦合参数，使得共形状态-算符对应（conformal state-operator correspondence）能在谱中得到最精确观测。该方法仅需少量假设，主要基于一般共形不变性（conformal invariance）。

Result: 在伊辛模型（Ising model）上验证了该协议，从仅20个量子比特系统的谱中提取了多个标度算符（scaling operators）的标度维度，精度达到几个百分点。这证明了该方法在近期量子比特平台上的可行性。

Conclusion: 三维共形场论为当前或近期量子比特平台提供了独特机遇——这是一个经典计算机难以解决但可通过量子模拟解决的前沿问题。论文讨论了在量子计算机上实现该方案的要求和挑战。

Abstract: We propose that scaling dimensions of d=3 conformal field theories can be studied on a system of qubits with near term quantum simulation platforms. Our proposal chooses couplings of quantum many-body problems on a polyhedral lattice at which the conformal state-operator correspondence can be observed most accurately in the spectrum. We validate our protocol on the Ising model where we extract the scaling dimensions of a number of scaling operators with a few percent accuracy from the spectrum of a system of just 20 qubits. The procedure makes only minor assumptions beyond general conformal invariance -- it may hence be applied widely. Requirements and challenges to realize this proposal on quantum computers are discussed. Our results demonstrate that for current or near term qubit platforms, three dimensional conformal field theories present a unique opportunity -- a forefront problem that is difficult on classical computers but may be solved through quantum simulation.

</details>

Result: 该代码已针对常见代表性磁系统的文献结果进行了全面基准测试，证明其可靠性和准确性，为研究人员提供了一个探索复杂磁系统热力学性质的多功能平台。

Abstract: Monte Carlo (MC) simulations are powerful computational tools for investigating thermodynamic behavior and validating analytical approaches in complex physical systems. Here we present ETHER (Efficient Tool for THermodynamics Exploration via Relaxations), an open-source MC simulation package, developed for studying temperature-dependent magnetic properties in spin systems. ETHER enables large-scale MC simulations of various spin systems to analyze phase transitions, critical behavior, and complex magnetic structures. The package constructs spin-lattice networks from standard structural input files and supports exchange interaction definitions through user-specified neighbor lists. It also provides tools for easy visualization and post-processing of simulation outputs. Our code has been benchmarked thoroughly against results reported in the literature for common representative magnetic systems. This user-friendly code offers researchers a versatile platform for exploring thermodynamic properties of complex magnetic systems.

### [11] [Spin Group Symmetry Criteria For Unconventional Magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07643)
*Xun-Jiang Luo,Jin-Xin Hu,Mengli Hu,K. T. Law*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于自旋空间群（spin space group）的统一框架，为非常规磁体（unconventional magnets）中的偶宇称磁体（EPMs）和奇宇称磁体（OPMs）建立了全面的对称性判据，并发现了多种新的对称性驱动机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非常规磁体通常被分为偶宇称磁体（even-parity magnets, EPMs）和奇宇称磁体（odd-parity magnets, OPMs）两类，它们分别表现出在动量反演下相同和相反的自旋劈裂（spin splittings）。目前缺乏一个统一的对称性框架来全面分类和理解这两类磁体。

Method: 本文建立了一个基于自旋空间群（spin space group）的统一框架，为EPMs和OPMs建立了全面的对称性判据。该框架将两类磁体根据自旋纹理（spin textures）分为三类：共线型（collinear, type-I）、共面型（coplanar, type-II）和非共面型（noncoplanar, type-III）。

Result: 该框架不仅完成了对EPMs和OPMs的完整分类，还发现了多种新的对称性驱动机制：为OPMs识别出8种不同的机制，为EPMs识别出7种机制。其中，交替磁体（altermagnets）自然成为EPMs的一种特定机制。基于这些判据，从Magndata数据库中识别出许多候选材料，实现了OPMs和EPMs的一些新对称性机制。

Conclusion: 这项工作为理解、预测和设计非常规磁性材料建立了一个基础的对称性框架，统一了偶宇称磁体和奇宇称磁体的分类，并揭示了多种新的对称性驱动机制。

Abstract: Unconventional magnetism has typically been classified into two fundamental classes: even-parity magnets (EPMs) and odd-parity magnets (OPMs). These two classes exhibit identical and opposite spin splittings, respectively, under momentum inversion, while both maintain symmetry-compensated magnetization. In this Letter, we present a unified spin space group-based framework that establishes comprehensive symmetry criteria for both classes. Our framework not only yields a complete classification of EPMs and OPMs but also uncovers a wealth of new symmetry-driven mechanisms for them. Specifically, we classify both classes into three types based on their spin textures: collinear (type-I), coplanar (type-II), and noncoplanar (type-III), and we demonstrate that both classes can be realized across collinear, coplanar, and noncoplanar magnetic orders. We identify eight distinct symmetry-driven mechanisms for OPMs and seven for EPMs, among which some paradigms of unconventional magnetism, for instance, altermagnets naturally emerge as one specific mechanism of EPMs. Using these established criteria, we identify numerous candidate materials from the Magndata database, realizing some new symmetry mechanisms for OPMs and EPMs. Our work establishes a foundational symmetry framework for understanding, predicting, and designing unconventional magnetic materials.

### [12] [Weyl excitonic condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07665)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索二维半填充Su-Schrieffer-Heeger晶格中长程库仑电子-空穴吸引相互作用的作用，揭示拓扑性与激子集体行为交织产生的新型物质态。

Method: 通过自洽计算粒子-空穴配对能隙在整个布里渊区的完整动量依赖性，分析Weyl点附近的配对能隙特征，并讨论该新型物质态的实验实现可能性。

Result: 发现了一种独特的激子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚态，其粒子-空穴配对能隙在整个布里渊区具有非零实部和虚部，但在两条不同节线上分别消失，这两条节线相交于两个具有相反赝自旋手性的Weyl点，这些Weyl点作为Berry流量的源和汇，导致了Bogoliubov-deGennes费米弧边缘态的形成。

Conclusion: 在特定条件下，拓扑性与激子集体行为的罕见交织产生了一种新型物质态，其特征包括激子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚、赝自旋手性纹理、Weyl点结构以及时间反演对称性破缺的p_x+ip_y配对特征，为实验探索提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We consider a half-filled two-dimensional Su-Schrieffer-Heeger lattice and examine the role of the long-range Coulomb electron-hole attractive interaction. We demonstrate that, under specific conditions, a rare interplay of topological and excitonic-collective behavior emerges as a novel state of matter. A unique Bose-Einstein condensate of excitons forms, exhibiting co-presence of pseudo-spin chiral texture. The emerging complex order-parameter, a particle-hole pairing-gap, has non-zero real and imaginary parts throughout the Brillouin zone (BZ) but vanish separately on two different nodal lines, which intersect at two Weyl points. The Weyl nodes possess opposite pseudo-spin chiralities, which act as source and drain of a Berry-flux associated with the particle-hole pairing-wavefunction, and are the cause of Bogoliubov-deGennes Fermi-arc edge-states. We self-consistently calculate the full momentum-dependence of the particle-hole pairing gap throughout the entire BZ. Near the Weyl points, the pairing gap exhibits the unconventional time-reversal-symmetry breaking $p_x+ip_y$ character. Finally, we discuss general potential experimental realizations of this novel state of matter.

### [13] [Magnetic and electrical transport properties of the single-crystalline half-Heusler antiferromagnet DyNiSb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07702)
*Abhinav Agarwal,Prabuddha Kant Mishra,Orest Pavlosiuk,Maciej J. Winiarski,Piotr Wisniewski,Dariusz Kaczorowski*

TL;DR: DyNiSb单晶在低温下表现出两个磁相变（7.3K和3.4K），与多晶样品仅观察到一个转变不同。样品呈现金属性导电行为，而非多晶的半导性。磁阻测量显示弱反局域化效应和场致费米面重构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前对DyNiSb多晶样品的研究仅报告单一磁相变和半导体行为，本研究旨在通过高质量单晶样品探究其真实的低温热力学和磁输运性质，揭示结构无序对物性的影响。

Method: 采用高质量DyNiSb单晶样品，通过磁化率、热容和电阻率测量研究低温热力学性质。在横向和纵向配置下进行磁阻测量，并开展角度依赖的电阻率研究以分析磁场效应。

Result: 发现两个清晰的磁相变：TN1 = 7.3 K和TN2 = 3.4 K。样品表现出金属性导电（metal-like conductivity），而非多晶的半导体行为。小磁场下观察到弱反局域化效应（weak antilocalization effect），高温时转变为正单调磁阻。角度依赖电阻率显示从四重对称向二重对称的交叉，表明场致费米面重构（field-induced reconstruction of the Fermi surface）。

Conclusion: DyNiSb表现出复杂的磁性和电输运行为，对结构无序高度敏感且易受外磁场调控。单晶与多晶样品的显著差异凸显了样品质量对准确表征半赫斯勒化合物物性的重要性。

Abstract: High-quality single crystals of the half-Heusler compound DyNiSb were investigated for their low temperature thermodynamic and magnetotransport properties. Magnetic susceptibility, heat capacity, and electrical resistivity measurements revealed two distinct magnetic phase transitions at TN1 = 7.3 K and TN2 = 3.4 K, contrasting with previous reports on polycrystalline samples, which identified only a single transition near TN2 . Moreover, the studied samples were found to exhibit Metal like conductivity, at odds with a semiconducting behavior reported for the polycrystals. Magnetoresistance measurements performed in both transverse and longitudinal configurations revealed in small magnetic fields a weak antilocalization effect that diminishes with increasing temperature, giving way to a positive, monotonic magnetoresistance at high temperatures. Angular-dependent resistivity studies showed a crossover from fourfold to twofold symmetry with increasing magnetic-field strength, suggesting a field-induced reconstruction of the Fermi surface. Our findings highlight a complex magnetic and electrical transport behavior in DyNiSb, highly sensitive to structural disorder and easily tunable by external magnetic field.

Abstract: We report the thermodynamic and magnetotransport properties of the half-Heusler antimonide ErPdSb, studied on single-crystalline samples in wide ranges of temperature and magnetic fields. The compound was found to order antiferromagnetically at 1.2 K. In the paramagnetic state, it shows semimetallic behavior with a broad hump in the temperature-dependent electrical resistivity around 70 K. The results of ab initio calculations of the electronic structure of ErPdSb indicated a bulk insulating nature. In small magnetic fields the magnetoresistance is driven by a weak antilocalization effect, while in strong fields it is negative and describable by the deGennes-Friedel formalism. The Hall effect data indicated that holes are the dominant charge carriers. At 2 K, the Hall conductivity exhibits a sizable anomalous contribution, which is obscured by multiband effects at higher temperatures. The angular magnetoresistance shows unusual features as functions of magnetic field and temperature, pointing to a possible field-induced reconstruction of the Fermi surface.

Conclusion: 该研究提供了先前无法获得的巨磁阻切换实空间太赫兹视图，建立了一个通用分析框架，用于在超越传统sSNOM分辨率的空间尺度上映射自旋-电荷-晶格-轨道耦合动力学。

Abstract: Resolving sub-10 nm spin switching and the associated terahertz (THz) electrodynamics during the colossal magnetoresistance (CMR) transition is a definitive frontier in reaching the fundamental spatial, temporal, and energy-dissipation limits of spin-based microelectronics and quantum logic architectures. Yet, the requirement of simultaneous control of high magnetic field, cryogenic environment, and nanometer-scale resolution has remained an elusive benchmark for terahertz nanoscopy, leaving the obscured nano-scale high-frequency dynamics of these transitions largely unexplored. Here, we overcome these limitations by utilizing a custom-built cryogenic magneto-THz scattering-type scanning near-field optical microscopy (cm-THz-sSNOM) platform to resolve the nanoscale, THz spectroscopic evolution of the magnetic field-driven CMR transition in a manganite single crystal $\text{Pr}_{2/3}\text{Ca}_{1/3}\text{MnO}_{3}$. Our measurements provide a real-space visualization of the local THz conductivity, capturing the moment that magnetic-field-induced spin switching triggers the phase transition from an antiferromagnetic insulator to a ferromagnetic metal. THz nano-imaging, together with an ellipsoidal near-field model, reveals a multi-scale transition initiated by 1-2 nm isolated spin-flip sites at low magnetic fields, which coalesce into $\sim$15~nm conducting regions as the threshold field is approached. These results provide an in situ, previously inaccessible THz real-space view of CMR switching, establishing a general analysis framework for mapping spin-charge-lattice-orbit-coupled dynamics at spatial scales that transcend the nominal sSNOM resolution.

Conclusion: Cs₂CoI₄的结构相变导致对称性降低，这对磁相互作用产生重要影响。研究成功建立了能捕获实验观测的最小磁模型，为理解这类受挫磁体家族的结构-磁性关联提供了新见解。

Unlike previously studied members, Cs$_2$CoI$_4$ undergoes a structural phase transition, for which we determine the low-temperature crystallographic structure. The resulting symmetry reduction strongly affects both the magnetic exchange interactions and single-ion anisotropy. ### [17] [Microscopic theory of flexo Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya-type interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08356)
*Takehito Yokoyama*

TL;DR: 该研究基于微扰理论分析了弯曲磁体表面上巡游电子介导的两个磁性杂质之间的相互作用，发现即使没有自旋轨道耦合，弯曲引起的非均匀自旋织构也能产生Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya型相互作用，并在一维环模型中验证了这一效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用微扰理论（perturbation theory）分析弯曲磁体表面上的相互作用机制，并在一维环模型（one-dimensional ring model）中具体演示该效应。

Result: 研究发现弯曲引起的非均匀自旋织构（inhomogeneous spin texture）能够产生Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya型相互作用，即使在没有自旋轨道耦合的情况下也能实现，并获得了该相互作用的解析表达式。

Conclusion: 研究证明弯曲磁体的几何曲率可以诱导出Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya型相互作用，这为在没有自旋轨道耦合的材料中实现此类相互作用提供了新机制。

Abstract: We study interaction between two magnetic impurities mediated by itinerant electrons on the surface of curved magnets based on perturbation theory. We show that Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya type interaction can arise from inhomogeneous spin texture by bending, without any spin-orbit coupling. Analytical expressions of the Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya type interaction are obtained. We demonstrate this effect in a one-dimensional ring model.

### [18] [Stochastic Loop Corrections to Belief Propagation for Tensor Network Contraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08427)
*Gi Beom Sim,Tae Hyeon Park,Kwang S. Kim,Yanmei Zang,Xiaorong Zou,Hye Jung Kim,D. ChangMo Yang,Soohaeng Yoo Willow,Chang Woo Myung*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种混合方法，通过随机采样环修正来改进信念传播（BP），从而在具有环的图上获得精确的张量网络收缩结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 张量网络收缩（tensor network contraction）是量子多体物理、统计力学和机器学习中的基本计算挑战。信念传播（belief propagation, BP）虽然提供高效近似解，但在具有环（loops）的图上会引入系统性误差。

Method: 该方法将配分函数（partition function）精确分解为BP贡献和环修正因子，后者对所有有效环构型求和。采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov chain Monte Carlo）结合伞形采样（umbrella sampling）来采样环构型，确保在所有相关强度下的高效探索。

Result: 该方法在二维铁磁伊辛模型（two-dimensional ferromagnetic Ising model）上得到验证，能够为任何具有对称边势（symmetric edge potentials）的成对马尔可夫随机场（pairwise Markov random field）提供无偏估计，且统计误差可控。

Conclusion: 该随机方法通过采样环修正来克服BP在环状图上的局限性，实现了在任意参数区域内的精确计算，为张量网络收缩问题提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Tensor network contraction is a fundamental computational challenge underlying quantum many-body physics, statistical mechanics, and machine learning. Belief propagation (BP) provides an efficient approximate solution, but introduces systematic errors on graphs with loops. Here, we introduce a hybrid method that achieves exact results by stochastically sampling loop corrections to BP and showcase our method by applying it to the two-dimensional ferromagnetic Ising model. For any pairwise Markov random field with symmetric edge potentials, our approach exploits an exact factorization of the partition function into the BP contribution and a loop correction factor summing over all valid loop configurations, weighted by edge weights derived directly from the potentials. We sample this sum using Markov chain Monte Carlo with moves that preserve the loop constraint, combined with umbrella sampling to ensure efficient exploration across all correlation strengths. Our stochastic approach provides unbiased estimates with controllable statistical error in any parameter regime.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用共振弹性X射线散射测量技术，结合磁对称性分析和方位角依赖性研究，解析材料的磁性结构。

Result: 确定基态磁序为单-q非公度共线（single-q incommensurate, collinear）磁序，在16 K相变以上向公度波矢滑动；磁矩沿面内a轴方向排列，形成矩调制自旋密度波态（moment-modulated spin density wave state）。

Conclusion: 成功解析了GdNiSn₄的磁性基态结构，并讨论了观察到的磁序与该方形网格化合物电子性质之间的关联。

Abstract: We characterize the magnetic ground state of the newly synthesized lanthanide intermetallic GdNiSn$_4$ via resonant elastic x-ray scattering measurements. This compound forms distorted square nets of Gd that initially order magnetically below 23 K followed by a lower temperature transition at 16 K. Our scattering data identify the ground state order as a single-$q$ incommensurate, collinear order that slides towards a commensurate wave vector above the 16 K transition. Magnetic symmetry analysis combined with azimuthal dependence resolves the ground state magnetic structure as a moment-modulated spin density wave state with Gd moments oriented parallel to the in-plane a-axis. We discuss connections between the observed magnetic order and electronic properties in this square-net compound.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用最先进的矩阵乘积态（matrix product state）模拟方法，在YC6圆柱几何上研究J2/J1 = 0.125参数点的两个基态扇区。通过比较静态关联函数和高分辨率的动态结构因子（dynamical structure factors）来分析两个扇区的性质差异。

Result: 两个扇区在静态关联中已显示出明显差异，而高分辨率动态结构因子进一步揭示了它们在低能激发（low-energy excitations）方面的本质区别。这些差异表明两个基态不能简单理解为有隙Z2自旋液体的不同拓扑扇区。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，先前将两个近简并基态解释为Z2自旋液体不同拓扑扇区的观点可能过于简化，两个基态之间的差异超出了单纯拓扑扇区区别的范畴。

Abstract: It is generally believed that the spin-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ triangular-lattice $J_1$-$J_2$ Heisenberg model hosts a quantum spin liquid in the intermediate regime between the $120^\circ$ and stripe ordered phases. Density matrix renormalization group studies on cylinders have consistently found two nearly degenerate ground states, commonly interpreted as distinct topological sectors. Using state-of-the-art matrix product state simulations on YC6 cylinders, we compare the static and dynamical properties of these two sectors at $J_2/J_1 = 0.125$. Noticeable differences appear already in static correlations; moreover, high-resolution dynamical structure factors reveal qualitatively distinct low-energy excitations. These results suggest that the two ground states cannot be understood as merely topologically distinct sectors of a gapped $\mathbb{Z}_2$ spin liquid.

### [21] [Understanding thermal and quantum fluctuations in extended Kitaev-Yao-Lee spin-orbital model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08710)

Method: 采用经典蒙特卡洛模拟（classical Monte Carlo simulations）和适用于自旋轨道模型的广义自旋波理论（generalized spin wave theory），系统研究热涨落和量子涨落对自旋轨道模型的影响。

Conclusion: 自旋轨道模型中的额外自由度通过增强热涨落和量子涨落，促进了无序相（特别是向列相）的形成和稳定，这为理解复杂量子材料中的新奇物态提供了重要理论框架。

Abstract: Building upon the spin-1/2 Kitaev model on a honeycomb lattice, the Yao-Lee spin-orbital model provides exactly solvable quantum spin liquids with potentially better stability against perturbations due to the additional degree of freedom. Recently, the microscopic mechanism underlying the Yao-Lee interaction in honeycomb materials has been uncovered, leading to an extended Kitaev-Yao-Lee spin-orbital model when the celebrated Kugel-Khomskii interaction is included. Numerical studies of this model have identified various disordered phases, including a broad region of the nematic phase that is reminiscent of a spin-orbital liquid. Here, we investigate the origin and stability of this nematic phase via thermal and quantum fluctuations using classical Monte Carlo simulations and a generalized spin wave theory appropriate for the spin-orbital model. We demonstrate that the additional spin-orbital degree of freedom gives rise to strong thermal and quantum fluctuations in spin-orbital models, providing insight into the emergence of disordered phases.

Despite their importance, black hole-neutron star mergers remain relatively less studied and therefore not yet well understood, largely due to the lack of publicly available numerical relativity setups suitable for such investigations. In this work, we present a fully reproducible black hole-neutron star merger simulation performed exclusively using Einstein Toolkit thorns, targeting the detected event \texttt{GW230529}. We review key challenges and modeling approaches, focusing on partial differential equation (PDE) frameworks. Borrowed from statistical physics, PDEs capture spatial heterogeneity, anisotropy, stochasticity, and feedbacks between land use and transport networks. Integrating economic and institutional factors remains a major challenge for policy relevance. We propose a research agenda that bridges remote sensing, urban economics, and complexity science to develop dynamic, empirically grounded models of urban expansion.

### [24] [Explicit Construction of Floquet-Bloch States from Arbitrary Solution Bases of the Hill Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07855)

### [25] [Fluctuation imaging of disorder in monolayer semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07418)
*Tom T. C. Sistermans,Rasmus H. Godiksen,Sara A. Elrafei,Alberto G. Curto*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种超分辨荧光涨落显微技术，用于成像单层半导体中的局域激子涨落，从而识别材料中的不稳定位点。该方法能够检测与原子力显微镜和超光谱成像相似的界面无序特征，但实施更快速简便，为评估单层半导体质量提供了有前景的工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单层半导体在纳米电子学、光电子学和光子学中具有巨大潜力，但其光学性质由激子主导。由于激子电场延伸到单层外部，它们对环境敏感，无序会导致激子不稳定性，这对器件性能、可扩展性和可重复性产生不利影响。

Method: 研究采用超分辨荧光涨落显微技术（super-resolution fluorescence fluctuation microscopy）成像单层半导体中的局域激子涨落。通过比较不同基底材料，分析界面无序对涨落的影响，并利用超光谱成像（hyperspectral imaging）进一步探究无序来源。同时评估了热退火处理对无序的减少效果。

Result: 该方法能够识别连续单层中具有恒定荧光的区域内的不稳定位点，这些位点与原子力显微镜测量的界面无序相对应。不同材料界面对激子涨落有显著影响，热退火处理可减少无序，表现为涨落的降低。荧光涨落成像能够检测与原子力显微镜和超光谱成像相似的无序特征。

Conclusion: 荧光涨落成像技术比原子力显微镜和超光谱成像更快速且易于实施，是评估单层半导体质量的有前景方法，特别是在与纳米光电器件中的纳米结构和异质结构集成时具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Monolayer semiconductors hold great potential for nanoscale electronics, optoelectronics, and photonics. Excitons dominate their optical properties. As their electric fields extend outside the monolayer, they are sensitive to their surroundings. Thus, disorder can cause exciton instability, which is detrimental to device performance and critical for scalability and reproducibility. Here, we adapt a super-resolution fluorescence fluctuation microscopy technique to image localized exciton fluctuations in monolayer semiconductors, allowing us to identify unstable spots in an otherwise continuous monolayer with constant fluorescence. These spots correspond to interfacial disorder measured by atomic force microscopy. We examine how different material interfaces influence the fluctuations by comparing several substrates and provide additional insight into the disorder behind the fluctuations using hyperspectral imaging. We also assess the reduction of disorder upon thermal annealing, evidenced by a decrease in fluctuations. Our results show that fluorescence fluctuation imaging can detect disorder features similar to those of atomic force microscopy and hyperspectral imaging, while being faster and easier to implement. Therefore, it is a promising method for evaluating the quality of monolayer semiconductors, particularly when integrated with nanostructures and heterostructures found in nano-optoelectronic devices.

### [26] [Geometry-Controlled Excitonic Emission Engineering in Monolayer MoS2 Using Plasmonic Hollow Nanocavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07732)
*Abdullah Efe Yildiz,Emre Ozan Polat*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟，利用中空金纳米柱腔体（hollow gold nanocylindrical cavities）调控单层二硫化钼（MoS2）中A和B激子（excitons）的光致发光，实现了高达143.85倍的增强和激子峰相对强度的重新分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在单层二硫化钼中，A和B激子能级仅相隔数十毫电子伏特（meV），这使得光谱调控在基础研究和谷电子学（valleytronic photonics）、纳米光源等技术应用中都至关重要且具有挑战性。

Method: 研究采用时域有限差分法（finite-difference time-domain simulations）结合光致发光速率框架（photoluminescence-rate framework），数值模拟了MoS2与垂直取向的中空金纳米柱腔体通过介电间隔层（dielectric spacer）耦合的系统。通过调节腔体纵横比（aspect ratio）使局域表面等离子体共振（localized surface plasmon resonance）与特定激子跃迁对齐，并利用间隔层厚度和折射率调控近场限制和光学态密度（local density of optical states）。

Result: 在优化条件下，激发速率（excitation rates）增强了4.34倍，辐射衰变（radiative decay）增强超过40倍，导致A和B激子的光致发光（photoluminescence）分别增强了143.85倍和87.27倍。腔体还重新分配了激子峰的相对强度，与裸MoS2相比，归一化激子峰比（normalized exciton peak ratios）可达2.4。

Conclusion: 结果表明，中空等离子体纳米腔（hollow plasmonic nanocavities）是一种几何结构可调的（geometry-tunable）平台，可用于控制原子级薄半导体中的激子发射和电荷生成（charge generation）。

Abstract: Spectral control of closely spaced excitonic transitions is essential for valleytronic photonics, nanoscale light sources, and wavelength-encoded sensing. In monolayer molybdenum disulfide (MoS2), the A and B excitons are separated by only tens of meV, making spectral engineering both fundamentally important and technologically challenging. Here, we numerically investigate plasmon-enhanced excitonic emission in MoS2 coupled to vertically oriented hollow gold nanocylindrical cavities separated by a dielectric spacer. Finite-difference time-domain simulations combined with a photoluminescence-rate framework allow independent evaluation of excitation enhancement, radiative decay modification, non-radiative quenching, and excitonic charge generation. By tuning the cavity aspect ratio, the localized surface plasmon resonance is aligned with either the A or B excitonic transition, while spacer thickness and refractive index regulate near-field confinement and the local density of optical states. Under optimized conditions, excitation rates reach 4.34-fold enhancement while radiative decay exceeds 40-fold, producing photoluminescence increases of 143.85 and 87.27 times for the A and B excitons. The cavity also redistributes the relative intensities of the excitonic peaks, yielding normalized exciton peak ratios up to 2.4 compared to bare MoS2. These results establish hollow plasmonic nanocavities as a geometry-tunable platform for controlling excitonic emission and charge generation in atomically thin semiconductors.

</details>


### [27] [Resonances in light scattering from nonequilibrium dipoles pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07735)
*Vanik E. Mkrtchian,Armen E. Allahverdyan,Mikayel Khanbekyan*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了两个点状电偶极子的光散射特性，发现当每个偶极子的极化率违反光学定理（optical theorem）时，系统在频率和偶极间距的函数上会表现出精确共振。这种共振在非平衡条件下（如活性偶极子）可以无限大，而在平衡域中虽有限但能产生显著放大效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索点状电偶极子对的光散射行为，特别是当极化率违反光学定理时系统的共振特性。这有助于理解非平衡条件下光与物质相互作用的基本物理机制。

Method: 采用经典光学方法，研究单色入射场下点状偶极子的响应。分析包括两个电偶极子以及一个电偶极子与一个磁偶极子的组合，考察频率和偶极间距对散射的影响。

Result: 当极化率违反光学定理时，系统在远场和近场均出现精确共振，这些共振在非平衡条件下可以无限大。在平衡域中，共振虽有限但能显著放大散射强度，例如金属纳米粒子对的等离子体共振可放大约100倍。研究还揭示了弱磁响应可通过共振放大，并讨论了双偶极子散射中的反共振（暗态）效应。

Conclusion: 违反光学定理的极化率能导致精确共振，这些共振在非平衡条件下可无限大，而在平衡域中虽有限但能显著增强散射。全局散射最大化仍需违反光学定理，且共振可放大单个偶极子的弱磁响应，同时存在反共振效应。

Abstract: We consider the light scattering from a pair of point-like electrical dipoles. Whenever the polarizability of each dipole violates the optical theorem, the response of the pair (both in far-field and near-field) exhibits exact resonances as a function of the frequency and the inter-dipole distance. This polarizability is consistent with causality and the crossing condition (i.e., a real field generates a real response). Hence, the emergence of the resonances requires nonequilibrium conditions, e.g., corresponding to active dipoles. Within our approach (classical optics, monochromatic incident field, point-like dipoles), the exact resonances can be infinite. The resonances also appear in the equilibrium domain, where the optical theorem is valid. In that domain, they are finite, but can produce large amplification factors; e.g., for a pair of metallic nanoparticles under Drude's model, the single-particle plasmonic resonance can be amplified $\sim 10^{2}$ times. But the global maximization of the scattering can still be achieved by violating the optical theorem. Our results for one electric and one magnetic dipole show how resonances can amplify a weak magnetic response of a single dipole to the incident field. We also discuss an anti-resonance (dark-state) effect present in the two-dipole scattering.

</details>


### [28] [Large differential attosecond delays in solid state photoemission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08203)
*Andreas Gebauer,Walter Enns,Sergej Neb,Tillmann Schabbehard,Luis Maschmann,Stefan Muff,J. Hugo Dil,Ulrich Heinzmann,Stephan Fritzsche,Ricardo Diez Muiño,Pedro M. Echenique,Nikolay M. Kabachnik,Eugene E. Krasovskii,Walter Pfeiffer*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究报道了利用阿秒时间分辨光电子能谱测量自旋轨道劈裂态之间的微分阿秒延迟，揭示了表面多重散射对光电子发射动力学的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统相对光电子发射延迟测量中，终态能量差异较大，掩盖了复杂的精细结构并阻碍了测量结果的解释。研究旨在通过测量能量相近的自旋轨道劈裂态之间的微分阿秒延迟，揭示光电子发射动力学的精细特征。

Method: 采用微分阿秒延迟（differential attosecond delays, τ_DAD）测量方法，即测量能量相近的自旋轨道劈裂态之间的相对光电子发射延迟。研究对象为Bi₂Te₃和Bi₂Se₃中Bi 5d、Te 4d和Se 3d芯能级的光电子发射。

Result: 实验观测到30-100阿秒量级的微分阿秒延迟，这些延迟既不能归因于原子内延迟，也不能归因于弹道输运和后续发射过程。基于一步光电子发射理论的计算表明，光电子发射延迟在自旋轨道劈裂的能量尺度上强烈变化，与实验观测定量吻合。

Conclusion: 微分阿秒延迟的强烈变化源于表面的多重散射，导致终态同时包含衰减波和传播布洛赫波。这两种成分的相对振幅强烈变化，从而影响光电子发射的时间特性，因为衰减波和传播成分本质上具有不同的动力学行为。

Abstract: Time-resolved photoelectron spectroscopy provides access to the electronic structure and non-equilibrium electron dynamics in matter. At solid surfaces photoemission dynamics can be investigated on its natural time scale by measuring attosecond time delays of emitted electrons. Photoelectrons with final state energies of several tens of eV need tens to hundreds of attoseconds to be released into the vacuum. Competing effects determine the emission dynamics and, hence, the full picture of the process is still under debate. The rather large energy differences between the final states probed in commonly reported relative photoemission delays obscure their complex fine structure and hinders the interpretation of the measurements. Here we report differential attosecond delays $τ_{\mathrm{DAD}}$, i.e., relative photoemission delays for energetically close-lying spin-orbit split states. Differential attosecond delays on the order of 30 to 100 as for Bi 5d, Te 4d, and Se 3d core level photoemission from Bi$_2$Te$_3$ and Bi$_2$Se$_3$ can neither be attributed to intra-atomic delays, nor to ballistic transport and subsequent emission. Instead, calculations based on the one-step photoemission theory reveal that photoemission delays vary strongly on the energy scale of the spin-orbit splitting and quantitatively match experimental observations. This strong variation arises from multiple scattering at the surface leading to final states that involve both evanescent and propagating Bloch waves. Their relative amplitudes vary strongly affecting thereby the timing of the photoemission event since evanescent and propagating components exhibit inherently different dynamics.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Using reinforcement learning (RL), the microswimmer learns to adapt its aspect ratio based on its orientation and local velocity-gradient signals. The learned strategies outperform fixed-shape and short-time-optimal baselines across different flow regimes and remain effective when transferred from stochastic flows to fully resolved turbulence. Guided by the learned policies, we propose a minimal analytical model that captures the essential navigation mechanisms and reproduces the performance across flow regimes. Abstract: One of the crucial aspects of current research in quantum information science is the identification and control of loss mechanisms in superconducting circuits. Although microwave measurements directly quantify device performance, additional techniques that probe quasiparticle excitations in superconducting films are needed to understand the microscopic mechanisms underlying dissipation and decoherence. Here, we present results from quasiparticle spectroscopy of Ta/sapphire films by measuring the Meissner-state magnetic susceptibility using a precision frequency-domain resonator specifically designed for thin films. We find direct evidence for additional low-energy excitations in samples with lower internal quality factors. These excitations are consistent with deep subgap states due to two-level systems, Yu-Shiba-Rusinov states near the gap edge, and perhaps other pair-breaking mechanisms. The developed non-destructive frequency-domain quasiparticle spectroscopy is a valuable addition to the quantum materials toolbox.

*Logan E. Smith,Paolo Settembri,Alessio Cucciari,Lilia Boeri,Gianni Profeta,Sharon Hammes-Schiffer*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核量子效应对于正确描述高压富氢材料至关重要，超导氢化物和冰是典型例子，需要同时考虑晶格非谐性和核量子效应才能准确预测实验观测的结构和相变压力。

Method: 采用核-电子轨道密度泛函理论（nuclear-electronic orbital density functional theory, NEO-DFT）方法，将特定原子核与电子在相同量子力学水平上处理，并与更昂贵的随机自洽谐振近似（stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation, SSCHA）方法进行基准测试。

Result: NEO-DFT准确预测了H₃S和D₃S的氢键对称化压力，与SSCHA方法结果一致；在宽压力范围内正确预测了LaH₁₀的对称Fm$\bar{3}$m结构；同时预测的H₂O和D₂O从冰VIII到冰X的相变压力与实验测量相符。

Conclusion: NEO方法的准确性、计算效率和广泛适用性为大规模研究这类系统打开了大门，为高压富氢材料的核量子效应描述提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Nuclear quantum effects are essential for correctly describing hydrogen-rich materials at high pressures. Superconducting hydrides and ice are prime examples of such systems, requiring the inclusion of lattice anharmonicity and nuclear quantum effects to correctly predict and describe the structures and phase transition pressures observed experimentally. Herein, we show that the nuclear-electronic orbital density functional theory (NEO-DFT) method, which treats specified nuclei quantum mechanically on the same level as the electrons, is capable of accurately describing nuclear quantum effects in superconducting hydrides and ice. NEO-DFT predicts the hydrogen-bond symmetrization pressure in H$_3$S and D$_3$S, benchmarking against the more expensive stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation (SSCHA) method, and predicts the correct symmetric Fm$\bar{3}$m structure for LaH$_{10}$ at a wide range of pressures. NEO-DFT also predicts the ice VIII to ice X phase transition pressures for H$_2$O and D$_2$O in agreement with experimental measurements. The accuracy, computational efficiency, and broad applicability of the NEO method opens the door for expanded large-scale studies into these types of systems.

### [34] [Interband pairing in two-band superconductors with spin-orbit and Zeeman couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07342)
*Shohei O. Shingu,Jun Goryo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Interband pairing in multiband superconductors is often neglected because of its higher energetic cost compared with intraband pairing. Using hexagonal tight-binding models with locally broken inversion symmetry, we find a Zeeman-driven transition between a conventional intraband s-wave state and an interband-dominated superconducting Mixing state. The resulting quasiparticle spectrum is intrinsically gapless, leading to anomalous thermodynamic behavior, including a T-linear specific heat at low temperatures, reflecting a finite zero-energy density of states.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要开发一种统一且强大的探测方法来研究具有拉什巴自旋轨道耦合（Rashba SOC）的平面约瑟夫森结（planar Josephson junctions）的微观和拓扑特性，特别是在面内磁场作用下的行为。

Method: 通过理论分析磁电流相位关系（magneto-CPR），研究超电流的完整相位和塞曼场依赖性，并利用该关系重构无相位偏置时系统自由能最小的基态相位。

Result: 磁电流相位关系测量可重构显示0-π类转变的基态相位，其相位跳变幅度提供拉什巴自旋轨道耦合的定量信息；同时可提取第二混合自旋磁化率作为能隙闭合的敏感诊断，并构建基于相对拓扑能隙的超导拓扑相图。

Conclusion: 磁电流相位关系测量被确立为一种多功能光谱工具，可用于提取关键系统参数，并为平面约瑟夫森结中的拓扑超导相提供证据，同时还能表征约瑟夫森二极管效应及其与塞曼场、拉什巴自旋轨道耦合和结透明度的关系。

Abstract: We present a theoretical study of proximitized planar Josephson junctions (JJs) with Rashba spin-orbit coupling (SOC) subject to an in-plane magnetic field and demonstrate that the magneto-current-phase relation (magneto-CPR) provides a powerful and unified probe of their microscopic and topological properties. By analyzing the full phase and Zeeman-field dependence of the supercurrent, we show that magneto-CPR measurements allow one to reconstruct the ground-state phase that minimizes the system's free energy in the absence of phase bias. This reconstructed phase generally displays 0-pi-like transitions as a function of the Zeeman energy, and we demonstrate that the magnitudes of the associated phase jumps provide quantitative information about the Rashba SOC. We further show that the mixed phase-field response encoded in the magneto-CPR enables the extraction of the second mixed spin susceptibility, which serves as a sensitive diagnostic of gap closings and can be used to construct a superconducting topological phase diagram in terms of the relative topological gap. In addition, the magneto-CPR yields the field dependence of the forward and reverse critical currents, allowing one to characterize the Josephson diode effect and its connection to the Zeeman field, Rashba SOC, and junction transparency. Our results establish magneto-CPR measurements as a versatile spectroscopic tool that can be used to extract key system parameters and provide evidence of topological superconducting phases in planar JJs.

</details>


### [36] [Enhancement of metallicity by Na doping in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7+δ}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08168)
*Yingying Gao,Wei Zhou,W. H. Guo,Chunqiang Xu,H. F. Chen,Z. D. Han,Xiaofeng Xu,Yinzhong Wu,Bin Qian*

TL;DR: 该研究系统探索了钠（Na）掺杂对Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇₊δ的结构与物性影响，发现Na掺杂在x≥0.075时诱导从'Amam'相到'Bmab'相的结构转变，同时显著增强金属性并抑制密度波（DW）转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高压下双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇中高温超导（high-Tc superconductivity）的发现为探索新型非常规超导体提供了新平台。后续化学替代研究旨在稳定常压超导性或降低所需压力阈值，本研究通过钠掺杂探索元素替代和载流子掺杂对层状镍酸盐竞争电子相的影响。

Method: 研究采用钠（Na⁺）替代La³⁺的A位掺杂策略，系统合成不同掺杂浓度的多晶样品。通过X射线衍射（XRD）、热重分析（TGA）等手段表征结构变化，并测量热学、磁学和电子输运性质，包括电阻率测量和压力效应研究。

Result: Na掺杂在x≥0.075时诱导从'327'Amam相到'4310'Bmab相的结构转变，同时引起'327'相晶格逐渐膨胀。电阻率测量显示密度波（DW）转变被轻微抑制，金属性显著增强。施加压力可进一步抑制DW转变，但低温绝缘行为对压力不敏感。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解元素替代和载流子掺杂在调控层状镍酸盐竞争电子相中的作用提供了关键见解，为通过化学掺杂稳定镍酸盐超导性提供了重要实验依据。

Abstract: The observation of high-$T_c$ superconductivity in bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ under high pressure provides a new venue for exploring novel unconventional superconductors and elucidating the mechanism of high-$T_c$ superconductivity. Subsequently, numerous chemical substitution studies have been reported, aiming to stabilize superconductivity at ambient pressure, or significantly reduce the pressure threshold required for its occurrence. Here, we report the comprehensive study on sodium (Na) doping in the Ruddlesden-Popper nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7+δ}$, where Na$^+$ substitutes for La$^{3+}$ at the A-site with varying doping concentrations. The structural, thermal, magnetic, and electronic transport properties of as-synthesized polycrystalline samples were systematically investigated. X-ray diffraction (XRD) analysis reveals that Na doping induces a structural transition from the '327' Amam phase to the '4310' Bmab phase when $x\geq0.075$, which is further corroborated by thermogravimetric analysis (TGA) measurements. Substitution of La$^{3+}$ with Na$^+$ gives rise to a gradual expansion of the '327' phase lattice. Meanwhile, resistivity measurements indicate that the density wave (DW) transition is marginally suppressed and metallicity is significantly enhanced. Upon the application of pressure, DW transition can be further suppressed, whereas the low-$T$ insulating behaviors remain insensitive to pressure. These results offer critical insights into the roles of elemental substitution and charge carrier doping in steering the competing electronic phases in layered nickelates.

### [37] [On the estimating the superconducting volume fraction from the internal magnetic susceptibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08302)
*Aleksandr V. Korolev,Evgeny F. Talantsev*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文对Zhang等人提出的超导相体积分数计算方法提出质疑，指出其核心假设$f = \vert χ_{internal} \vert$存在错误，并通过反例证明该假设在Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀样品中不成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在质疑Zhang等人在高压Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐超导性研究中使用的计算方法。作者发现该研究基于的核心假设——超导相体积分数$f$等于内部磁化率幅值$\vert χ_{internal} \vert$——存在根本性错误。

Method: 作者通过构建反例来反驳现有假设，展示在Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀样品S3中，即使$\vert χ_{internal} \vert = 0.82$，实际超导相体积分数$f$可能小于0.10。该方法直接针对计算方法的核心假设进行证伪。

Result: 研究结果表明，Zhang等人报道的$f = 0.85$计算结果可能严重高估了实际超导相体积分数。反例明确证明了$f = \vert χ_{internal} \vert$这一假设在Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀体系中不成立，从而质疑了原始研究的结论可靠性。

Conclusion: 作者得出结论：$f = \vert χ_{internal} \vert$这一在超导领域广泛使用的假设需要重新评估。鉴于该假设在超导研究中的普遍应用，作者呼吁整个超导领域重新审视这一基本假设的有效性。

Abstract: Zhang et al.$^1$ reported zero-field cooled (ZFC) and field cooled (FC) data measured in a highly compressed $Pr_4Ni_3O_{10}$ single crystal. These measurements provide unambiguous confirmation of bulk superconductivity in pressurized Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates. Zhang et al.$^1$ applied an equation (described in Refs.$^{2,3}$) to recalculate ZFC data measured in a $Pr_4Ni_3O_{10}$ (sample S3) in volume fraction $f$ of the superconducting phase in the sample. In result$^1$, $f = 0.85$ was reported for sample S3 at pressure P = 40.2 GPa. The key postulate of the methodology for the calculation of $f$ (see also works$^{4-6}$) is that $f$ is equal to the amplitude of the internal magnetic susceptibility $\vert χ_{internal} \vert $, or $ f = \vert χ_{internal} \vert $. Here we argue that this postulate is incorrect and present counterexample where the $Pr_4Ni_3O_{10}$ sample S3 can exhibit $f < 0.10$ and $\vert χ_{internal} \vert = 0.82 $. In the result, we addressed recent Replies$^{2,3}$ on our Comments$^{7,8}$. Considering that the postulate $ f = \vert χ_{internal} \vert $ is widely used in superconductivity, we extend our request to reconsider the validity of this postulate in the entire field of superconductivity.

</details>


### [38] [Magnetic landscape of NbTiN superconducting resonators under radio-frequency excitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08500)
*J. Baumgarten,N. Lejeune,L. Nulens,I. P. C. Cools,J. Van de Vondel,A. V. Silhanek*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过法拉第旋转成像直接可视化射频激发下的磁通量渗透，揭示了磁通雪崩与射频传输特性的关联，并识别了最有害事件的位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面超导谐振器（planar superconducting resonators）的性能常因磁通量渗透而受损，特别是在低温下热磁不稳定性会引发磁通雪崩（magnetic flux avalanches）。一个重要未解问题是射频激发本身是否会刺激超导薄膜中磁通雪崩的成核和传播，现有文献对此尚无定论。

Method: 采用前所未有的法拉第旋转成像（Faraday rotation imaging）直接可视化技术，在同步射频激发下观察磁通量渗透。同时通过电磁模拟（electromagnetic simulations）验证，其中局部动力学电感（kinetic inductance）的变化模拟了磁通雪崩。

Result: 在坎贝尔线性区（Campbell regime）内，雪崩活动对射频强度表现出弱依赖性，但磁通爆发（magnetic flux bursts）明显影响器件的射频传输特性。能够明确地将特定雪崩事件与共振频率跳跃相关联，从而识别最有害事件的位置并理解频率上移和下降的不同起源。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解超导谐振器的磁弹性（magnetic resilience）提供了新见解，有助于提高其效率和稳定性。同时证实了磁光成像（MOI）技术的侵入性特征。

Abstract: Planar superconducting resonators are essential components in quantum circuits and highly sensitive sensors. However, their performance is often compromised by magnetic flux penetration, as the interaction of flux quanta and the induced radio-frequency (RF) currents in the superconducting thin film leads to significant energy dissipation. At low operating temperatures, this issue is aggravated as thermomagnetic instabilities can trigger the sudden propagation of magnetic flux avalanches. An important open question is whether the RF excitation itself stimulates the nucleation and propagation of magnetic flux avalanches in the superconducting thin film. The literature remains inconclusive on this point, partly due to the lack of compelling evidence for this phenomenon. In this work, we address this issue by unprecedented direct visualization of magnetic flux penetration through Faraday rotation imaging under simultaneous RF excitation. We demonstrate that the avalanche activity exhibits a weak dependence on the RF intensity for RF excitations within the linear Campbell regime. However, magnetic flux bursts clearly influence the RF transmission properties of the device. Furthermore, it is possible to unambiguously associate a particular avalanche event with a jump in resonance frequency. This enables us to identify the loci of most deleterious events and understand the distinct origins of upward and downward frequency shifts. These observations are supported by electromagnetic simulations in which local changes of the kinetic inductance mimic flux avalanches and confirm the invasive character of the MOI technique. The insights gained from this study aim to contribute to the broader understanding of the magnetic resilience of superconducting resonators, with the goal of improving their efficiency and stability.

</details>


### [39] [Discovery of intertwined pair density and charge density wave orders in UTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08688)
*Zhen Zhu,Yudi Huang,Julian May-Mann,Kaiming Liu,Zheyu Wu,Shanta R. Saha,Johnpierre Paglione,Alexander G. Eaton,Andrej Cabala,Michal Vališka,Eduardo Fradkin,Vidya Madhavan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究利用配备矢量磁场的扫描隧道显微镜，在强关联自旋三重态超导体UTe2中系统研究了不同电荷密度波（CDW）序的演化与关联，揭示了由三重态对密度波（PDW）驱动的复合CDW序结构及其与超导性的耦合机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UTe2作为强关联自旋三重态超导体，展现出磁场敏感的电荷密度波相，是研究交织电子序的理想平台。核心挑战在于确定观察到的电荷调制是否源于三重态对密度波序，以及三重态超导性的各向异性磁场响应如何在CDW响应中体现。

Method: 研究采用配备矢量磁场的扫描隧道显微镜，系统研究了不同CDW序的演化和相互关系。该方法能够分辨具有不同温度和磁场依赖性的非色散调制，并分析其与超导转变温度Tc和临界磁场Hc2的关联。

Result: 除了先前识别的非公度CDW峰（qi=1,2,3）外，研究还分辨出具有不同温度和磁场依赖性的额外非色散调制（pi=1,2,3和h1,2）。pi CDW峰在Tc附近消失，而qi峰在远高于Tc时仍存在，但以各向异性方式被磁场逐渐抑制。qi峰的临界磁场反映了Hc2的方向层次结构，表明在体相Tc以上存在PDW。

Conclusion: 这些发现确立了UTe2作为一个稀有平台，其中母体PDW和衍生序都能被直接分辨，从而能够同时研究PDW物理的基本表现和涌现表现。研究支持朗道自由能图像，其中波矢为pi的PDW在体相Tc以上形成，导致波矢为qi的复合CDW序，而在Tc以下，PDW与均匀超导性的耦合产生了pi CDW。

Abstract: The strongly correlated spin-triplet superconductor UTe2 hosts an unusual landscape of magnetic-field-sensitive charge density wave (CDW) phases, positioning it as a compelling system for studying intertwined electronic orders. A central challenge is determining whether the observed charge modulations arise from a triplet pair density wave (PDW) order and, if so, how the anisotropic magnetic field response of triplet superconductivity is manifested in the CDW response. Here, using a scanning tunneling microscope equipped with a vector magnetic field, we systematically investigate the evolution and interrelation of distinct CDW orders. Complementing the previously identified incommensurate CDW peaks (qi=1,2,3), we resolve an additional set of nondispersive modulations (pi=1,2,3 and h1,2) with distinct temperature and magnetic field dependencies. The pi CDW peaks vanish near Tc, while the qi peaks survive well above Tc but are progressively suppressed by magnetic field in an anisotropic manner. The critical fields of the qi peaks mirror the directional hierarchy of Hc2, which suggests a PDW is present above the bulk Tc. This is consistent with a Landau free-energy picture where PDWs with wavevectors pi form above the bulk Tc, leading to composite CDW orders with wavevector qi. Below Tc, the coupling of PDWs and uniform superconductivity leads to the pi CDWs. Together, these findings establish UTe2 as a rare platform where both the parent PDW and descendant orders are directly resolved, enabling access to both the fundamental and emergent manifestations of PDW physics.

### [40] [A Note on the Peter-Weyl Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07105)
*Y. Bavuma,E. Stevenson,F. G. Russo*

Method: 方法基于紧群表示论中的经典概念，特别是利用代表性函数（representative functions）的局部性质。研究主要处理具有大型非平凡紧开子群的局部紧群上的函数。

Result: 论文证明了这类函数可以通过其他函数来逼近，这些逼近函数在局部上与经典的代表性函数完全相同。这构成了Peter-Weyl定理的一个新推广。

Conclusion: 研究成功地将Peter-Weyl定理推广到更广泛的群类，为具有大型非平凡紧开子群的局部紧群上的函数逼近提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We introduce some classical concepts in the representation theory of compact groups, in order to use them for a new generalization of the Peter-Weyl Theorem. We mostly deal with functions on locally compact groups possessing large nontrivial compact open subgroups: in fact, we show that these functions can be approximated via others which are locally identical to the well known representative functions.

Here, we solve problem B for superstrings in superdimension $(1\vert 1)$ -- superizations of the result of arXiv:2404.18222. Open problems are offered.

### [42] [Force Dipole Interactions in Membranes with Odd Viscosity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07830)
*Sneha Krishnan,Udaya Maurya,Rickmoy Samanta*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个流体力学框架，用于研究嵌入在由浅粘性亚相支撑的可压缩流体膜中的力偶极子（force dipoles）的相互作用和集体动力学。该框架考虑了剪切、膨胀和奇（霍尔）粘度，揭示了多个不同的动力学机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究可压缩流体膜中力偶极子的相互作用和集体动力学需要建立一个包含剪切、膨胀和奇粘度（odd viscosity）效应的流体力学框架。现有模型通常局限于不可压缩膜或具有宇称对称性的可压缩膜，缺乏对奇粘度产生的非对称响应的描述。

Method: 从包含剪切、膨胀和奇（霍尔）粘度的广义二维斯托克斯方程（generalized two-dimensional Stokes equations）出发，使用汉克尔变换（Hankel transforms）推导出精确的实空间格林张量（real-space Green tensor）。该张量由与剪切、压缩和奇粘性模式相关的三个流体力学屏蔽尺度（hydrodynamic screening scales）表征。

Result: 推导出的格林张量平滑地简化为不可压缩膜和可压缩宇称对称膜的标准极限情况，同时捕捉了奇粘度产生的非对称响应。通过该张量获得了力偶极子产生的速度场和涡度场，并建立了控制相互作用的偶极子的动力学系统。

Conclusion: 分析揭示了几个不同的动力学机制，并识别了能够分离出奇粘度对偶极子相互作用的非对称贡献的可观测量，包括横向漂移（transverse drift）和手性相对运动（chiral relative motion）。该框架为研究可压缩膜中力偶极子的集体行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We develop a hydrodynamic framework for the interactions and collective dynamics of force dipoles embedded in a compressible fluid membrane supported by a shallow viscous subphase. Starting from the generalized two-dimensional Stokes equations with shear, dilatational, and odd (Hall) viscosities, we derive an exact real-space Green tensor using Hankel transforms. The resulting tensor is characterized by three hydrodynamic screening scales associated with shear, compressional, and odd-viscous modes, and smoothly reduces to the standard limiting cases of incompressible membranes and compressible parity-symmetric membranes, while also capturing the chiral response generated by odd viscosity. Using this Green tensor we obtain the velocity and vorticity fields generated by a force dipole and formulate the dynamical system governing interacting dipoles. The analysis reveals several distinct dynamical regimes and identifies observables that isolate the antisymmetric odd-viscous contribution to dipole interactions, including transverse drift and chiral relative motion.

</details>


### [43] [Nematic Bubbles and the Breaking of Spherical Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07082)
*Gaetano Napoli,Silvia Paparini*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个连续介质模型，将二维Landau-de Gennes序张量（描述面内向列相有序）与质量守恒的可变形球壳力学相耦合，研究了向列相有序如何自发打破球对称性并产生不同平衡形态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可变形闭合表面上向列相有序（nematic order）的出现对活性生物物质的形态发生（morphogenesis）至关重要，如水螅再生过程。研究旨在理解体轴形成和缺陷介导的形态发生机制。

Method: 建立连续介质模型，耦合二维Landau-de Gennes序张量与质量守恒的可变形球壳力学。通过模拟温度降低驱动的各向同性-向列相相变（isotropic-to-nematic phase transition），进行线性和弱非线性分岔分析（bifurcation analysis）。

Result: 向列相有序自发打破球对称性，产生由壳层可变形性（deformability）支配的不同平衡形态。轴对称构型通过不连续分岔产生两极具有两个+1缺陷的全球稳定长球体（prolate shape）和亚稳态扁球体（oblate shape）。非轴对称构型通过连续分岔产生四个+1/2缺陷呈正方形排列。整数缺陷与局部质量重分布强耦合，表现为壳层变薄或增厚，而半整数缺陷不诱导此类局部变形。

Conclusion: 壳层柔软度（softness）驱动相变的一级特征，而在无限刚度极限下所有分岔变为连续。这些发现为理解生物囊泡中体轴形成和缺陷介导的形态发生提供了纯力学框架。

Abstract: The emergence of nematic order on deformable closed surfaces plays a pivotal role in the morphogenesis of active biological matter, such as the regeneration of Hydra. In this work, we present a continuum model that couples the two-dimensional Landau-de Gennes order tensor, describing in-plane nematic ordering, with the mechanics of a mass-conserving, deformable spherical shell. By investigating the isotropic-to-nematic phase transition driven by a reduction in temperature, mimicking the natural induction of nematic order in actomyosin fibres, we perform both linear and weakly non-linear bifurcation analyses. The onset of nematic ordering spontaneously breaks spherical symmetry, yielding distinct equilibrium morphologies governed by the shell's deformability. Axisymmetric configurations, featuring two +1 defects at the poles, emerge via a discontinuous bifurcation, resulting in a globally stable prolate shape, alongside a metastable oblate shape. Non-axisymmetric configurations, featuring four +1/2 defects arranged in a square, arise via a continuous bifurcation. Shell softness drives the first-order character of the transition, while in the limit of infinite stiffness all bifurcations become continuous. Integer defects strongly couple with local mass redistribution, manifesting as shell thinning or thickening, whilst half-integer defects induce no such local deformation. These findings provide a purely mechanical framework for understanding body-axis formation and defect-mediated morphogenesis in biological vesicles.

</details>


### [44] [Realizing microrheological response of configurable viscoelastic media with a dynamic optical trap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07100)
*Sanatan Halder,Manas Khan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用动态光镊实现可配置粘弹性介质的方法，能够系统且独立地调控介质特性，为研究单重和多重弛豫粘弹性流体的微流变响应提供了实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究局部粘弹性（viscoelastic, VE）环境对嵌入微球运动的影响面临挑战，主要因为粘弹性参数之间存在强耦合关系且依赖于实验条件（如温度）。现有方法难以实现粘弹性特性的系统独立调控。

Method: 采用动态光镊（dynamic optical trap）技术，通过调控光阱强度和扩散系数分别调节弹性响应和低频粘度，实现可配置粘弹性介质。对于双重弛豫介质，通过在光阱轨迹中引入适当相关噪声来扩展该方法。

Result: 该方法成功模拟了单重弛豫粘弹性流体（Jeffreys或Maxwell-Voigt流体）的线性微流变响应，并通过与真实流体实验、理论预测和模拟结果对比验证了其有效性。方案可进一步扩展至双重弛豫粘弹性介质。

Abstract: The local viscoelastic (VE) environment governs the motion of an embedded microsphere and consequently, pertinent dynamical phenomena. However, studying such phenomena with varying VE properties remains challenging for various reasons, including the strong coupling among the VE parameters and their dependence on experimental conditions, such as temperature. Here, we demonstrate the experimental realization of configurable VE media with broad variations, wherein the VE properties can be systematically and independently tuned, employing a dynamic optical trap. Specifically, the dynamics of a particle in a slowly diffusing optical trap provides the linear microrheological response of single-relaxation VE fluids, namely, Jeffreys or Maxwell-Voigt (MV) fluids, where the trap strength and its diffusion coefficient regulate the elastic response and the low-frequency viscosity, respectively. We validate this approach by comparing the experimentally observed dynamics of the trapped bead with those of a probe particle in real single-relaxation complex fluids, analytical predictions, and simulation results following harmonically bound Brownian particle with long-time diffusion model describing MV fluids. We extend the applicability of this scheme for realizing the microrheological response of double-relaxation VE media by incorporating appropriately correlated noise in the trap trajectory, signifying its validity for any linear VE media with multiple relaxations. Our scheme can be further extended to realize probe particle dynamics in an active VE environment, e.g., an entangled network of active polymers, by translating the trap along an active Brownian trajectory. Therefore, our scheme enables systematic microrheological studies in VE regimes that are otherwise challenging to realize or not readily accessible with real materials.

Abstract: We extend the statistical field-theoretical framework of rough surface contact mechanics to characterize the interfacial gap between an elastic half-space and a randomly rough surface incorporating exponential repulsion. Solving this equation with appropriate initial and boundary conditions yields the gap distribution under varying external pressures.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究扩展经典成核理论，通过离散和连续描述相结合的方式，将衣壳边缘的热涨落纳入模型。该方法允许部分形成的衣壳边缘发生小幅度几何波动，从而分析这些涨落产生的熵贡献。

Result: 研究表明边缘涨落通过熵贡献重整化有效线张力，其效应取决于亚基-亚基结合自由能、温度和涨落幅度。当结合自由能低于阈值时，涨落通常降低成核势垒；而在足够强的结合条件下，涨落反而通过闭合边缘的有限尺寸熵罚分稳定不完全衣壳，从而提高势垒。

Abstract: Most spherical viruses exhibit icosahedral symmetry, yet the growth of viral shells remains poorly understood due to the short lifetimes and broad size distribution of assembly intermediates. Classical nucleation theory has been widely applied to describe this process, but it treats the boundary of a growing shell as rigid and structureless. Here, we extend classical nucleation theory by incorporating thermal fluctuations of the capsid rim using both discrete and continuum descriptions. Allowing the rim of a partially formed capsid to undergo small geometric undulations, we show that these fluctuations generate an entropic contribution that renormalizes the effective line tension. As a result, rim fluctuations can either promote or hinder capsid closure, depending on the subunit-subunit binding free energy, temperature, and fluctuation amplitude. We find that fluctuations generally lower the nucleation barrier when the binding free energy is below a threshold value, while for sufficiently strong binding, they can instead raise the barrier by stabilizing incomplete capsids through a finite-size entropy penalty associated with rim closure. By moving beyond the idealized capillarity approximation, our results provide a controlled extension of classical nucleation theory that clarifies how boundary fluctuations influence capsid nucleation and growth.

In three dimensions the ring polymer may also be knotted, or linked, and have its conformational degrees of freedom constrained by its topology. In a lattice model of confined knotted ring polymers there are indications that the thermodynamic properties of the ring polymer (for example, the osmotic pressure \cite{GJvR18,JvR19}) is a function of its topology. In this paper we explore a lattice knot model of a confined ring polymer as a function of its chemical potential. ### [51] [Structural aging of a cohesive and amorphous granular solid under cyclic loading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07852)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对漂浮在气-油界面的颗粒筏施加小应变幅度的单轴循环加载（uniaxial cyclic loading），观察其老化过程。随后对老化后的颗粒筏进行准静态拉伸或压缩测试（quasi-static tension or compression tests）直至破坏，并与未老化的颗粒筏进行对比。

Conclusion: 循环加载通过诱导颗粒筏的结构老化，显著改变其力学性能。这种老化过程涉及空隙形态演化和颗粒重排，最终导致材料强度增加但延展性降低，为理解颗粒材料的循环加载效应提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate how cyclic loading evolves the structure and deformation behaviors of a granular raft composed of particles floating at an air-oil interface. The raft has a disordered particle packing structure, and is cohesive due to capillary interactions between particles. Under uniaxial cyclic loading with a small strain amplitude, the raft's packing structure experiences an aging process characterized by logarithmically increasing packing fraction and decreasing structural heterogeneity. The observed structural change is due to particle dynamics that are organized around morphologically evolving voids in the raft. The raft is then subjected to quasi-static tension or compression tests until failure. In comparison with non-aged rafts, the rafts that experienced cyclic loading show a higher strength, higher stiffness, and lower ductility, along with qualitatively different features, such as a stress overshoot in the loading curve.

*Joscha Mecke,Klaus Kroy*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过非平衡分子动力学和布朗动力学模拟，展示了活性聚合物中多重有效（"活性"）温度的出现。利用广义朗之万方程识别谱噪声温度，并通过可变刚度谐波阱作为光谱装置选择性扫描这些有效温度，从而解析尺度依赖的活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测跨尺度的空间异质性活性是活性物质研究的主要挑战。不同长度尺度的能量注入会导致模式耦合、模式间能量转移和熵产生，需要新的方法来表征这种复杂行为。

Method: 采用非平衡分子动力学（nonequilibrium molecular-dynamics）和布朗动力学（Brownian-dynamics）模拟活性聚合物。通过标记单体的广义朗之万方程（generalised Langevin equation）识别谱噪声温度，并使用可变刚度谐波阱作为最小侵入式光谱装置。

Result: 研究发现活性聚合物中出现了多重有效（"活性"）温度。这些谱噪声温度与底层活性景观相关，且谐波阱能够选择性扫描不同的有效温度，从而解析尺度依赖的活性。

Conclusion: 可变刚度谐波阱可作为原型光谱装置，通过选择性扫描多重有效温度来解析活性物质的尺度依赖活性，为解决活性物质空间异质性表征提供了新方法。

Abstract: Probing the spatially heterogeneous activity across scales is a major challenge in living matter. Energy injection at diverse length scales leads to mode coupling, inter-modal energy transfer, and entropy production. We demonstrate the emergence of multiple effective (``active'') temperatures in nonequilibrium molecular- and Brownian-dynamics simulations of an active polymer. Via a generalised Langevin equation for a labelled monomer we identify spectral noise temperatures and their relation to the underlying activity landscape. A harmonic trap of variable stiffness can serve as a minimally invasive prototypical spectroscopic device to selectively scan through the emergent effective temperatures and thereby resolve the scale-dependent activity.

</details>


### [53] [A thermodynamic metric quantitatively predicts disordered protein partitioning and multicomponent phase behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08300)
*Zhuang Liu,Beijia Yuan,Mihir Rao,Gautam Reddy,William M. Jacobs*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个热力学模型，能够定量预测内在无序区域（IDRs）在复杂混合物中的相行为，该模型学习IDR序列的低维、上下文无关表示，形成混合物表示并产生上下文依赖的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管内在无序区域（intrinsically disordered regions, IDRs）强烈影响生物分子凝聚体（biomolecular condensates）的组成，但能够预测和解释其在复杂混合物中相行为的定量框架仍然缺乏。需要建立能够处理任意IDR组合的预测模型。

Method: 引入一个热力学模型，学习IDR序列的低维、上下文无关表示（low-dimensional, context-independent representations），这些表示组合形成混合物表示并产生上下文依赖的相互作用（context-dependent interactions）。该模型定义了热力学度量空间（thermodynamic metric space），其中IDR之间的距离直接对应其热力学性质的差异。

Result: 模型能够定量预测多组分相图（multicomponent phase diagrams），与分子模拟结果一致，且无需在自由能或相共存数据上进行训练。度量空间提供了IDR分配、多组分凝聚和上下文依赖突变效应的几何直观预测。系统分析揭示了氨基酸组成和序列模式如何共同决定混合物热力学。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个统一且可解释的框架，用于预测和理解IDR及其他序列依赖性生物分子复杂混合物的行为，解决了IDR生物物理学中的多个核心问题。

Abstract: Intrinsically disordered regions (IDRs) of proteins mediate sequence-specific interactions underlying diverse cellular processes, including the formation of biomolecular condensates. Although IDRs strongly influence condensate compositions, quantitative frameworks that predict and explain their phase behavior in complex mixtures remain lacking. Here we introduce a thermodynamic model that quantitatively predicts the behavior of arbitrary combinations of IDRs across a wide range of concentrations, with accuracy comparable to state-of-the-art simulations. The model learns low-dimensional, context-independent representations of IDR sequences that combine to form mixture representations, producing context-dependent interactions. These representations define a thermodynamic metric space in which distances between IDRs correspond directly to differences in their thermodynamic properties. We show that the model predicts multicomponent phase diagrams in quantitative agreement with molecular simulations without being trained on free-energy or phase-coexistence data. The metric space provides geometrically intuitive predictions of IDR partitioning, multicomponent condensation, and context-dependent mutational effects, addressing several central problems in IDR biophysics within a single model. Systematic interrogation of the learned representations reveals how amino-acid composition and sequence patterning jointly determine mixture thermodynamics. Together, our results establish a unified and interpretable framework for predicting and understanding the behavior of complex mixtures of IDRs and other sequence-dependent biomolecules.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用胶体探针原子力显微镜（CP-AFM）测量LaCl₃水溶液，通过调整实验条件使其与SFA研究条件相匹配，以在高盐浓度下检测异常屏蔽行为。
