### [55] [Torque Hyperuniformity in Frictional Granular Matter - Theory and Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08363)
*Jin Shang,Jie Zhang,Itamar Procaccia*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究验证了摩擦性非晶固体中应力自相关矩阵由压力和扭矩自相关两个空间各向同性函数决定的理论预测，并确认了扭矩涨落的超均匀性（hyperuniformity）是导致应力自相关呈现弹性格林函数衰减的关键条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核心问题在于摩擦性颗粒集合体（如沙粒或粉末）的应力自相关是否呈现长程各向异性衰减，类似于弹性格林函数行为。理论预测需要实验验证，以检验这些条件在实际摩擦性非晶固体中是否普遍成立。

Method: 研究回顾了二维摩擦性圆盘在等向载荷下的已有结果，并进一步报告了二维圆盘在剪切载荷下以及等向加载的摩擦性椭圆颗粒系统中的实验确认，其中扭矩贡献同时来自法向力和切向力。

Result: 实验确认了理论预测：在二维摩擦性圆盘（剪切载荷）和摩擦性椭圆颗粒（等向载荷）系统中，应力自相关矩阵确实由压力和扭矩自相关两个函数决定，且扭矩涨落呈现超均匀性，导致应力自相关呈现弹性格林函数式的衰减。

Conclusion: 研究证实了摩擦性非晶固体中机械平衡和材料各向同性要求应力自相关矩阵由压力和扭矩自相关决定的理论框架，并提供了扭矩涨落超均匀性的物理解释，预测了结果向d维系统的扩展。

Abstract: A question of some fundamental importance is whether a given assembly of frictional granules (say sand or powder) will exhibit stress autocorrelations with long-range anisotropic decay as determined by the elastic Green's function. In Hamiltonian systems with central forces, mechanical balance and material isotropy demand the stress auto-correlation matrix to be fully determined by the pressure auto-correlation only. If the local pressure fluctuations are normal, it follows that stress autocorrelations decay at long distance like the elastic Green's function. With friction, Hamiltonian symmetry is lost, and one may expect more constraints. Indeed, it was shown recently that for frictional amorphous solids mechanical balance and material isotropy demand the stress auto-correlation matrix to be fully determined by two spatially isotropic functions: the pressure and torque auto-correlations. Elastic-like decay of the stress autocorrelations follows from normal fluctuations of the pressure and from the torque fluctuations being hyperuniform. The theoretical discovery of these conditions required experimental confirmation, to test whether these conditions are generically obeyed in actual frictional amorphous solids. Recently the confirmation was announced for 2-dimensional amorphous assemblies of frictional disks under isotropic load, in which torque is caused by tangential forces only. In this paper we review that case and report confirmation of the theoretical predictions in 2-dimensional systems of disks under shear and in isotropically loaded frictional ellipses, where contributions to torque come also from normal forces. The paper ends with physical explanations of the hyperuniformity of the torque fluctuations and predictions for how the results are expected to extend to d-dimensions.

</details>


### [56] [Modeling the Slow Arrhenius Process (SAP) in Polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08474)
*Valeriy V. Ginzburg,Oleg V. Gendelman,Simone Napolitano,Riccardo Casalini,Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了TS2理论，为玻璃态聚合物中的α弛豫和慢阿伦尼乌斯过程（SAP）提供了统一的理论框架，将SAP解释为粗粒化流体中动态相关团簇的类α过程高温极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶态玻璃形成聚合物中存在多种弛豫过程，其中在α弛豫频率以下观察到的慢阿伦尼乌斯过程（slow Arrhenius process, SAP）虽然温度依赖性符合阿伦尼乌斯行为，但涉及更长的弛豫时间且微观起源尚不明确。

Method: 扩展了两态两时标（two-state, two-timescale, TS2）理论，提出SAP代表粗粒化流体中动态相关团簇（dynamically correlated clusters）的类α过程（α-like process）的高温极限，通过重整化的相互作用能和配位参数来描述。

Result: 该模型无需额外可调参数即可定量复现多种聚合物的α和SAP数据，并解释了观察到的迈耶-内尔德补偿行为（Meyer-Neldel compensation behavior）。理论进一步预测SAP在足够低温下会偏离阿伦尼乌斯行为，转变为类似沃格尔-富尔彻-塔曼-黑塞（Vogel-Fulcher-Tammann-Hesse-like）的动力学。

Conclusion: 该理论为玻璃形成聚合物中团簇尺度弛豫提供了物理透明的解释，建立了α弛豫和SAP的统一描述框架，揭示了SAP作为粗粒化流体中动态相关团簇弛豫过程的本质。

Abstract: Amorphous glass-forming polymers exhibit multiple relaxation processes, including the structural α-relaxation associated with the glass transition and faster secondary relaxations that typically follow Arrhenius behavior. Recently, a distinct slow Arrhenius process (SAP) has been observed at frequencies well below the α-process. Although Arrhenian in its temperature dependence, the SAP involves much longer relaxation times and its microscopic origin remains unclear. Here, we extend the two-state, two-timescale (TS2) theory to describe both the α-relaxation and the SAP within a unified framework. We propose that the SAP represents the high-temperature limit of an α-like process in a coarse-grained fluid of dynamically correlated clusters. With renormalized interaction energies and coordination parameters, the same model quantitatively reproduces both α and SAP data across multiple polymers without additional adjustable parameters and explains the observed Meyer-Neldel compensation behavior. The theory further predicts that the SAP should deviate from Arrhenius behavior at sufficiently low temperatures, transitioning to Vogel-Fulcher-Tammann-Hesse-like dynamics, thereby offering a physically transparent interpretation of cluster-scale relaxation in glass-forming polymers.

</details>


### [57] [Fluid-Solid Pattern Formation and Strain Localisation via Shear Banding Instability in Model Biological Tissues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08644)
*Aidan J. Nicholas,Suzanne M. Fielding*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了生物组织流变特性在形态发生中的新机制：通过组织应变场的力学不稳定性（mechanical instability）实现自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking），导致流体和固体区域共存的图案化结构，应变高度局域化为剪切带（shear bands）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用组织力学的顶点模型（vertex model of tissue mechanics），分析组织应变场中的力学不稳定性机制。通过比较内部细胞间耗散（internal cell-cell dissipation）主导与外部基底阻力（external drag）主导两种不同组织环境下的差异。

Result: 研究表明自发对称破缺可通过变形组织的应变场力学不稳定性实现，导致流体和固体区域共存的图案化结构，应变高度局域化为剪切带。剪切带的性质在内部细胞间耗散主导的组织与外部基底阻力主导的组织中存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了组织力学不稳定性作为形态发生中图案形成的新机制，超越了传统的化学形态发生素浓度场理论，为理解生物组织流变特性在发育过程中的作用提供了新的力学视角。

Abstract: The rheological properties of biological tissues are core to processes such as cancer metastasis, wound healing and embryo development. The emergence of tissue and organ structures during morphogenesis requires the precise formation of spatial patterns. Dating back to Turing, pattern formation has been suggested to arise in tissues via spontaneous symmetry breaking instabilities in the concentration field of chemical morphogens. Within the vertex model of tissue mechanics, we show that spontaneous symmetry breaking may also arise via a mechanical instability in the strain field of a deformed tissue, leading to a patterned coexistence of fluid and solid regions, with a strong localisation of the strain into shear bands. The nature of the bands differs between tissues in which internal cell-cell dissipation dominates external drag against a substrate, and vice versa.

### [58] [Enhanced Rydberg Blockade through RF-tuned Förster Resonance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07958)
*Lukas Palm,Bowen Li,Yiming Cady Feng,Marius Jürgensen,Jon Simon*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用微波驱动产生的交流斯塔克效应（AC Stark shifts）调谐至福斯特共振（Förster resonance）的新技术，将里德堡原子（Rydberg atoms）相互作用从范德瓦尔斯（Van-der-Waals）的1/R⁶标度提升为偶极-偶极（dipolar）的1/R³标度，从而增强了相互作用的强度和范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 增强里德堡原子（Rydberg atoms）之间的相互作用是当前量子技术的关键挑战。更强的相互作用能够在数字处理器中实现更快的里德堡门（Rydberg gates），并在模拟仿真中产生更大的纠缠态（entangled states）。在较低的主量子数（principal quantum number）下实现相同的相互作用强度，可以解决当前大规模光镊（tweezer）或腔QED（cavity QED）实验中可用拉比频率（Rabi frequency）和场灵敏度的限制。

Method: 本文展示了一种新技术：利用微波驱动产生的交流斯塔克效应（AC Stark shifts）调谐至福斯特共振（Förster resonance），从而将相互作用随距离的标度从1/R⁶修改为1/R³。该方法在铷-87（⁸⁷Rb）原子中n=44的里德堡极化子（Rydberg polariton）腔阻塞（cavity Rydberg polariton blockade）实验中进行了验证。

Result: 实验验证了增强的里德堡相互作用（强度和范围）：在范德瓦尔斯（Van-der-Waals）区域测得g²(0)=1.0(1)，而在福斯特共振（Förster resonance）的偶极区域（dipolar regime）测得g²(0)=0.38(1)。该技术使原始里德堡态（Rydberg state）的偏移最小化，抑制了门协议中的失谐误差（detuning errors），同时保持了对直流电场（DC electric fields）的二次不敏感性。

Conclusion: 该技术通过微波驱动的交流斯塔克效应（AC Stark shifts）调谐至福斯特共振（Förster resonance），有效增强了里德堡原子（Rydberg atoms）的相互作用强度和范围，同时最小化了对原始里德堡态的扰动，为量子信息处理和模拟仿真提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Enhancing interactions between Rydberg atoms is a key challenge in contemporary quantum technologies. Stronger interactions enable faster Rydberg gates in digital processors and larger entangled states in analog simulation. Achieving the same interaction strength at lower principal quantum number addresses current constraints in available Rabi frequency and field sensitivity in large scale tweezer or cavity QED experiments. Here, we demonstrate a new technique using AC Stark shifts from a microwave drive to tune into a Förster resonance, thereby modifying the interaction scaling with distance from $1/R^6$ to $1/R^3$. We validate enhanced Rydberg interactions (in strength and range) by probing cavity Rydberg polariton blockade at $n=44$ in $^{87}$Rb, improving from $g^{(2)}(0) = 1.0 (1)$ in the Van-der-Waals regime to $g^{(2)}(0) = 0.38 (1)$ in the dipolar regime on the Förster resonance. Importantly, our technique allows minimal shifts of the original Rydberg state, suppressing detuning errors in gate protocols while maintaining quadratic insensitivity to DC electric fields.

</details>

### [60] [Soliton solutions to the coupled Sasa-Satsuma equation under mixed boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08686)
*Changyan Shi,Xiyao Chen,Guangxiong Zhang,Chengfa Wu,Bao-Feng Feng*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文通过KP约化方法推导了耦合Sasa-Satsuma方程的亮-暗孤子解，从四分量Hirota方程的双亮-双暗孤子解出发，通过参数约束约化为CSS方程的亮-暗孤子解，并分析了其动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为耦合Sasa-Satsuma方程（CSS equation）推导通用的亮-暗孤子解（bright-dark soliton solutions）。由于CSS方程是四分量Hirota方程的特殊情况，因此需要建立从更一般方程到特定方程的约化方法。

Method: 采用Kadomtsev-Petviashvili约化方法（KP reduction method），首先构造四分量Hirota方程的双亮-双暗孤子解（two-bright-two-dark soliton solutions），然后通过施加特定参数约束，将这些解约化为CSS方程的亮-暗孤子解。

Result: 成功推导出耦合Sasa-Satsuma方程的亮-暗孤子解，包括单亮-暗孤子解和双亮-暗孤子解。对这些解的动力学行为进行了详细分析和图示说明。

Conclusion: 通过KP约化方法有效获得了CSS方程的亮-暗孤子解，该方法从更一般的四分量Hirota方程出发，通过参数约束实现约化，为研究耦合非线性系统的孤子动力学提供了系统框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we derive general bright-dark soliton solutions to the coupled Sasa-Satsuma (CSS) equation using the Kadomtsev-Petviashvili (KP) reduction method. Since the CSS equation is a special case of the four-component Hirota equation, our approach begins with the construction of two-bright-two-dark soliton solutions for the four-component Hirota equation. By imposing specific parameter constraints, these solutions are subsequently reduced to the bright-dark soliton solutions of the CSS equation. Finally, the dynamical behaviors of the one- and two-bright-dark soliton solutions are thoroughly analyzed and illustrated.

</details>

### [61] [First inclusive triple-differential measurement of the muon-antineutrino charged-current cross section using the NOvA Near Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06718)
*The NOvA Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: NOvA实验首次测量了μ子反中微子三重微分电荷交换包容截面，使用NuMI束流中12.5×10²⁰质子靶数据，获得了约100万个μ子反中微子事件，这是迄今最大的相关数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在首次测量μ子反中微子三重微分电荷交换包容截面（triple-differential muon antineutrino charged-current inclusive cross section），以隔离不同中微子反应过程占据的相空间区域并定义它们之间的过渡区域。

Method: 使用NOvA近探测器（Near Detector）和NuMI束流中12.5×10²⁰质子靶数据，测量基于末态动能、散射角和相互作用可用能量的三重微分截面。

Result: 获得了约100万个选择的μ子反中微子事件，这是迄今最大的相关数据集。测量结果显示，在广泛的能量范围和相互作用类型中，与中微子学界主要事件生成器（event generators）的预测存在能量和角度依赖的差异。

Conclusion: 该三重微分截面测量能够隔离不同中微子反应过程占据的相空间区域，并定义它们之间的过渡区域，为理论模型验证提供了重要实验数据。

Abstract: We present the first measurement of the triple-differential muon antineutrino charged-current inclusive cross section, using the NOvA Near Detector and $12.5 \times 10^{20}$ protons on target in the NuMI beam. This sample of muon antineutrino interactions is the largest ever published, with approximately 1 million selected muon antineutrino events. The triple-differential cross section is measured in the final-state kinetic energy, the scattering angle, and the available energy of the interaction. The measurement enables phase-space regions populated by differing neutrino reaction processes to be isolated and the transition regions between them to be defined. The results are compared with the predictions of the main event generators used in the neutrino community and we observe energy- and angle-dependent discrepancies across a broad range of energies and interaction types

</details>


### [62] [AI Agents, Language, Deep Learning and the Next Revolution in Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07940)
*Ke Li,Beijiang Liu,Bruce Mellado,Changzheng Yuan,Zhengde Zhang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出以智能AI代理（intelligent AI agents）为核心的新科学范式，旨在解决数据生成与理解之间的失衡问题，并以粒子物理（particle physics）为测试平台，通过Dr. Sai系统展示其应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代科学面临数据规模、多样性和相互依赖性的急剧增长，传统分析方法已无法应对。数据生成与理解之间的失衡（growing imbalance）迫切需要新的科学范式（new scientific paradigm）。

Method: 提出基于大语言模型（large language models）和多模态学习（multimodal learning）的智能AI代理系统，这些代理能够解释科学意图、设计和执行分析工作流程，并通过特定领域语言（domain-specific languages）确保可追溯性和人类监督。

Result: 在中国科学院高能物理研究所（Institute of High Energy Physics of the Chinese Academy of Sciences）部署的Dr. Sai系统体现了这一愿景，这是一个应用于CEPC对撞机研究的多智能体推理框架（multi-agent reasoning framework）。

Conclusion: 这种新兴方法不取代人类科学家，而是扩展其认知能力，使发现能够随复杂性扩展，并重新定义智能机器时代知识生产的方式。该范式的重要性超越了粒子物理，为所有面临复杂性上限的数据驱动科学提供了蓝图。

Abstract: Modern science is reaching a critical inflection point. Instruments across disciplines, from particle physics and astronomy to genomics and climate modeling, now produce data of such scale, diversity, and interdependence that traditional analytical methods can no longer keep pace. This growing imbalance between data generation and data understanding signals the need for a new scientific paradigm. We propose that intelligent, human-supervised AI agents operating over deep-learning algorithms, represent the next evolution of the scientific method. Built upon large language models and multimodal learning, these agents can interpret scientific intent, design and execute analytical workflows, and ensure traceability through domain-specific languages that preserve human oversight and accountability. Particle physics, a historic incubator of computational innovation, offers the ideal testbed for this transition. At the Institute of High Energy Physics of the Chinese Academy of Sciences, the Dr. Sai system embodies this vision, a multi-agent reasoning framework deployed within collider research at the CEPC. This emerging approach does not replace human scientists but extends their cognitive reach, enabling discovery to scale with complexity and redefining how knowledge itself is produced in the age of intelligent machines. The significance of this paradigm transcends particle physics, offering a blueprint for all data-driven sciences facing the same complexity ceiling.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器收集的$(10087 \pm 44) \times 10^{6}$ $J/ψ$事例，改进了$η^{\prime}\rightarrow e^{+}e^{-}ω$衰变的分支比测量，并首次报告了该衰变的跃迁形状因子截断参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在改进$η^{\prime}\rightarrow e^{+}e^{-}ω$衰变的分支比测量精度，并首次测量该衰变的跃迁形状因子（transition form factor）截断参数，为理解$η^{\prime}$介子的内部结构和检验理论模型提供重要数据。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器收集的$(10087 \pm 44) \times 10^{6}$ $J/ψ$事例样本，分析$η^{\prime}\rightarrow e^{+}e^{-}ω$衰变过程，其中$ω\rightarrowπ^{+}π^{-}π^{0}$且$π^{0}\rightarrowγγ$，采用改进的测量方法。

Result: 测得分支比$\mathcal{B}(η^{\prime}\rightarrow e^{+}e^{-}ω) = (1.79 \pm 0.09 \pm 0.12) \times 10^{-4}$，统计不确定度在前，系统不确定度在后；首次报告跃迁形状因子截断参数$Λ^{-1} = (2.92 \pm 0.83 \pm 0.15)~\text{GeV}^{-1}$，结果与先前测量一致但精度显著提高。

Conclusion: 这些测量结果为理解$η^{\prime}$介子的内部结构和检验理论模型提供了有价值的输入，改进的测量精度和首次报告的跃迁形状因子参数对相关理论研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: Using a sample of $(10087 \pm 44) \times 10^{6}$ $J/ψ$ events collected with the BESIII detector, an improved measurement of the decay $η^{\prime}\rightarrow e^{+}e^{-}ω$, with $ω\rightarrowπ^{+}π^{-}π^{0}$ and $π^{0}\rightarrowγγ$ is performed. The branching fraction is determined to be $\mathcal{B}(η^{\prime}\rightarrow e^{+}e^{-}ω) = (1.79 \pm 0.09 \pm 0.12) \times 10^{-4}$, where the first uncertainty is statistical and the second is systematic. This result is consistent with the previous measurement and is obtained with significantly improved precision. Furthermore, the first measurement of the transition form factor cutoff parameter for this decay is reported, with $Λ^{-1} = (2.92 \pm 0.83 \pm 0.15)~\text{GeV}^{-1}$. These measurements provide valuable input for understanding the internal structure of the $η^{\prime}$ meson and testing theoretical models.

</details>


### [64] [Search for long-lived charginos and $τ$-sleptons using final states with a disappearing track in $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08315)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报告了在ATLAS探测器Run 2数据中，对长寿命带电荷粒子（charginos）或τ-标轻子（τ-sleptons）衰变为包含短寿命消失径迹、单个高能喷注和横向动量缺失的末态进行的搜寻。未发现显著超出，并对不同寿命区间的粒子质量设置了95%置信水平下限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在搜寻长寿命超对称粒子，特别是带电荷粒子（charginos）和τ-标轻子（τ-sleptons），这些粒子衰变会产生特征性的短寿命消失径迹（disappearing track）、高能喷注和横向动量缺失（missing transverse momentum）。此类搜寻对于探索超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理至关重要。

Method: 使用ATLAS探测器记录的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据（137 fb⁻¹），定义了多个搜寻区域。所有区域都要求在ATLAS探测器最内层通过三或四次测量重建出径迹。对于仅有三次测量的径迹，进一步使用基于机器学习（machine learning）的专用算法，根据是否存在重建的低能带电π介子进行特征化。采用数据驱动方法（data-driven methods）估计背景贡献。

Result: 未发现显著超出。在0.01-10 ns寿命范围内，对带电荷粒子和τ-标轻子的质量设置了95%置信水平（CL）下限。对于寿命低于0.03 ns的纯希格斯微子（pure-higgsino）带电荷粒子，观测（预期）质量上限达225 GeV（250 GeV）；对于寿命约1 ns的带电荷粒子，上限达720 GeV（840 GeV）。在温诺（wino）产生情景下，寿命约1 ns、质量达880 GeV（1020 GeV）的带电荷粒子被排除。对于寿命约1 ns的τ-标轻子，在约束最小超对称标准模型（Constrained Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model）和规范介导超对称破缺（Gauge-Mediated Supersymmetry-Breaking）情景下，质量上限分别为320 GeV（390 GeV）和300 GeV（380 GeV）。

Conclusion: 该搜寻未发现长寿命带电荷粒子或τ-标轻子衰变的显著证据。研究为不同超对称情景下的粒子质量设定了严格的实验限制，为探索超出标准模型的新物理提供了重要约束。

Abstract: This paper reports a search for decays of long-lived charginos or $τ$-sleptons to final states containing a short disappearing track, a single high-energy jet, and missing transverse momentum. The search uses 137 fb$^{-1}$ of data from 13 TeV proton-proton collisions recorded by the ATLAS detector during Run 2 of the LHC. Multiple search regions are defined, all requiring the presence of a track reconstructed from either three or four measurements in the innermost layers of the ATLAS detector. Regions with tracks having only three measurements are further characterised by the absence or presence of a low-energy charged pion reconstructed using a dedicated algorithm, leveraging machine learning. Data-driven methods are used to estimate the background contributions in the search regions. No significant excesses are found and 95% CL lower limits are placed on the masses of charginos and $τ$-sleptons in the lifetime range $0.01{-}10$ ns. Observed (expected) mass limits of up to 225 GeV (250 GeV) are set for pure-higgsino charginos in scenarios with lifetimes below 0.03 ns, where the electroweakino mass splitting is entirely due to loop corrections involving the Standard Model bosons, and up to 720 GeV (840 GeV) for charginos with a lifetime of around 1 ns. For wino production, charginos with masses up to 880 GeV (1020 GeV) are excluded for lifetimes of around 1 ns. For $τ$-sleptons with lifetimes of around 1 ns, masses are excluded up to 320 GeV (390 GeV) in Constrained Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model scenarios and 300 GeV (380 GeV) in Gauge-Mediated Supersymmetry-Breaking scenarios.

</details>


### [65] [Search for decays of the Higgs boson into pair-produced pseudoscalar particles decaying into $τ^+τ^-τ^+τ^-$ using $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08323)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究利用ATLAS探测器在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上收集的140 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，搜索低质量赝标量粒子对a衰变为τ轻子的过程，并对希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）衰变为四个τ轻子的奇异衰变分支比设置了上限约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）可能存在的奇异衰变模式H→aa→τ⁺τ⁻τ⁺τ⁻，其中a为低质量赝标量粒子（pseudoscalar）。这种衰变通道是超越标准模型（Beyond Standard Model）物理的重要探针，有助于揭示希格斯玻色子与暗物质候选粒子等新物理现象的可能联系。

Method: 研究使用ATLAS探测器在13 TeV质心能量下记录的140 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据。搜索专注于包含一个或两个τ轻子（τ-lepton）强子衰变（hadronic decay）与中微子（neutrino），以及剩余三个或两个τ轻子电子或μ子衰变的事件。通过分析这些特定衰变通道来识别可能的信号事件。

Result: 在15-60 GeV质量范围内，未观察到显著超出标准模型（Standard Model）背景预期的信号。基于95%置信水平（95% confidence level），对衰变分支比ℬ(H→aa→τ⁺τ⁻τ⁺τ⁻)设置了上限约束，其数值范围从0.06到0.23，具体取决于赝标量粒子质量m_a。

Conclusion: 本研究对希格斯玻色子奇异衰变H→aa→τ⁺τ⁻τ⁺τ⁻通道进行了系统搜索，未发现新物理证据。获得的衰变分支比上限为未来类似搜索提供了重要参考基准，并约束了相关超越标准模型理论参数空间。

Abstract: A search for a pair of low-mass pseudoscalars $a$ that promptly decay into $τ$-leptons is presented using 140 fb$^{-1}$ of proton-proton collision data at $13$ TeV centre-of-mass energy recorded with the ATLAS detector at the Large Hadron Collider. The result is used to place constraints on exotic decays of the Higgs boson into four $τ$-leptons, $H\to aa\to τ^+τ^-τ^+τ^-$. This search focuses on events with either one or two $τ$-leptons decaying into hadrons and neutrinos, and the remaining three or two $τ$-leptons decaying into either electron or muon and neutrinos. No significant excess is observed above the expected Standard Model background and upper limits at the 95% confidence level on $\mathcal{B}(H\rightarrow aa\rightarrow τ^+τ^-τ^+τ^-)$ are set ranging from 0.06 to 0.23, depending on the mass $m_a$ ranging from 15 to 60 GeV.

</details>


### [66] [End-to-end optimisation of HEP triggers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08428)
*Noah Clarke Hall,Ioannis Xiotidis,Nikos Konstantinidis,David W. Miller*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种端到端优化框架，将高能物理实验中的实时触发系统设计重新表述为约束优化问题，相比传统模块化方法在固定误报率下实现了2-4倍的真阳性率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理实验面临极端数据速率，需要实时触发系统在降低事件吞吐量的同时保持对稀有过程的敏感性。传统触发系统采用模块化链式结构，各算法仅针对局部目标优化，无法保证整体最优性。

Method: 将触发设计重新表述为约束端到端优化问题，将数据编码、去噪、聚类和校准等所有阶段视为单一可微分系统的组件，针对统一的物理目标进行训练。该框架在优化性能的同时纳入物理和部署约束。

Result: 在受ATLAS高亮度大型强子对撞机设计启发的硬件多喷注触发系统上验证该方法，以希格斯玻色子对产生为基准，在固定误报率下观察到真阳性率提升2-4倍，同时保持了可解释的中间物理对象和单调校准约束。

Conclusion: 端到端优化为下一代实时事件选择系统提供了实用范式，通过整体优化方法显著提升了触发系统性能，同时保持了物理可解释性和约束满足。

Abstract: High-energy physics experiments face extreme data rates, requiring real-time trigger systems to reduce event throughput while preserving sensitivity to rare processes. Trigger systems are typically constructed as modular chains of sequentially optimised algorithms, including machine learning models. Each algorithm is optimised for a specific local objective with no guarantee of overall optimality. We instead formulate trigger design as a constrained end-to-end optimisation problem, treating all stages- including data encoding, denoising, clustering, and calibration- as components of a single differentiable system trained against a unified physics objective. The framework jointly optimises performance while incorporating physics and deployment constraints. We demonstrate this approach on a hardware multi-jet trigger inspired by the ATLAS High-Luminosity Large Hadron Collider design. Using Higgs boson pair production as a benchmark, we observe x2-4 improvement in true-positive rate at fixed false-positive rate, while preserving interpretable intermediate physics objects and monotonic calibration constraints. These results highlight end-to-end optimisation as a practical paradigm for next-generation real-time event selection systems.

</details>

R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII实验利用4.4 fb⁻¹的e⁺e⁻对撞数据，对单卡比玻压低衰变Λ⁺_c→pK⁺K⁻进行振幅分析，首次观测到Λ(1405)K⁺和Λ(1670)K⁺衰变模式，并将Λ⁺_c→pK⁺K⁻的分支比更新为(9.94±0.65_stat±0.50_syst)×10⁻⁴，精度提高约1.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过振幅分析（amplitude analysis）精确测量单卡比玻压低（singly Cabibbo-suppressed）衰变Λ⁺_c→pK⁺K⁻的分支比，并探索其中可能的共振态衰变模式，特别是首次观测Λ(1405)K⁺和Λ(1670)K⁺衰变通道。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的4.4 fb⁻¹积分亮度e⁺e⁻湮灭数据，质心能量范围为4600-4698 MeV，对Λ⁺_c→pK⁺K⁻衰变进行振幅分析，测量多个衰变模式的分支比。

Result: 测量得到Λ⁺_c→pφ(1020)、pf₀(980)、Λ(1405)K⁺和Λ(1670)K⁺的分支比，其中后两种模式为首次观测；基于振幅分析结果，将Λ⁺_c→pK⁺K⁻总分支比更新为(9.94±0.65_stat±0.50_syst)×10⁻⁴，与当前世界平均值在一个标准偏差内一致，精度较先前BESIII测量提高约1.5倍。

Conclusion: 该研究成功实现了对Λ⁺_c→pK⁺K⁻衰变的精确振幅分析，首次观测到Λ(1405)K⁺和Λ(1670)K⁺衰变模式，并显著提高了Λ⁺_c→pK⁺K⁻分支比的测量精度，为理解粲重子衰变机制提供了重要实验数据。

Abstract: Using a sample of $e^{+}e^{-}$ annihilation data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 4.4 $\rm{fb}^{-1}$ collected with the BESIII detector at the BEPCII collider and produced at center-of-mass energies from $4600$ to $4698~\rm{MeV}$, an amplitude analysis is performed of the singly Cabibbo-suppressed decay $Λ^{+}_{c}\to pK^{+}K^{-}$. The branching fractions of $Λ^{+}_{c}\to pφ(1020)$, $pf_{0}(980)$, $Λ(1405)K^{+}$, and $Λ(1670)K^{+}$ are measured, where the latter two modes are decays that are observed for the first time. At the same time, with the detection efficiency based on the results of the amplitude analysis, the branching fraction of $Λ^{+}_{c}\to pK^{+}K^{-}$ is updated to be $(9.94\pm0.65_{\text{stat.}}\pm0.50_{\text{syst.}})\times10^{-4}$, which is consistent with the current world average value within one standard deviation. The result supersedes the previous BESIII measurement with precision improved by approximately a factor of 1.5.

</details>

Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,Q. Zou,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文首次观测到B_s^0介子衰变到K_S^0 K^+ K^-的过程，并测量了多个无粲（charmless）三体衰变的支化比（branching fraction ratios）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究B^0和B_s^0介子的无粲三体衰变过程，特别是首次观测B_s^0 → K_S^0 K^+ K^-衰变，以理解这些衰变模式的特性并测量其支化比。

Method: 利用LHCb实验收集的质子-质子（pp）对撞数据，对应积分亮度为9 fb^{-1}，分析B^0_{(s)} → K_S^0 h^+ h'^-衰变（其中h^{(')} = π, K）。

Result: 首次观测到B_s^0 → K_S^0 K^+ K^-衰变，并测量了五个支化比，包括B^0 → K_S^0 K^+ K^-与B^0 → K_S^0 π^+π^-的比值为0.578 ± 0.007 ± 0.017等结果。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了B^0和B_s^0介子无粲三体衰变的重要测量结果，特别是首次观测到的B_s^0 → K_S^0 K^+ K^-衰变，为理解这些衰变过程提供了新的实验数据。

Abstract: This paper presents a study of the charmless three-body decays ${B^0_{(s)} \to K_{\mathrm{S}}^0 h^+ h^{\prime -}}$ (where $h^{(\prime)} = π, K$), using a sample of $pp$ collision data collected by the LHCb experiment, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $9\mbox{\,fb}^{-1}$. The decay ${B^0_s \to K_{\mathrm{S}}^0 K^+ K^-}$ is observed for the first time, and the following ratios of branching fractions are measured: \begin{alignat*}{6}
  &\frac{{\cal B}(B^0 \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} K^+ K^-)}{{\cal B}(B^0 \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} π^+π^-)} &&= 0.578 &&\pm 0.007 &&\pm 0.017\,,
  &\frac{{\cal B}(B^0 \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} K^\pmπ^\mp)}{{\cal B}(B^0 \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} π^+π^-)} &&= 0.1363 &&\pm 0.0035 &&\pm 0.0051\,,
  &\frac{{\cal B}(B^0_s \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} π^+π^-)}{{\cal B}(B^0 \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} π^+π^-)} &&= 0.269 &&\pm 0.011 &&\pm 0.015 && \pm 0.008\,,
  &\frac{{\cal B}(B^0_s \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} K^+ K^-)}{{\cal B}(B^0 \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} π^+π^-)} &&= 0.0303 &&\pm 0.0041 &&\pm 0.0025 && \pm 0.0009\,,
  &\frac{{\cal B}(B^0_s \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} K^\pmπ^\mp)}{{\cal B}(B^0 \to K^0_{\mathrm{S}} π^+π^-)} &&= 1.818 &&\pm 0.021 &&\pm 0.031 && \pm 0.056\,, \end{alignat*} where the uncertainties are statistical, systematic, and due to knowledge of the ratio of hadronisation fractions of the $B^0_s$ and $B^0$ mesons, respectively.

</details>

### [69] [Group Entropies and Mirror Duality: A Class of Flexible Mirror Descent Updates for Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08651)
*Andrzej Cichocki,Piergiulio Tempesta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个连接形式群论（formal group theory）、群熵（group entropies）与机器学习的理论算法框架，构建了无限灵活的镜像下降（Mirror Descent）算法族，通过群理论镜像映射实现高度可适应的优化更新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有镜像下降算法缺乏足够的灵活性来适应多样化的数据几何结构和统计分布。本文旨在通过形式群论和群熵的丰富结构，构建一个更通用、可扩展的优化框架，超越传统的Shannon、Tsallis和Kaniadakis熵族。

Method: 利用群熵（group entropies）作为广义熵泛函，通过群组合律（group composition laws）进行控制。采用群理论镜像映射（group-theoretical mirror maps）或链接函数（link functions），表达为多参数广义对数（multi-parametric generalized logarithms）及其逆（群指数，group exponentials）。引入镜像对偶性（mirror duality）概念，允许在特定学习率约束下无缝切换链接函数与其逆函数。

Result: 提出了一个无限、灵活的镜像下降算法族，能够通过调整或学习群对数的超参数来适应训练分布的统计特性，同时通过微调确保理想的收敛特性。该框架不仅提供了更大的灵活性和改进的收敛特性，还为机器学习中的正则化器和自然梯度算法设计开辟了新视角。

Conclusion: 该框架在大型单纯形约束二次规划问题上进行了广泛评估，验证了其有效性、鲁棒性和性能。通过桥接形式群论、群熵与现代机器学习，为优化算法设计提供了新的理论基础和应用前景。

Abstract: We introduce a comprehensive theoretical and algorithmic framework that bridges formal group theory and group entropies with modern machine learning, paving the way for an infinite, flexible family of Mirror Descent (MD) optimization algorithms. Our approach exploits the rich structure of group entropies, which are generalized entropic functionals governed by group composition laws, encompassing and significantly extending all trace-form entropies such as the Shannon, Tsallis, and Kaniadakis families. By leveraging group-theoretical mirror maps (or link functions) in MD, expressed via multi-parametric generalized logarithms and their inverses (group exponentials), we achieve highly flexible and adaptable MD updates that can be tailored to diverse data geometries and statistical distributions. To this end, we introduce the notion of \textit{mirror duality}, which allows us to seamlessly switch or interchange group-theoretical link functions with their inverses, subject to specific learning rate constraints. By tuning or learning the hyperparameters of the group logarithms enables us to adapt the model to the statistical properties of the training distribution, while simultaneously ensuring desirable convergence characteristics via fine-tuning. This generality not only provides greater flexibility and improved convergence properties, but also opens new perspectives for applications in machine learning and deep learning by expanding the design of regularizers and natural gradient algorithms. We extensively evaluate the validity, robustness, and performance of the proposed updates on large-scale, simplex-constrained quadratic programming problems.

### [70] [Physics-Consistent Neural Networks for Learning Deformation and Director Fields in Microstructured Media with Loss-Based Validation Criteria](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06939)
*Milad Shirani,Pete H. Gueldner,Murat Khidoyatov,Jeremy L. Warren,Federica Ninno*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在分析具有微观结构的固体力学行为，这些材料中的变形场与取向场存在耦合效应。传统方法需要发展能够捕捉这种耦合的计算框架。

Method: 采用具有单一单位指向矢（single unit director）的Cosserat弹性理论框架，开发了两种互补计算方法：基于变分原理的有限元公式和直接最小化总势能的神经网络求解器。神经网络架构被设计为尊重理论的基本运动学结构。

Result: 推导了Cosserat模型的拟凸性条件（quasiconvexity condition）、秩一凸性条件（rank-one convexity condition）和Legendre-Hadamard不等式，并将其表述为适合评估神经网络预测的形式。这些必要的稳定性条件构成了基于物理的验证框架。

Conclusion: 通过将经典变分稳定性理论与现代机器学习求解器相结合，建立了一个计算工作流程，其中平衡解不仅被学习，还根据能量一致性进行评估。违反必要稳定性条件的网络输出可以被拒绝，因为它们不对应于稳定的能量最小化器。

Abstract: In this work, we study the mechanical behavior of solids with microstructure using the framework of Cosserat elasticity with a single unit director. This formulation captures the coupling between deformation and orientational fields that arises in many structured materials. To compute equilibrium configurations of such media, we develop two complementary computational approaches: a finite element formulation based on variational principles and a neural network-based solver that directly minimizes the total potential energy. The neural architecture is constructed to respect the fundamental kinematic structure of the theory. In particular, it enforces frame invariance of the energy, satisfies the unit-length constraint on the director field, and represents deformation and director fields through separate networks to preserve their kinematic independence in the variational setting. Beyond satisfying balance laws, however, physically admissible solutions must also correspond to stable energy minimizers. To assess this requirement, we derive the quasiconvexity condition, rank-one convexity condition, and the Legendre-Hadamard inequalities for the Cosserat model and formulate them in a manner suitable for evaluating neural network predictions. These necessary stability conditions provide a physics-based validation framework: network outputs that violate these necessary conditions cannot correspond to stable energy minimizers and can therefore be rejected. In this way, we integrate classical variational stability theory with modern machine-learning solvers, establishing a computational workflow in which equilibrium solutions are not only learned but also assessed for energetic consistency.

### [71] [Mass Without Mass from a Berry--Shifted SU(3) Holonomy Rotor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06770)
*Ahmed Farag Ali*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究在纯SU(3)杨-米尔斯理论中识别出一种局域、规范不变的机制，可在三维穿孔球上产生有限谱标度。通过固定$\mathbb{Z}_3$中心扇区，隔离出单个规范不变完整角，其贝里位移产生具有严格非零能级间距的量子转子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索纯杨-米尔斯理论中如何在不引入显式质量项或希格斯场的情况下产生质量尺度。这实现了威尔切克意义上的"无质量的质量（mass without mass）"，其中非零能级间距由规范不变性、拓扑结构和所选中心扇区共同决定。

Method: 方法包括：固定$\mathbb{Z}_3$中心扇区以隔离规范不变完整角；使用具有相对边界条件的协变标量拉普拉斯算子的狄利克雷逆构建协变狄利克雷亥姆霍兹投影算子来实施高斯定律；通过变分法选择慢完整模作为完整约束下横向电能的最小化器。

Result: 获得了与规范代表无关的惯性，具有线性域尺寸标度性和受控的对易子主导区域。证明了投影算子的稳定性，并推导出第一个正杨-米尔斯特征值的绝热变分上界。在飞米尺度和实际耦合下的基准测试给出了强子尺度（约1 GeV）的上界。

Conclusion: 该研究在有限域上实现了纯SU(3)杨-米尔斯理论中的"无质量的质量"机制。非零能级间距由规范不变性、拓扑和中心扇区选择共同固定。在闵可夫斯基空间中解释长度$R$需要额外的物理输入（如局域禁闭长度）。

Abstract: We identify a local, gauge-invariant mechanism that generates a finite spectral scale in pure SU(3) Yang--Mills theory on a punctured three-ball. Fixing a $\mathbb{Z}_3$ center sector isolates a single gauge-invariant holonomy angle whose Berry shift produces a quantum rotor with strictly nonzero level spacing. Gauss law is enforced by a covariant Dirichlet Helmholtz projector built from the Dirichlet inverse of the covariant scalar Laplacian with relative boundary conditions. The slow holonomy mode is chosen variationally as the minimizer of transverse electric energy under the holonomy constraint, yielding an inertia \emph{independent of the gauge representative} with linear domain-size scaling and a controlled commutator-dominated regime. We prove projector stability and derive an adiabatic variational upper bound on the first positive Yang--Mills eigenvalue, with error controlled by the transverse vector gap of the covariant Laplacian on divergence-free one-forms. A femtometer-scale benchmark at realistic coupling gives an upper bound at a hadronic ($\sim 1\,$GeV) scale. In Wilczek's sense this realizes ``mass without mass'': no explicit mass term or Higgs field is introduced, and the nonzero level spacing is fixed by gauge invariance, topology, and the chosen center sector. The present results are derived on a finite domain; interpreting the length $R$ in Minkowski space requires an additional physical input (e.g.\ as a local confinement length), which we make explicit.

### [72] [All $2D$ generalised dilaton theories from $d\geq 4$ gravities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06786)
*Johanna Borissova*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明所有二维霍恩德斯基理论（Horndeski theories）均可从d≥4维纯引力理论约化得到，并建立了这类理论的伯克霍夫定理（Birkhoff theorem），提出"准拓扑引力（quasi-topological gravities）"概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维霍恩德斯基理论的高维引力起源，探索这类理论与高维真空引力解之间的对应关系，为理解特定引力理论的结构提供新视角。

Method: 通过维度约化方法，将d维广义协变引力作用量（仅包含曲率不变量且运动方程为二阶）约化为二维霍恩德斯基理论；建立伯克霍夫定理并分析静态球对称解的性质。

Result: 证明所有二维霍恩德斯基理论都对应d维引力真空解；建立了这类理论的伯克霍夫定理，静态球对称解在史瓦西规范（Schwarzschild gauge）下满足g_tt g_rr = -1；提出"准拓扑引力"概念描述这类理论。

Conclusion: 所有满足特定条件的引力理论都可约化为可积的二维霍恩德斯基理论，其静态球对称解具有特殊形式；这类理论可重构满足g_tt g_rr = -1条件的d维渐近平坦时空，但某些正则黑洞（如巴丁时空）无法从仅含曲率不变量的准拓扑引力获得。

Abstract: We show that all two-dimensional Horndeski theories can arise from the reduction of pure gravities in $d \geq 4$ dimensions and therefore all onshell configurations for the two-dimensional metric and scalar field correspond to genuine $d$-dimensional gravitational vacuum solutions. We discuss separately the two-dimensional Horndeski theories which can arise from the reduction of $d$-dimensional generally covariant gravitational actions built only from curvature invariants without covariant derivatives and possessing second-order equations of motion on $2 + (d-2)$ warped-product backgrounds. The discussion is subsequently extended to generic $d$-dimensional gravitational actions with this latter property. We establish a Birkhoff theorem for all gravitational theories whose reduction yields an integrable two-dimensional Horndeski theory, in which case static spherically symmetric solutions satisfy $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$ in Schwarzschild gauge whereby the metric function $g_{tt} = -f$ is determined by an algebraic equation. We therefore propose to call all such theories quasi-topological gravities. These results can be used to show in reverse that any $d$-dimensional static spherically symmetric and asymptotically flat spacetime satisfying $g_{tt} g_{rr} = -1$ in Schwarzschild gauge with an invertible dependence of $f$ on the ADM mass can be reconstructed explicitly as a vacuum solution to a $d$-dimensional gravitational theory. We discuss examples of regular black holes such as the Bardeen spacetime, which could not be obtained from polynomial and non-polynomial quasi-topological gravities involving only curvature invariants without covariant derivatives.

### [73] [Flat holography for spinor fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06794)
*Dmitry S. Ageev,Anna S. Bernakevich*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了四维闵可夫斯基时空中自由大质量旋量场的平坦时空全息字典，通过双曲（米尔恩）切片将体场分解为$\mathbb H^3$谐函数，获得重整化的壳上作用量并提取天球上对偶自旋算符的两点关联函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为四维闵可夫斯基时空中的自由大质量旋量场（free massive spinor field）建立平坦时空全息字典（flat-space holographic dictionary）。通过将体场分解为$\mathbb H^3$谐函数，研究其对偶边界理论的性质，特别是天球（celestial sphere）上自旋算符的关联函数。

Method: 采用双曲（米尔恩）切片（hyperbolic (Milne) slicing）将四维闵可夫斯基时空分解为$\mathbb H^3$（欧几里得$\mathrm{AdS}_3$）。将体旋量场分解为以连续参数标记的$\mathbb H^3$谐函数（harmonics），计算重整化的壳上作用量（renormalized on-shell action）作为边界数据的泛函，并提取对偶自旋算符的两点关联函数（two-point correlation functions）。

Result: 获得的天球关联函数具有二维共形对称性（two-dimensional conformal symmetry）所要求的普适形式，对应于自旋-$\frac{1}{2}$原初场（spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ primaries）。四维狄拉克问题被约化为一系列有效的$\mathrm{AdS}_3$问题，遵循标准AdS/CFT的逻辑。体旋量场的近边界行为（near-boundary behavior）确定了适当的天球源（celestial sources）和对偶算符的共形维数（conformal dimension）。

Conclusion: 本文成功构建了四维自由大质量旋量场的平坦时空全息对应，将四维狄拉克问题约化为有效的AdS$_3$问题。进一步构造了相关的旋量共形原初波函数（spinor conformal primary wavefunctions），并阐明了它们与平坦时空体-边界映射（bulk-to-boundary map）的关系。

Abstract: We develop a flat-space holographic dictionary for a free massive spinor field in four-dimensional Minkowski spacetime, using the hyperbolic (Milne) slicing into $\mathbb H^3$ (Euclidean $\mathrm{AdS}_3$). Decomposing bulk fields into $\mathbb H^3$ harmonics labeled by a continuous parameter, we obtain the renormalized on-shell action as a functional of boundary data and extract the corresponding two-point correlation functions of dual spinning operators on the celestial sphere. The resulting correlators take the universal form dictated by two-dimensional conformal symmetry for spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ primaries. In this way, the four-dimensional Dirac problem is reduced to a family of effective $\mathrm{AdS}_3$ problems, closely following the logic of standard AdS/CFT. We show how the near-boundary behavior of the bulk spinor selects the appropriate celestial sources and determines the conformal dimension of the dual operators. As a further application, we construct the associated spinor conformal primary wavefunctions and clarify their relation to the flat-space bulk-to-boundary map.

### [74] [Moduli Space Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06795)
*Luis Anchordoqui,Muldrow Etheredge,Dieter Lust*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用迷你超空间方法研究模空间中的量子力学。将模依赖函数视为算符，并利用涌现弦猜想中的分类关系来约束这些算符之间的非对易性。

Result: 研究发现模空间几何在波函数行为中起重要作用，导致激发波函数局域化于模空间内部，并具有正能量本征值。当存在势能时，这些效应导致模局域化远离经典最小值，通常产生激发态正能量态。

Conclusion: 模空间几何显著影响量子力学行为，导致激发态波函数的局域化和正能量特征。涌现弦猜想的分类关系能够约束模空间算符的非对易性，为模空间量子力学提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: In this paper, continuing the discussion about Species Quantum Mechanics, we investigate quantum mechanics in moduli spaces using a mini-superspace approach. From this perspective, moduli-dependent functions can be viewed as operators, and we explore how the taxonomic relations from the Emergent String Conjecture can constrain the non-commutativity between these operators. Next, we study wave functions on moduli spaces, and we find that the geometry of moduli space plays an important role and leads to excited wave functions localised in the bulks of moduli spaces, and with positive energy eigenvalues. For cases when potentials are present, these effects result in moduli localised away from classical minima, and often result in excited, positive energy states.

### [75] [Quantum (quadratic) gravity: replacing the massive tensor ghost with an inverted harmonic oscillator-like instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07150)
*K. Sravan Kumar,João Marto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 二次引力理论（quadratic gravity）中的额外自旋-2自由度可转化为健康的倒谐振子（IHO）型不稳定性，通过直和量子场论（DQFT）实现一致量子化，避免幺正性破坏，并为量子引力提供新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二次引力理论是四维中唯一的可重整化量子引力理论，但传统理解认为其包含有质量张量鬼态（massive tensor ghost），需要寻找新量子化方案来规避其不利影响。

Method: 采用直和量子场论（direct-sum quantum field theory, DQFT）框架，将额外自旋-2自由度转化为倒谐振子（inverted harmonic oscillator, IHO）型不稳定性，该模式具有几何超选择扇区（geometric superselection sectors）。

Result: 额外自旋-2自由度保持离壳（off-shell）状态，有效与普通物质场解耦，避免可观测过程中的幺正性破坏（unitarity violations）；该IHO不稳定性是基础物理中的普遍特征。

Conclusion: 这一新理解为量子引力提供了基本途径，并为宇宙起源提供了安全起点；同时推导出原初引力波（primordial gravitational waves）的关键观测预测，包括张量-标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）的新界限和大角尺度上的宇称不对称特征。

Abstract: The quadratic theory of gravity is the unique renormalizable theory of quantum gravity in 4 dimensions, as proved by K. S. Stelle in 1977. Over the decades, the theory has been understood to contain a massive tensor ghost, and several attempts have been made to evade its adverse effects by proposing new quantization prescriptions and interpretations. In this paper, we show that the additional spin--2 of quadratic gravity can be turned into a healthy inverted harmonic oscillator (IHO)-like instability, which can be quantized consistently with direct-sum quantum field theory (DQFT), which incorporates geometric superselection sectors. Such modes possess a well-defined quantum description yet do not admit a particle interpretation and are not part of the asymptotic spectrum, being characterized by hyperbolic evolution and spacelike momentum support. We argue that, as a consequence, the extra spin--2 degree of freedom remains off-shell and effectively decoupled from ordinary matter fields, avoiding unitarity violations in observable processes. We argue that this IHO instability is a prevalent feature of fundamental physics, whether it concerns quantum fields on curved spacetimes or the Higgs $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry breaking in the Standard Model of particle physics. Thus, we demonstrate that our new understanding of quadratic gravity offers a fundamental pathway to quantum gravity and a safe beginning for the Universe. Furthermore, we derive key observational predictions of this construction in the view of primordial gravitational waves with new bounds on the tensor-to-scalar ratio and the parity asymmetric features on the large angular scales.

</details>


### [76] [Time Dependent String Compactification: Towards Bouncing Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07298)
*Mir Mehedi Faruk*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究弦世界面上的维拉索罗约束（Virasoro constraint）如何产生零能量条件（Null Energy Condition, NEC），并探讨在时间依赖的弦紧致化下外部时空方向的NEC如何出现。

Result: 发现存在一种紧致化方案，其中平均爱因斯坦框架条件允许外部时空的低维描述违反NEC，从而实现反弹宇宙学（bouncing cosmology），而高维NEC仍保持满足。

Conclusion: 通过弦紧致化可以实现低维时空违反NEC而高维NEC保持满足的情况，这由世界面对称性决定，为反弹宇宙学提供了弦理论框架下的实现途径。

Abstract: We study the Null Energy Condition (NEC) arising from the Virasoro constraint on the string worldsheet. We then analyze how the NEC in the external spacetime directions emerges under general time-dependent string compactifications. Finally, we exhibit compactifications in which the averaged Einstein-frame condition allows the lowerdimensional description of the external spacetime to violate the NEC, thereby realizing a bouncing cosmology, while the higher-dimensional NEC remains satisfied, as dictated by worldsheet symmetry.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统性地将高阶导数修正纳入Horowitz-Polchinski弦/黑洞对应关系的解析处理中，特别是在对紫外敏感区域进行受控推导。

Method: 采用欧氏签名和大D展开（large-D expansion），将几何结构分离为普适近区和渐近远区；在近区将热标量（thermal scalar）简化为精确可解的薛定谔问题，在远区构建Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet理论的闭式解。

Abstract: We develop a unified analytic treatment of the Horowitz--Polchinski string/black hole correspondence that systematically incorporates higher-derivative corrections to gravity. Working in Euclidean signature -- where the Euclidean black hole and the thermal scalar arise as competing saddles of the same finite-temperature ensemble -- we include the Gauss--Bonnet term. The analysis is rendered tractable in this UV--sensitive regime by the large-\(D\) expansion, which sharply separates the geometry into a universal near-zone and an asymptotic far-zone. In the near-zone, the coupled large-\(D\) equations reduce the thermal-scalar sector to an exactly solvable Schrödinger problem, from which we extract the \(α'\)-corrected decay exponent and the corresponding shift of the Hagedorn temperature. In the far-zone, we construct closed-form Euclidean solutions of Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet theory at leading order in both \(1/D\) and \(α'\). Matching the two regions yields the complete corrected saddle -- fixing its temperature, horizon data, and on--shell action -- and permits a fully analytic comparison of free energies between the thermal-scalar and black hole phases. This provides a controlled derivation of the HP correspondence point with explicit higher-curvature corrections.

Abstract: We study entanglement entropy (EE) in interacting quantum field theories (QFTs) at finite density. We consider Neumann and Dirichlet boundary conditions for the bosonic fields, and the most general boundary conditions for the fermions that preserve unitarity, conformal invariance, and charge conjugation symmetry. We analyze the phase diagram and identify distinct fixed points corresponding to different universality classes of boundary critical behavior. The associated boundary critical exponents, which govern the scaling behavior and crossover phenomena, are computed to one-loop order. Abstract: We present a covariant field-theoretical framework for a rank-4 tensor gauge field theory describing fractonic string-like objects. In order to understand the physical meaning of this, we carefully identify the splitting in the effective supergravity between the graviphoton direction and matter vector multiplets. Abstract: We investigate the Casimir effect as a probe of Lorentz symmetry violation for a real scalar field confined to a rectangular waveguide with Dirichlet boundary conditions. The field dynamics is governed by a Lorentz-violating extension of the Klein-Gordon theory involving a fixed background four-vector $u_μ$. Focusing on four representative configurations in which the background is aligned with the temporal direction or with one of the spatial axes of the cavity, we derive the modified mode spectra and the corresponding vacuum energies. We show that these configurations induce anisotropic modifications of the dispersion relations that depend explicitly on the orientation of the background vector relative to the cavity geometry, while still preserving mode separability. The resulting Casimir energy acquires characteristic direction-dependent corrections that encode the breaking of Lorentz symmetry, without altering the universal functional structure of the spectral kernel. Our analysis provides a controlled and transparent framework for isolating Lorentz-violating effects in confined geometries and highlights Casimir systems as sensitive probes of anisotropic physics and fundamental spacetime symmetries.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索E₈格的构造方法，特别是通过有理椭圆曲面的代数几何结构与经典纠错码理论的结合，为已知的格构造（如Construction A和Construction A_C）提供李代数（Lie algebraic）扩展和进一步推广。

Method: 方法基于Oguiso-Shioda分类中所有具有秩8（最大）奇点格（singularity lattice）的有理椭圆曲面，利用Mordell-Weil格结构定理，当奇点格秩最大时，Mordell-Weil群是循环群或其直和，通过在其自然环上的码将这些奇点格粘合（glued together）形成E₈格。

Result: 成功构造了E₈格，这种从码构造E₈格的方法可视为已知码格构造（如Construction A和Construction A_C）的李代数扩展和进一步推广。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了代数几何中的有理椭圆曲面、Mordell-Weil群与经典纠错码理论之间的新联系，为E₈格的构造提供了新的代数几何-编码理论框架。

Abstract: We construct the $E_8$ lattice from classical error-correcting codes over the Mordell-Weil groups of rational elliptic surfaces that have a singularity lattice of rank 8 (maximal) for all cases of Oguiso-Shioda's classification. By the structure theorem of the Mordell-Weil lattice of rational elliptic surfaces, if the rank of the singularity lattice is maximal, then the Mordell-Weil group is a cyclic group or a direct sum of them. The singularity lattices are glued together by a code over their natural ring to form the $E_8$ lattice. Such constructions of the $E_8$ lattice from codes can be seen as a Lie algebraic extension and further generalization of known code lattice constructions such as Construction A and Construction A${}_{\rm C}$.

</details>


### [86] [WKB-asymptotics for multipoint Virasoro conformal blocks and applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08194)
*Aleksandr Artemev,Dmitry Khromov*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究球面上梳状通道的多点Virasoro共形块，旨在获得大中间维度下的渐近表达式，以扩展对共形块行为的理解，并为相关物理问题提供计算工具。

Method: 采用WKB方法求解"经典BPZ方程（classical BPZ equation）"，通过单值性方法（monodromy method）研究经典Virasoro共形块，从而推导出大中间维度下的渐近表达式。

Result: 获得了梳状通道多点Virasoro共形块在大中间维度下的渐近表达式，该结果通过了非平凡检验：与特殊情况下五点共形块的已知精确表达式一致，且与使用AGT对应关系计算的Virasoro共形块通常级数展开相符。

Conclusion: 推导的渐近表达式具有多个应用前景，包括推广Zamolodchikov椭圆递归关系和最小弦理论（minimal string theory）中振幅的数值计算，为相关领域提供了有效的计算工具。

Abstract: We study multipoint Virasoro conformal blocks on the sphere in the comb channel. We arrive at the asymptotic expression for these blocks at large intermediate dimensions, applying WKB method for "classical BPZ equation", which is used to study (classical) Virasoro blocks via monodromy method. Several applications of this asymptotic are discussed, such as the possibility to generalize Zamolodchikov's elliptic recursion and numerical evaluation of amplitudes in minimal string theory. Our expressions pass nontrivial checks, such as agreement with known exact expressions for 5-point blocks in special cases and the usual series expansion of Virasoro blocks computed using AGT correspondence.

### [87] [Transport properties of baryon rich back-reacted thermal plasma with finite 't Hooft coupling correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08250)
*Rishi Pokhrel,Karma P. Sherpa,Indra K. P. Chettri,Tanay K. Dey*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究采用全息方法分析具有有限't Hooft耦合修正的重子富集热等离子体的输运性质，重点考察了拖曳力、喷注淬火参数、屏蔽长度等物理量随不同参数的变化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析重子富集、具有有限't Hooft耦合修正的热等离子体的输运性质。这类系统在夸克-胶子等离子体物理中具有重要意义，需要理解其在高能重离子碰撞实验中的行为。

Method: 采用全息方法（holographic approach），构建了具有高阶导数Gauss-Bonnet修正和弦云（string cloud）的带电AdS黑洞作为对偶体几何。通过该框架研究了拖曳力、喷注淬火参数、屏蔽长度、径向分布和能量损失等物理量。

Result: 研究发现：拖曳力和喷注淬火参数随GB耦合、重子密度和味密度增加而增强；屏蔽长度随这些参数增加而减小。旋转夸克的径向分布随重子势、味密度、温度和角频率增加而减小，但随共轭动量和GB耦合增加而增强。夸克能量损失随势、味密度、速度和角频率增加而增大，但受GB耦合抑制。

Conclusion: 研究表明，高阶导数修正和弦云对重子富集热等离子体的输运性质有显著影响。GB耦合、重子密度和味密度等参数系统地改变了拖曳力、喷注淬火参数、屏蔽长度和能量损失等关键物理量，为理解夸克-胶子等离子体在高能重离子碰撞中的行为提供了理论洞见。

Abstract: In this work, holographic approach has been used to analyse the transport properties of baryon rich back-reacted thermal plasma with finite 't Hooft coupling correction. The dual bulk geometry is charged AdS black hole with higher derivative Gauss-Bonnet (GB) correction and string cloud. Specially, we have studied the nature of drag force, jet quenching parameter, screening length, radial profile and energy loss with respect to different parameters. The drag force and jet quenching parameter are enhanced with GB coupling, baryon and flavor density whereas the screening length reduces with these parameters. The radial profile and energy loss of the rotating quark has also been studied and it is observed that the radial profile decreases with increase in baryon potential and flavor density, temperature and angular frequency, whereas it is enhanced with conjugate momenta and GB coupling. Further, the energy loss of the quark grows with potential and flavor density, velocity and angular frequency and it is suppressed with GB coupling.

</details>

### [89] [Effects of fermions in one-loop propagators in the Curci-Ferrari-Delbourgo-Jarvis gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08460)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用CFDJ规范计算夸克传播子的单圈修正，使用红外安全的重整化方案（infrared-safe renormalization scheme），研究有限规范参数对QCD关联函数红外行为的影响。

Result: 发现耦合常数、胶子质量和规范参数在有限能量尺度以下冻结（freeze），证实了框架的红外稳定性；夸克修饰函数Z(p)在Landau规范和有限ξ情况下显示出凹凸性变化，表明非零规范可能更好地再现格点计算结果趋势。

Conclusion: CFDJ规范被确立为具有质量胶子的微扰QCD的可能红外安全设定候选；若与格点计算结果一致，可为未来研究夸克-胶子顶点（quark-gluon vertex）及相关可观测量提供基础。

Abstract: We present the one-loop computation of the quark propagator in the Curci-Ferrari-Delbourgo- Jarvis (CFDJ) gauge, extending previous analyses to include dynamical quarks. Using the infrared- safe renormalization scheme, we study how finite gauge parameters affect the infrared behavior of QCD correlation functions. The coupling, gluon mass, and gauge parameter are found to freeze below a finite energy scale, confirming the infrared stability of the framework. The quark dressing function Z(p) shows a change in concavity between the Landau and finite-ξ cases, suggesting that nonvanishing gauges may better reproduce lattice trends. These results establish the CFDJ gauge as a possible infrared-safe setting candidate for perturbative QCD with massive gluons. In the case of a consistency check from lattice calculations, it could provide a basis for future studies of the quark-gluon vertex and related observables.

### [90] [Gravitational formulation of stress-tensor deformed field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08481)
*Yunfei Xie,Yun-Ze Li,Lixin Xu,Song He*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过将种子量子场论（seed QFT）耦合到爱因斯坦引力（Einstein gravity）中，在度规鞍点（metric saddle）处计算引力路径积分，揭示了应力张量形变（stress-tensor deformations）的几何起源。研究发现，在固定参考背景附近，主导形变是普适的双局域项（bilocal term），其核由引力子格林函数（graviton Green's function）设定，而在鞍点度规上该流变为局域。论文还提供了两种构造性完备化方案，并应用于多个具体模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 应力张量形变通常暗示了涌现引力（emergent gravity）的几何起源，但在$d>2$维度下通常是非局域的。本文旨在通过将量子场论与引力耦合，探索这些形变的几何本质及其局域化机制。

Method: 将种子量子场论耦合到爱因斯坦引力，形变参数为$λ$，在度规鞍点处计算引力路径积分。在固定参考背景附近展开分析，并提供了两种构造性完备化方案：Palatini $f(R)$引力和基于里奇（Ricci-based theories）的一般理论的特征值方法。

Result: 主导形变是普适的双局域项，二次于应力张量，其核由引力子格林函数设定，并包含系统的高阶展开。在鞍点度规上，该流变为局域。具体应用包括：任意维度$d$的标量广义Nambu-Goto和$\det T$形变，二维多标量ModMax和Born-Infeld模型，以及四维Maxwell理论的root-$T\bar T$和$T\bar T$流，后者产生了ModMax和Born-Infeld电动力学。在自由场论中，离壳分析进一步显示主导量子修正生成了爱因斯坦-希尔伯特项（Einstein-Hilbert term）及受控的高阶导数项。

Conclusion: 应力张量形变具有几何起源，通过引力耦合和鞍点近似可使其局域化。论文提供的构造性方法能够系统地处理各种具体模型，并揭示了量子修正如何生成引力作用量项，为涌现引力的研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: Stress-tensor deformations suggest a geometric origin of emergent gravity but are typically non-local for $d>2$. We couple a seed QFT to Einstein gravity with deformation parameter $λ$ and evaluate the gravitational path integral at the metric saddle. Around a fixed reference background, the leading deformation is universal: a bilocal term quadratic in the stress tensor with kernel set by the graviton Green's function, plus a systematic higher-order expansion. Expressed on the saddle-point (deformed) metric, the flow becomes local. We then provide two constructive completions on deformed backgrounds--Palatini $f(R)$ gravity and an eigenvalue method for general Ricci-based theories--and apply them to scalar generalized Nambu-Goto and $\det T$ deformations (arbitrary $d$), two-dimensional multi-scalar ModMax and Born-Infeld models, and four-dimensional root-$T\bar T$ and $T\bar T$ flows of Maxwell theory yielding ModMax and Born-Infeld electrodynamics. In free field theory, an off-shell analysis further shows that the leading quantum correction generates an Einstein-Hilbert term with controlled higher-derivative terms.

</details>


### [91] [Parity-dependent Casimir forces and Hall currents for a confined Dirac field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08601)
*Aitor Fernández,César D. Fosco*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了d+1维空间中狄拉克场在两种不同边界条件下的卡西米尔效应，对称配置产生吸引力而反对称配置产生排斥力，并分析了相关的电流关联和诱导霍尔电流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究质量为零的狄拉克场（massless Dirac field）在平行薄壁上的两种边界条件配置，探讨反射对称性对卡西米尔效应符号的影响，并分析真空涨落相关的物理现象。

Method: 在d+1维空间中，对狄拉克场施加两种不同的边界条件：关于两壁中间平面对称的偶（对称）配置和反对称的奇（反对称）配置，研究由此产生的卡西米尔力、壁面电流关联以及外部电场下的诱导体电流。

Result: 对称配置产生吸引性卡西米尔力（attractive Casimir force），而反对称配置产生排斥力，这与连接宇称（parity）与费米子卡西米尔效应符号的一般定理一致。在2+1维中，外部电场会诱导出横向（霍尔型）电流，其空间分布继承了约束势的对称性。

Conclusion: 边界条件的宇称对称性对狄拉克场的卡西米尔效应有决定性影响，对称与反对称配置分别导致吸引和排斥行为。真空涨落相关的电流现象同样对宇称敏感，在低维系统中可诱导出具有特定对称性的霍尔型电流。

Abstract: We study a massless Dirac field subjected to two alternative boundary conditions on two parallel thin walls, in d + 1 dimensions. The two configurations correspond to the system being even or odd under reflection about the midplane between the two walls, and lead to qualitatively different behaviors. The even (symmetric) configuration produces an attractive Casimir force, whereas the odd (antisymmetric) one yields repulsion, in agreement with a general theorem linking parity to the sign of the fermionic Casimir effect. We complement this result by studying two phenomena associated with the vacuum fluctuations responsible for the Casimir interaction, both of which are also sensitive to parity: the correlation between currents concentrated on the walls, and the induced bulk current under the influence of an external electric field. For the latter we show that, in 2 + 1 dimensions, an induced transverse (Hall-like) current arises, whose spatial profile inherits the symmetry of the confining potential.

</details>


### [92] [Cluster Bootstrap for Cosmological Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08670)
*Shruti Paranjape,Marcos Skowronek,Marcus Spradlin,Anastasia Volovich,He-Chen Weng*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在德西特（de Sitter）时空中，与n-点链图和环图相关的宇宙学波函数系数具有由A_{2n-2}和B_{2n-1}簇变量子集构成的符号字母表，并满足相应的簇邻接性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索宇宙学波函数系数（cosmological wavefunction coefficients）的数学结构，特别是其在德西特时空中的代数性质。该研究旨在建立图论组合学与簇代数（cluster algebra）之间的精确联系。

Method: 方法的核心是识别图"管道（tubings）"与多边形"三角剖分（triangulations）"之间的精确联系，前者出现在运动学流方程中，后者编码了簇相容性的组合学。通过这一联系证明波函数系数满足簇邻接性质。

Result: 主要结果表明：1) 立方标量理论的宇宙学波函数系数具有A_{2n-2}和B_{2n-1}簇变量子集的符号字母表；2) 在一般幂律FRW宇宙学中，这些系数在ε展开的所有阶都满足簇邻接；3) 对于n≤4的情况，德西特符号可由简单的物理约束唯一确定。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了宇宙学波函数系数与簇代数结构之间的深刻联系，证明了其在德西特时空中的簇邻接性质。这一发现为通过自举方法（bootstrap approach）确定波函数系数提供了新的数学框架和约束条件。

Abstract: We show that cosmological wavefunction coefficients associated with $n$-site chain and loop graphs for a cubic scalar theory in de Sitter spacetime have symbol alphabets given by subsets of $A_{2n{-}2}$ and $B_{2n{-}1}$ cluster variables, respectively, and satisfy the associated cluster adjacency properties. The key step in proving this is identifying a precise connection between graph "tubings" that appear in the kinematic flow equation and polygon "triangulations" that encode the combinatorics of cluster compatibility. Our results imply that cosmological wavefunction coefficients in a general power-law FRW cosmology satisfy cluster adjacency to all orders in the $ε$ expansion. We use this information as bootstrap input to show that de Sitter symbols for $n \leq 4$ are uniquely determined by simple physical constraints.

</details>


### [93] [A proof of conservation laws in gravitational scattering: tails and breaking of peeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08705)
*Geoffrey Compère,Sébastien Robert*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种与零无穷远（null infinity）相容的渐近平坦时空（asymptotically flat spacetime）定义，并证明了三个在空间无穷远（spatial infinity）处的反极匹配条件（antipodal matching conditions），这些条件可重新表述为空间无穷远边界双曲面上的渐近守恒定律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在提出一个与零无穷远相容的渐近平坦时空定义，该定义需要兼容引力散射（gravitational scattering）、进出辐射以及物质相互作用的已知性质，从而为研究时空的渐近结构提供更一致的框架。

Method: 作者首先提出了一类渐近平坦时空的定义，然后针对这类时空证明了三个在空间无穷远处的反极匹配条件：一个针对所谓的对偶质量方面（dual mass aspect），一个针对剪切（shear）的主导尾部，另一个将时空在过去和零无穷远处的剥离性质（peeling properties）与空间无穷远的主导尾部和质量方面非平凡地联系起来。

Result: 本文证明了三个反极匹配条件，并将这些恒等式重新表述为定义在空间无穷远边界双曲面（boundary hyperboloid）上的渐近守恒定律（asymptotic conservation laws），从而建立了不同无穷远区域之间的数学联系。

Conclusion: 提出的渐近平坦时空定义与零无穷远相容，且证明的反极匹配条件揭示了时空在不同无穷远区域之间的深层联系，这些结果可表述为边界上的渐近守恒定律，为理解引力系统的渐近结构提供了重要工具。

Abstract: We propose a definition of asymptotically flat spacetimes that is consistent with both null infinities and compatible with known properties of gravitational scattering, incoming and outgoing radiation, and interactions with matter. For this class of spacetimes, we prove three antipodal matching conditions at spatial infinity: one for the so-called dual mass aspect, one for the leading tail of the shear, and one that non-trivially relates the peeling properties of the spacetime at past and null infinities to the leading tail and mass aspect at spatial infinity. Furthermore, we reformulate these identities as asymptotic conservation laws defined on the boundary hyperboloid at spatial infinity.

</details>

### [94] [GNN For Muon Particle Momentum estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06675)
*Vishak K Bhat,Eric A. F. Reinhardt,Sergei Gleyzer*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在大型强子对撞机（LHC）的CMS实验中，使用图神经网络（GNN）进行动量估计，以改进触发系统效率。研究显示GNN在平均绝对误差（MAE）上优于传统模型如TabNet，并证明节点特征维度对GNN效率至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider）的CMS实验中，由于感兴趣数据生成率相对较低，需要结合硬件和软件触发器来选择捕获数据。精确的动量计算对于提高CMS触发系统效率、更好分类低动量和高动量粒子以及减少误触发至关重要。

Method: 本文探索了使用图神经网络（Graph Neural Networks, GNNs）进行动量估计任务。提出了两种图构建方法，并应用GNN模型来利用数据固有的图结构。

Result: 首先，研究显示GNN在平均绝对误差（Mean Absolute Error, MAE）方面优于传统模型如TabNet，证明了其在捕捉数据内复杂依赖关系方面的有效性。其次，研究表明节点特征维度对GNN的效率至关重要。

Conclusion: 图神经网络在CMS实验的动量估计任务中表现出优越性能，特别是在捕捉复杂数据依赖关系方面，同时节点特征维度的优化对模型效率有重要影响。

Abstract: Due to a high rate of overall data generation relative to data generation of interest, the CMS experiment at the Large Hadron Collider uses a combination of hardware- and software-based triggers to select data for capture. Accurate momentum calculation is crucial for improving the efficiency of the CMS trigger systems, enabling better classification of low- and high- momentum particles and reducing false triggers. This paper explores the use of Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) for the momentum estimation task. We present two graph construction methods and apply a GNN model to leverage the inherent graph structure of the data. In this paper firstly, we show that the GNN outperforms traditional models like TabNet in terms of Mean Absolute Error (MAE), demonstrating its effectiveness in capturing complex dependencies within the data. Secondly we show that the dimension of the node feature is crucial for the efficiency of GNN.

### [95] [Learning the Standard Model Manifold: Bayesian Latent Diffusion for Collider Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06754)
*Jigar Patel,Tommaso Dorigo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为高能物理（high-energy physics）中新物理（new Physics）搜索构建可靠的异常检测方法，需要同时考虑不确定性估计和物理一致性。现有方法在结合物理约束与灵活密度估计方面存在挑战。

Result: 在模拟LHC喷注数据（LHC jet data）上训练和测试模型，使用种子平均ROC曲线（seed-averaged ROC curves）和面向发现的度量进行评估。消融研究（ablation studies）表明扩散过程、贝叶斯正则化和物理驱动的损失项以互补方式贡献，有助于稳定训练并改善泛化能力。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了在高能物理新物理搜索中构建可靠异常检测方法时，同时纳入不确定性估计和物理一致性的重要性。即使峰值性能提升有限，这些组件也能显著改善训练稳定性和泛化能力。

Abstract: We propose a physics-informed anomaly detection framework for collider data based on a Bayesian latent diffusion model. Our method combines a probabilistic encoder with diffusion dynamics in the latent space, allowing for stable and flexible density estimation while explicitly enforcing physics constraints, such as mass decorrelation and regularization of latent correlations. We train and test the model on simulated LHC jet data and evaluate its performance using seed-averaged ROC curves together with discovery-oriented metrics. Through a series of ablation studies, we show that the diffusion process, Bayesian regularization, and physics-motivated loss terms each contribute in a complementary way: they help stabilize training and improve generalization, even when the gains in peak performance are moderate. Overall, our results emphasize the importance of incorporating both uncertainty estimates and physics consistency when building reliable anomaly detection methods for new Physics searches in high-energy physics.

Result: 文章总结了Weil-Petersson体积和Masur-Veech体积计算领域的主要研究成果。这些计算促进了多个数学分支的发展，并揭示了两种不同类型模空间体积计算之间的深刻联系。

Conclusion: 本文系统回顾了Weil-Petersson体积和Masur-Veech体积的计算研究，总结了现有成果、方法学进展以及未解决问题。特别强调了两种体积计算方法中出现的平行相似性，为进一步研究提供了框架。

Abstract: Weil-Petersson and Masur-Veech volumes measure the sizes of moduli spaces of Riemann surfaces equipped with hyperbolic and flat metrics, respectively. Over the past several decades, the computation of these volumes has inspired remarkable developments in combinatorial enumeration, intersection theory, and recursion relations. In this survey, we review key results, methods, open problems, as well as interesting parallels that emerge in the approaches to computing both types of volumes.

### [97] [Minority-Triggered Reorientations Yield Macroscopic Cascades and Enhanced Responsiveness in Swarms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07254)
*Simon Syga,Chandraniva Guha Ray,Josué Manik Nava-Sedeño,Fernando Peruani,Andreas Deutsch*

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于少数触发转向规则的集体运动机制，该机制能够在保持群体凝聚力的同时显著增强集体响应性，通过局部方向线索引发放大的群体级转向，产生重尾转向级联和临界类波动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动物和细胞集体运动常表现出快速转向和无标度速度相关性，这使信息能在群体中快速传播，从而对环境变化和捕食者威胁做出适当的集体响应。传统集群模型难以解释这一现象。

Method: 引入一种简单且生物学合理的机制：少数触发转向规则（minority-triggered reorientation rule）。当局部有序度高时，个体会偶尔跟随强烈偏离的邻居而非多数方向，这一规则与传统集群模型有本质区别。

Result: 该机制在广泛参数范围内产生重尾转向级联（heavy-tailed cascades of reorientations），在保持群体凝聚力的同时显著增强集体响应性，因为局部方向线索能引发放大的群体级转向。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种简约且生物学可解释的路径，用于解释集群运动中的临界类波动（critical-like fluctuations）和高响应性，为理解集体运动中的信息传播机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: Collective motion in animals and cells often exhibits rapid reorientations and scale-free velocity correlations. This allows information to spread rapidly through the group, allowing an adequate collective response to environmental changes and threats such as predators. To explain this phenomenon, we introduce a simple, biologically plausible mechanism: a minority-triggered reorientation rule. When local order is high, agents sometimes follow a strongly deviating neighbor instead of the majority. This rule qualitatively changes the macroscopic system behavior compared to traditional flocking models, as it generates heavy-tailed cascades of reorientations over broad parameter ranges. Our mechanism preserves cohesion while markedly enhancing collective responsiveness because localized directional cues elicit amplified group-level reorientation. Our results provide a parsimonious, biologically interpretable route to critical-like fluctuations and high responsiveness during flocking.

Abstract: A mesoscopic grain-envelope model applying a phase-field front-propagation method is developed to simulate grain growth under additive manufacturing process conditions. The envelope represents the outer surface of dendritic grains through a diffuse interface. While a modified heat-conduction model that incorporates moving heat sources and latent-heat release provides the evolution of local thermal field. Envelope propagation is determined from microscopic-solvability-based kinetic law. The model is validated through two- and three-dimensional simulations and subsequently applied to examine the influence of material and process parameters on microstructure evolution. The results demonstrate that the proposed mesoscopic model offers an efficient and predictive approach for modeling grain growth during multi-pass and multi-layer build-up in additive manufacturing.

### [99] [Collapse of Jahn-Teller Phonons in La$_{1-x}$Sr$_{x}$MnO$_3$ with Weak Magnetoresistance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06708)
*Tyler C. Sterling,Andrei T. Savici,Ryoichi Kajimoto,Kazuhiko Ikeuchi,Nazir Khan,Frank Weber,Dmitry Reznik*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过高分辨率中子散射和密度泛函理论，揭示了钙钛矿锰酸盐中巨磁阻（CMR）与电子-声子耦合（EPC）的复杂关系，发现Jahn-Teller活性氧振动在居里温度以上完全崩溃，表明巨磁阻大小与扩散速率而非EPC强度相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钙钛矿锰酸盐（perovskite manganites）作为量子材料表现出巨磁阻效应，传统理论强调电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）的关键作用，但越来越多的证据表明其机制更为复杂。本研究旨在探究具有较小巨磁阻的La₁₋ₓSrₓMnO₃（x=0.2,0.3）中的声子和自旋-声子耦合机制。

Method: 采用高分辨率中子散射实验（high-resolution neutron scattering experiments）结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）分析，研究铁磁相和顺磁相中的声子行为和磁振子（magnons）色散关系。

Result: 低温铁磁相表现常规特性：声子散射与DFT预测一致，磁振子遵循正弦色散。高温顺磁相中，尽管巨磁阻较小，Jahn-Teller活性（Jahn-Teller-active）光学氧振动在居里温度以上完全崩溃，部分谱权重以准弹性散射形式重新出现。

Conclusion: 研究将这种异常行为归因于电荷和/或轨道通道中的巨电子-声子耦合，驱动了准静态载流子俘获氧亚晶格畸变的协同扩散运动。假设巨磁阻大小与扩散速率而非Jahn-Teller电子-声子耦合强度相关。

Abstract: Perovskite manganites are quantum materials exhibiting competing interactions inducing colossal magnetoresistance (CMR). The prevailing theory of CMR highlights the essential role of electron-phonon coupling (EPC), but mounting evidence suggests the underlying mechanism is more complicated. Here, we investigate phonons and spin-phonon coupling in ferromagnetic CMR manganites La$_{1-x}$Sr$_x$MnO$_3$ ($x$=0.2,0.3) with relatively small CMR associated with melting of the magnetic order above room temperature. High-resolution neutron scattering experiments combined with density functional theory (DFT) show that the low-temperature ferromagnetic phase is conventional: neutron scattering from phonons agrees with DFT predictions and magnons follow sinusoidal dispersions. Fluctuating magnetic moments and low-energy phonons remain conventional in the high temperature paramagnetic phase, indicating the Mn and La/Sr sublattices are not strongly perturbed by melting of ferromagnetism. In contrast, the Jahn-Teller-active optical oxygen vibrations collapse entirely above the Curie temperature, despite low CMR in these compositions, with some of the lost spectral weight reappearing as quasielastic scattering. We attribute this highly anomalous behavior to giant EPC in the charge and/or orbital channel. It drives cooperative diffusive motion of quasistatic carrier-trapping oxygen sublattice distortions once ferromagnetism disappears. We hypothesize the magnitude of magnetoresistance correlates with the rate of diffusion rather than with the strength of Jahn-Teller EPC.

### [100] [Effect of Exchange-Correlation Functionals on Schottky Barriers at Si/Metal Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06725)
*Viviana Dovale-Farelo,Kamal Choudhary*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究系统评估了肖特基势垒高度（SBH）预测的计算策略，以Si(111)/金属界面为测试案例，发现结构-静电一致性是关键因素，混合杂化-半局域方法结合应变参考协议可获得接近实验精度的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确预测金属-半导体（M-SC）界面的肖特基势垒高度（SBH）对于理解和优化电子与光电器件中的电荷注入至关重要。然而，由于半导体带隙低估、金属费米能级定位、晶格失配、相对几何对准以及异质界面静电势对准等多重困难，SBH的第一性原理计算仍具挑战性。

Method: 研究采用Si(111)/金属（Al、Cu、Ag、Au）界面作为代表性测试案例，系统评估了多种交换关联（XC）处理方法，并结合三种不同的体相参考协议：弛豫体相、含自旋轨道耦合的弛豫体相、以及与界面几何一致的应变体相参考。

Result: 通过与实验数据基准测试，研究表明界面与体相参考计算之间的结构和静电一致性是决定SBH精度的主导因素。混合杂化-半局域（mixed hybrid-semilocal）方法结合应变参考协议可获得一致为正且显著改善的SBH，在保持计算成本与预测性能良好平衡的同时达到接近实验的精度。

Conclusion: 该研究为可靠的肖特基势垒预测建立了清晰且可迁移的方法论，并为大规模筛选和界面工程提供了实用指导。研究结果表明，结构-静电一致性的物理基础是获得准确SBH预测的关键。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of Schottky barrier heights (SBHs) at metal-semiconductor (M-SC) interfaces is essential for understanding and optimizing charge injection in electronic and optoelectronic devices. However, first-principles calculations of SBHs remain challenging due to the combined difficulties of semiconductor bandgap underestimation, metal Fermi level placement, lattice-mismatch, relative geometric alignment and electrostatic potential alignment across heterogeneous interfaces. In this work, we present a systematic and physically grounded assessment of computational strategies for SBH prediction using Si(111)/Metal (Al, Cu, Ag, Au) interfaces as representative test cases. We evaluate multiple exchange-correlation (XC) treatments, in combination with three distinct bulk reference protocols: relaxed bulk, relaxed bulk with spin-orbit coupling, and strained bulk references consistent with the interface geometry. By benchmarking against experimental data, we demonstrate that structural and electrostatic consistency between interface and bulk reference calculations is the dominant factor governing SBH accuracy. We show that mixed hybrid-semilocal approaches combined with strained reference protocols yield uniformly positive and significantly improved SBHs, achieving near-experimental accuracy while maintaining a favorable balance between computational cost and predictive performance. Our results establish a clear and transferable methodology for reliable Schottky barrier prediction and provide practical guidance for large-scale screening and interface engineering.

### [101] [Patterns of load, elastic energy and damage in network models of architected composite materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06744)
*Christian Greff,Leon Pyka,Michael Zaiser,Paolo Moretti*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 分层图案化结构设计比梯度结构更有效，能同时实现界面失效控制与韧性提升，为复合材料界面工程提供了新的设计策略。

Abstract: We investigate the role of architected thin films in the interfacial failure properties of bi-layer composites. Our results show that, while graded structures can be used to prescribe failure at the interface, they do not offer significant advantages in terms of fracture toughness. Hierarchically patterned layers can localize failure at the interface and simultaneously enhance interface toughness, by enforcing a buffer region where elastic energy is dissipated in the form of diffuse damage, so that no stress concentration can drive crack growth. To analyze these mechanisms, the associated patterns of local load redistribution and the soft deformation modes, we develop a network formalism that brings together concepts of discrete differential geometry and spectral graph theory.

### [102] [Bridging the lab-to-fab gap in non-fullerene organic solar cells via gravure printing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06827)
*Svitlana Taranenko,Chen Wang,David Holzner,Robert Eland,Christopher Wöpke,Toni Seiler,Alexander Ehm,Fabio Le Piane,Roderick C. I. Mackenzie,Dietrich R. T. Zahn,Carsten Deibel,Arved Carl Hübler,Maria Saladina*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究报道了全卷对卷兼容凹版印刷非富勒烯有机太阳能电池的最高效率，建立了定量框架分析印刷器件中的光学、复合和传输损失，发现实验室与印刷电池间的性能差距主要源于器件架构而非非富勒烯系统的本征物理限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非富勒烯有机太阳能电池（non-fullerene organic solar cells）已达到创纪录效率，但其向工业印刷的转化仍是关键瓶颈。实验室优化条件与卷对卷（roll-to-roll）制造在油墨稳定性、干燥动力学和多层集成方面存在根本差异，这些限制是否本质上制约器件物理性能尚未解决。

Method: 研究采用商用材料构建凹版印刷（gravure-printed）PM6:Y12太阳能电池架构，建立定量框架以区分印刷器件中的光学损失（optical losses）、复合损失（recombination losses）和传输损失（transport losses）。

Result: 研究发现有利的体相形态（bulk morphology）和激子收集（exciton harvesting）在凹版印刷和非卤化溶剂（non-halogenated solvents）条件下得以保持。主要效率损失源于印刷层堆叠内的光学干涉（optical interference）和缓慢的电荷传输（charge transport）。

Conclusion: 实验室与印刷太阳能电池间的性能差距源于器件架构而非现代非富勒烯系统的本征物理限制，为卷对卷制造非富勒烯太阳能电池提供了机理路线图（mechanistic roadmap）。

Abstract: Organic solar cells have reached record efficiencies with non-fullerene acceptors, yet their translation to industrial printing remains a critical bottleneck. Here we report the highest efficiency achieved for a fully roll-to-roll-compatible gravure-printed non-fullerene organic solar cell. High-performance blends are typically optimised under laboratory coating conditions, while roll-to-roll manufacturing imposes fundamentally different constraints on ink stability, drying dynamics, and multilayer integration. Whether these constraints intrinsically limit device physics has remained unresolved. Here, we demonstrate a gravure-printed PM6:Y12 solar cell architecture using commercially available materials and establish a quantitative framework that disentangles optical, recombination, and transport losses in printed devices. We find that favourable bulk morphology and exciton harvesting can be preserved under gravure printing and non-halogenated solvents. The dominant efficiency penalties arise instead from optical interference within the printed layer stack and slow charge transport. Abstract: The III-Se layered semiconductors, including InSe and GaSe, are promising optoelectronic materials due to their relatively high electron mobilities at room temperature, nonlinear optical responses, ferroelectricity, self-passivated van der Waals surfaces, and ability to alloy and synthesize heterostructures for bandgap engineering. ### [106] [Universal electronic manifolds for extrapolative alloy discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06953)
*Pranoy Ray,Sayan Bhowmik,Phanish Suryanarayana,Surya R. Kalidindi,Andrew J. Medford*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于非相互作用电子密度（non-interacting electron density）的计算高效框架，用于加速难熔高熵合金（refractory high-entropy alloys）的发现。该方法通过方向解析两点空间相关性和主成分分析提取物理特征，结合贝叶斯主动学习，仅需少量训练样本即可实现高精度性能预测和跨化学组分的可迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于自洽密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算的方法成本高昂，限制了合金设计空间的探索效率。本研究旨在开发一种计算高效的框架，利用非相互作用电子密度作为结构描述符，以加速难熔高熵合金的发现过程。

Method: 该方法采用非相互作用电子密度作为主要结构描述符，通过方向解析两点空间相关性（directionally resolved two-point spatial correlations）提取物理特征，并使用主成分分析（Principal Component Analysis）进行特征压缩。将所得描述符与贝叶斯主动学习（Bayesian active learning）相结合，构建预测模型。

Result: 对于Al-Nb-Ti-Zr合金体系，仅使用10个训练样本即可获得体模量（bulk modulus）的归一化平均绝对误差（normalized mean absolute error）低于2%。模型学习到的电子堆积流形（electronic packing manifold）在难熔高熵合金的不同化学组分间具有可迁移性。在完全未出现在训练数据中的7组分难熔体系（Mo-Nb-Ta-Ti-V-W-Zr）上，框架实现了严格的零样本外推（zero-shot extrapolation）。通过在目标域仅增加20个样本，对7组分合金的预测误差可降至3%以下，相比标准工作流程大幅降低了数据获取成本。

Conclusion: 非相互作用电子密度被确立为一种严格且具有外推能力（extrapolative）的描述符，适用于广阔的合金成分空间。该框架为加速合金发现提供了计算高效的方法，显著降低了数据获取成本，并展示了跨化学组分的良好可迁移性。

Abstract: This study presents a computationally efficient framework for accelerated alloy discovery that uses the non-interacting electron density to capture intrinsic structure-property relationships in refractory high-entropy alloys (HEAs). Unlike state-of-the-art approaches relying on expensive, self-consistent density functional theory calculations, our method employs the non-interacting electron density as the primary structural descriptor. By extracting physical features through directionally resolved two-point spatial correlations and compressing them via Principal Component Analysis, we efficiently map the design space. Coupling these descriptors with Bayesian active learning, we achieve a normalized mean absolute error (NMAE) of <2% for the bulk modulus of Al-Nb-Ti-Zr alloys using only 10 training samples. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the model learns an electronic packing manifold that is transferable across distinct chemical species within refractory HEAs. Validated on a distinct 7-component refractory system (Mo-Nb-Ta-Ti-V-W-Zr) containing four elements entirely absent from the training data, the framework enables rigorous zero-shot extrapolation. Moreover, by augmenting the base model with just 20 samples from the target domain, we achieve high-fidelity predictions (NMAE < 3%) for 7-component alloys, reducing data acquisition costs by orders of magnitude compared to standard workflows. These results establish the non-interacting electron density as a rigorous, extrapolative descriptor for vast compositional landscapes.

### [107] [Exotic Cooperative Quantum Optics of Moire Exciton Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06998)
*Haowei Xu,Wang Yao,Ju Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了二维莫尔（moiré）系统中莫尔激子（moiré excitons）形成的超晶格（superlattice）能够产生独特的合作光学响应，包括超辐射（superradiant）和亚辐射（subradiant）态的可控切换，以及通过微小应变或转角调整实现透射率从几乎不透明到几乎透明的巨大变化。

  <summary>Details</summary>
