### [169] [Bias in Local Spin Measurements from Deformed Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08618)
*Michele Arzano,Goffredo Chirco,Jerzy Kowalski-Glikman*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了当旋转对称性由量子群（quantum group）而非普通李群描述时，双粒子自旋单态关联的变化。研究发现，虽然单自旋可观测量与未变形理论相同，但非平凡余积（coproduct）重塑了"总"对称性概念，并导致贝尔单态（Bell singlet state）的变形类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索量子群对称性（quantum group symmetry）对双粒子自旋单态关联的影响。传统旋转对称性由李群描述，而量子群提供了更一般的对称性框架，需要理解在这种变形对称性下量子关联的性质变化。

Method: 研究方法包括：分析量子群对称性下的自旋单态可观测量；比较传统张量因子可观测量（conventional tensor-factor observables）与对称协变的R矩阵修饰嵌入（symmetry-covariant, R-matrix-dressed embedding）两种局部测量方案；通过数学推导展示两种方案对关联统计的不同影响。

Result: 主要结果发现：使用传统张量因子可观测量时，完美反关联（perfect anticorrelation）得以保持，但单点结果统计变得依赖于变形参数且存在偏差（biased）。而采用对称协变的R矩阵修饰嵌入方案时，既能恢复无偏统计（unbiased statistics），又能维持完美反关联。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在量子群对称性设定下，严格的张量因子局域性（strict tensor-factor locality）在对称性下不稳定，必须被编织局域性（braided notion of locality）取代，以构建一致的局部测量理论。

Abstract: We study bipartite spin-singlet correlations when rotational symmetry is described by a quantum group rather than an ordinary Lie group. We show that, even though the single-spin observables act as in the undeformed theory, the non-trivial coproduct reshapes the notion of "total" symmetry and leads to a deformed analogue of the Bell singlet state. We show that implementing local measurements with the conventional tensor-factor observables yields a striking effect: perfect anticorrelation is preserved, yet the one-site outcome statistics become deformation-dependent and biased. Using instead the symmetry-covariant, R-matrix-dressed embedding of local observables restores unbiased statistics while maintaining perfect anticorrelation. Our results demonstrate that, in a quantum group symmetry setting, strict tensor-factor locality is not stable under the symmetry and must be replaced by a braided notion of locality to formulate consistent local measurements.

### [170] [Efficient construction of time-invariant process tensors for simulating high-dimensional non-Markovian open quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06840)
*Émile Cochin,Jonathan Keeling,Brendon W. Lovett,Alex W. Chin*

Main category: quant-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于具有时间平移不变性的过程张量（process tensor）矩阵乘积算符（MPO）表示，提出改进的无限时间演化块解耦（iTEBD）算法。通过引入中间压缩步骤，优化计算过程，显著降低系统尺寸相关的计算复杂度和内存需求。

Here, we propose a new algorithm for computing process tensors--matrix product operator (MPO) representations that capture the environment influence--which achieves greatly enhanced computational scalings with system size, while maintaining linear scaling with simulation length. We build on recent developments in the field which allow for long-time evolutions through process tensors which have a time-translational invariance. These can be built for general Gaussian environments and generic coupling operators with the system using infinite time-evolving block decimation (iTEBD). We introduce a modified iTEBD algorithm using intermediate compression steps which bring down the computation time scaling with system size $d$ from $\mathcal{O}(d^8)$ to $\mathcal{O}(d^4)$, as well as significantly lowering the required memory. To illustrate the power of this method, we apply it to the problem of dispersive qubit readout in circuit QED, which was previously out-of-reach numerically. The full treatment of the measurement resonator, which requires a large system space, combined with the long simulation times precipitated by the separation of timescales between the measurement drive and the environment dissipation, is now possible. The algorithm we introduce not only allows for capturing non-Markovian dynamics in large open quantum systems, but also further extends all the existing capabilities of process tensors, for example in quantum optimal control, or in computation of multi-time correlations or of steady states, to more complex systems with tens of levels.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用半经典Husimi动力学结合详细的相空间稳定性分析，研究非厄米模型的半经典极限下的局域化行为。

Result: 非厄米模型中局域化转变在半经典极限下依然存在，但经典相空间分析推断的转变点与量子临界点不一致。半经典转变对定义准周期势的无理参数选择敏感，表明非厄米体系中缺乏普适的经典-量子对应关系。

Abstract: The localization transition in the Hermitian Aubry-André model is known to have a clear classical origin, with the critical point being exactly predictable from an analysis of classical phase-space trajectories. Motivated by this correspondence, we investigate whether a similar classical origin exists for localization transitions in non-Hermitian quasiperiodic Hamiltonians. Using semiclassical Husimi dynamics together with a detailed phase-space stability analysis, we show that localization transitions persist even in the semiclassical limit of such non-Hermitian models. However, in sharp contrast to the Hermitian Aubry-André case, the transition point inferred from classical phase-space analysis does not coincide with the quantum critical point. Instead, we find that the semiclassical transition depends sensitively on the choice of the irrational parameter defining the quasiperiodic potential, indicating the absence of a universal classical-quantum correspondence for the localization transition in the non-Hermitian setting. Nonetheless, we identify a suitable parameter regime in which the classical dynamics can faithfully mimic the quantum dynamics over a finite but appreciable time window.

### [174] [Lindbladian Learning with Neural Differential Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07778)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从测量数据推断多体量子系统的动力学生成元对于量子处理器的验证、校准和控制至关重要。开放系统比纯幺正情况更具挑战性，因为相干和耗散机制可能产生相似的测量统计，且长时间数据对相干耦合不敏感。

Method: 采用最大似然方法处理多个实验友好的瞬态时间点的泡利测量，利用瞬态动力学的丰富信息。通过神经微分方程项增强物理模型，在训练过程中逐步移除该项以蒸馏出可解释的林德布拉德解。

Result: 该方法可靠地学习了中性原子（具有二维连接性）和超导哈密顿量，以及自旋-1/2链上的海森堡XYZ和PXP模型的开放系统动力学。对于耗散部分，展示了在相位噪声、热噪声及其组合上的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Inferring the dynamical generator of a many-body quantum system from measurement data is essential for the verification, calibration, and control of quantum processors. When the system is open, this task becomes considerably harder than in the purely unitary case, because coherent and dissipative mechanisms can produce similar measurement statistics and long-time data can be insensitive to coherent couplings. Here we tackle this so-called Lindbladian learning problem of open-system characterisation with maximum-likelihood on Pauli measurements at multiple experimentally friendly \emph{transient} times, exploiting the richer information content of transient dynamics. To navigate the resulting non-convex likelihood loss-landscape, we augment the physical model neural differential-equation term, which is progressively removed during training to distil an interpretable Lindbladian solution. Our method reliably learns open-system dynamics across neutral-atom (with 2D connectivity) and superconducting Hamiltonians, as well as the Heisenberg XYZ, and PXP models on a spin-1/2 chain. For the dissipative part, we show robustness over phase noise, thermal noise, and their combination. Our algorithm can robustly infer these dissipative systems over noise-to-signal ratios spanning four orders of magnitude, and system sizes up to $N=6$ qubits with fewer than $5 \times 10^5$ shots.

Abstract: A higher-order Suzuki-Trotter decomposition or Trotterization can be exploited to mitigate the Trotter error in digital quantum simulation. While the work presents a pedagogical way to exploit a real quantum computer, the effectiveness of the symmetric Trotterization is evaluated in a prototype superconducting quantum device on IBM Quantum Experience. It turns out that the symmetric Trotterization does not provide higher accuracy than the first-order Trotterization in the testbed using the transverse-field Ising model. The result indicates that apart from the quantum errors, such as logical gate error and readout error, the use of a higher-order Trotterization should be circumspect, and the Trotter error would play an insignificant role in particular applications in an early stage of realized noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) devices.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 球面蚱蜢问题是一个几何优化问题，起源于贝尔不等式（Bell inequalities）的研究。其物理意义在于，为沿随机轴（random axes）测量且具有固定夹角的量子单态关联（quantum singlet correlations）寻找最佳的局域隐变量（local hidden variable）近似。

Method: 论文详细描述了支撑数值结果的几何与计算框架。方法包括：考察球面离散化（spherical discretization）的作用；比较问题的三种自然变体：对映互补草坪（antipodal complementary lawns）、对映独立草坪（antipodal independent lawns）和非对映互补草坪（non-antipodal complementary lawns）；并分析相应最优草坪构型的几何结构。

Result: 分析揭示了最优草坪构型的几何结构，并通过球谐函数展开（spherical harmonics expansion）进行了解释。研究还探讨了该问题与其他物理模型以及几何概率（geometric probability）中经典问题的联系。

Conclusion: 该论文作为先前数值研究工作的补充，系统阐述了球面蚱蜢问题的理论基础与几何框架，为理解其在单态模拟（singlet simulation）和测试中的意义提供了详细的数学支撑，并建立了与更广泛物理和数学领域的联系。

Abstract: The spherical grasshopper problem is a geometric optimization problem that arises in the context of Bell inequalities and can be interpreted as identifying the best local hidden variable approximation to quantum singlet correlations for measurements along random axes separated by a fixed angle. In a parallel publication [arXiv:2504.20953], we presented numerical solutions for this problem and explained their significance for singlet simulation and testing. In this companion paper, we describe in detail the geometric and computational framework underlying these results. We examine the role of spherical discretization and compare three natural variants of the problem: antipodal complementary lawns, antipodal independent lawns, and non-antipodal complementary lawns. We analyze the geometric structure of the corresponding optimal lawn configurations and interpret it in terms of a spherical harmonics expansion. We also discuss connections to other physical models and to classical problems in geometric probability.

</details>


### [177] [Coupled-Layer Construction of Quantum Product Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08711)
*Shuyu Zhang,Tzu-Chieh Wei,Nathanan Tantivasadakarn*

Main category: quant-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管乘积码（product codes）具有强大的代数表述，但从其组成代码构建一般乘积码的物理机制仍不清楚。本文旨在阐明张量积和平衡积代码的物理组装机制。

Result: 该框架能够容纳经典或量子CSS输入代码，统一了通过任意子凝聚（anyon condensation）构建高维拓扑相的已知物理机制，并自然地扩展到非拓扑代码。

Conclusion: 本文为乘积码提供了直观的物理构造框架，将代数表述与物理实现机制联系起来，统一了拓扑相构造方法并扩展了应用范围。

Abstract: Product codes are a class of quantum error correcting codes built from two or more constituent codes. They have recently gained prominence for a breakthrough yielding quantum low-density parity-check (qLDPC) codes with favorable scaling of both code distance and encoding rate. However, despite its powerful algebraic formulation, the physical mechanism for assembling a general product code from its constituents remains unclear. In this letter, we show that the tensor and balanced product codes admit an intuitive coupled-layer construction by taking a stack of one code and condensing a set of excitations in the pattern given by the checks of the other code. Our framework accommodates both classical or quantum CSS input codes, unifies known physical mechanisms for constructing higher dimensional topological phases via anyon condensation, and naturally extends to non-topological codes.

### [178] [Instanton construction of the mapping cone Thom-Smale complex](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08404)
*Hao Zhuang*

Motivation: 论文旨在研究由光滑闭$\ell$-形式诱导的映射锥德拉姆上链复形与映射锥Thom-Smale上链复形之间的对应关系，探索通过瞬子构造实现这种对应的方法。

Result: 证明了构造的瞬子复形与拓扑构造的映射锥Thom-Smale复形是上链同构的，建立了瞬子构造与拓扑构造之间的等价关系。

Conclusion: 通过瞬子构造成功实现了映射锥Thom-Smale复形的具体构建，为研究映射锥德拉姆上链复形与映射锥Thom-Smale上链复形之间的对应提供了新的构造方法。

Abstract: The wedge by a smooth closed $\ell$-form induces the mapping cone de Rham cochain complex. This complex is quasi-isomorphic to the mapping cone Thom-Smale cochain complex. We give an instanton construction of the mapping cone Thom-Smale complex in this paper. More precisely, for a Morse function with the transversality condition on a closed oriented Riemannian manifold, we construct an instanton cochain complex using the eigenspaces of the mapping cone Laplacian deformed by the Morse function and two parameters. As the main result, we prove that our instanton complex is cochain isomorphic to the topologically constructed mapping cone Thom-Smale complex.

### [179] [Mass and rigidity in almost Kähler geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08627)
*Partha Ghosh*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文推导了渐近局部欧几里得（ALE）近似凯勒流形的ADM质量显式公式，建立了正质量定理和Penrose型不等式，并研究了近似凯勒ALE流形的刚性现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究渐近局部欧几里得（asymptotically locally Euclidean, ALE）近似凯勒（almost Kähler）流形的质量公式，扩展Hein和LeBrun在凯勒ALE情形下的结果。探讨近似凯勒流形的刚性性质，为Bando-Kasue-Nakajima猜想提供新证据。

Method: 基于Witten证明自旋情形正质量猜想（positive mass conjecture）方法的spin^ℂ适应，区别于先前复几何方法。在四维情形下，研究渐近欧几里得（asymptotically Euclidean, AE）近似凯勒流形的质量性质。

Result: 推导了ALE近似凯勒流形ADM质量（ADM mass）的显式公式，用总埃尔米特标量曲率（total Hermitian scalar curvature）和底层近似复结构的拓扑数据表示。证明了四维AE近似凯勒流形的正质量定理（positive mass theorem）和Penrose型不等式（Penrose-type inequality）。

Conclusion: 具有非负标量曲率和特定衰减假设的近似凯勒-爱因斯坦ALE流形必然是凯勒-爱因斯坦流形。四维具有最大体积增长和L^2曲率的里奇平坦近似凯勒流形是凯勒流形，为Bando-Kasue-Nakajima猜想提供了新证据。类似刚性结果也适用于渐近局部平坦（asymptotically locally flat, ALF）流形。

Abstract: We derive an explicit formula for the ADM mass of asymptotically locally Euclidean (ALE) almost Kähler manifolds. The formula expresses the mass in terms of the total Hermitian scalar curvature and topological data associated with the underlying almost complex structure, extending a result of Hein and LeBrun in the Kähler ALE case. Our approach is based on a spin$^\mathbb {C}$ adaptation of Witten's proof of the positive mass conjecture in the spin case and is therefore distinct from previous complex-geometric methods. In dimension $4$, we prove a positive mass theorem and a Penrose-type inequality for asymptotically Euclidean (AE) almost Kähler manifolds. We also study rigidity phenomena of almost Kähler ALE manifolds. We prove that an almost Kähler-Einstein ALE manifold with nonnegative scalar curvature and certain decay assumptions is necessarily Kähler-Einstein. In particular, any four dimensional Ricci-flat almost Kähler manifold with maximal volume growth and curvature in $L^2$ is Kähler, yielding new evidence towards the Bando--Kasue--Nakajima conjecture. We also discuss analogous rigidity results for asymptotically locally flat (ALF) manifolds.

</details>

*Kazushi Kobayashi*

Method: 方法基于SYZ构造，将n维复环面视为平凡环面纤维化。通过引入沿纤维定义的泊松双向量θ进行非形式形变量子化，获得非交换复环面。进一步通过适当同构的扭曲，将线丛构造推广到更一般情形，并在镜像伙伴上定义对偶对象。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）将$L_θ$的构造推广到更一般的设定；2）在$X_θ^n$的镜像伙伴上构造与扩展非交换对象镜像对偶的对象。这些扩展为研究非交换几何与镜像对称的相互作用提供了新工具。

Conclusion: 本文成功扩展了非交换复环面上线丛变形的构造框架，建立了更一般的非交换几何对象及其镜像对偶。这项工作深化了对非交换变形与镜像对称之间关系的理解，为后续研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: By regarding a given $n$-dimensional complex torus $X^n$ as the trivial torus fibration $X^n \to \mathbb{R}^n/\mathbb{Z}^n$, we can obtain a mirror dual complexified symplectic torus $\check{X}^n$ based on the SYZ construction. In the middle 2000s, as a part of the study on noncommutative deformations of $X^n$, Kajiura examined the noncommutative complex torus $X_θ^n$ obtained via the (real) nonformal deformation quantization of $X^n \to \mathbb{R}^n/\mathbb{Z}^n$ by a Poisson bivector $θ$ defined along the fibers. In particular, he constructed the noncommutative deformations $L_θ \to X_θ^n$ of holomorphic line bundles on $X^n$ and a curved dg-category consisting of them. On the other hand, associated to this noncommutative deformation, we can construct a non-trivial deformation of the trivial holomorphic line bundle on $X^n$ by twisting it with a suitable isomorphism. In this paper, from this point of view, we extend the construction of $L_θ$ to the more general setting. Moreover, we also consider objects defined on a mirror partner of $X_θ^n$ which are mirror dual to such extended noncommutative objects.

*Keshav Raj Acharya,Andrei Ludu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于边界空间的辛几何（symplectic geometry）和拉格朗日子空间（Lagrangian subspaces）的各向同性结构，通过满足适当正交归一条件的拉格朗日边界矩阵Θ和B来定义受限关系TΘ,B。

Result: 证明了对于满足适当正交归一条件的每对拉格朗日边界矩阵Θ和B，受限关系TΘ,B是自伴的。该方法可扩展到使用渐近边界条件的半无限区间。

Conclusion: 该框架可应用于偏微分方程谱问题，包括行波稳定性（stability of traveling waves）和聚焦非线性薛定谔方程（focusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation）在孤子轮廓附近的线性化。自伴结构确保了使用Evans函数和传递矩阵方法进行稳定性分析所需的谱性质。

Abstract: This paper studies linear relations and their self-adjoint realizations arising from 2d-dimensional canonical systems, with a focus on how the symplectic structure interacts with boundary conditions. Understanding this interplay allows us to define self-adjoint realizations, which are crucial for analyzing the spectral properties of these systems. We prove that for each pair of Lagrangian boundary matrices Θ and B satisfying appropriate orthonormality conditions, the restricted relation TΘ,B is self-adjoint. Our approach relies on the symplectic geometry of boundary spaces and the isotropic structure of Lagrangian subspaces. We also discuss extensions to semi-infinite intervals using asymptotic boundary conditions. In the second part of the paper, we show how this framework applies to spectral problems from partial differential equations, including the stability of traveling waves and the linearization of the focusing nonlinear Schrodinger equation around soliton profiles. In particular, the self-adjoint structure with respect to the H-weighted inner product ensures the spectral properties needed for stability analysis using Evans function and transfer matrix methods. Applications to integrable systems, such as the stability of NLS bright solitons, are also presented.

Motivation: 研究动机在于建立一个统一的框架，连接已知的狄拉克-双曲正弦-戈登和狄拉克-正弦-戈登可积系统。通过引入相位参数控制变形，探索这两个系统之间的连续插值关系，并验证变形过程中可积性的保持。

Method: 方法基于构造一个sl(2,ℂ)值的Lax对（Lax pair），建立显式的零曲率表示（zero-curvature representation）。通过相位参数控制汤川耦合（Yukawa coupling）的变形，同时重新标度标量场反作用（scalar backreaction）。

Result: 研究证明了对于所有参数值，该理论族都保持可积性（integrability），并且参数不同的理论在物理上是非平凡的，即不能通过允许的场重定义相互关联。此外，推导了费米子双线性（fermion bilinear）的连续性关系，并构造了层次结构（hierarchy）的首批守恒密度。

Conclusion: 该单参数族在端点处分别约化为标准的可积狄拉克-双曲正弦-戈登模型，以及通过解析延拓得到的狄拉克-正弦-戈登系统，后者与质量型Thirring模型（massive Thirring model）对偶。研究建立了这两个已知可积系统之间的连续插值关系。

Abstract: We establish the integrability of a one-parameter family of coupled Dirac--scalar field theories in $(1+1)$ dimensions that interpolates between the known Dirac--sinh-Gordon and Dirac--sine-Gordon systems. The deformation is controlled by a phase parameter that modifies the Yukawa coupling and simultaneously rescales the scalar backreaction. For all values of the parameter, we construct an explicit zero-curvature representation based on an $sl(2,\mathbb{C})$-valued Lax pair and show that the deformation preserves integrability. We further prove that the family is physically non-trivial, in the sense that distinct parameter values are not related by admissible field redefinitions. In addition, we derive the continuity relation for the fermion bilinear, show that the spatial bilinear constraint follows from the zero-curvature equations, and construct the first conserved densities of the hierarchy. At the two endpoints, the family reduces to the standard integrable Dirac--sinh-Gordon model and, after analytic continuation, to the Dirac--sine-Gordon system which is dual to the massive Thirring model.

</details>


### [187] [Combining Symmetries and Helmholtz's Conditions to Construct Lagrangians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07760)
*Merced Montesinos,Diego Gonzalez,Jorge Meza*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于诺特定理（Noether's theorem）推导出新关系，揭示了拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）的Hessian矩阵分量、构型变量与时间的无穷小对称变换以及运动常数之间的相容性。利用这些关系，作者开发了两种新方法，将对称性要求直接纳入力学逆问题（inverse problem of mechanics）中，从而限制可接受拉格朗日量的集合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括：1）从诺特定理恒等式（Noether's identity）推导出新关系，揭示Hessian矩阵分量、无穷小对称变换和运动常数之间的相容性；2）结合赫尔姆霍兹条件（Helmholtz's conditions），开发两种新方法将对称性要求直接纳入力学逆问题；3）通过一维和二维示例验证理论。

Result: 主要成果是建立了诺特定理（Noether's theorem）与力学逆问题（inverse problem of mechanics）之间的直接联系。开发的方法能够从源头构造具有特定对称性的拉格朗日量（Lagrangian），并通过一维和二维示例验证了理论的有效性。

Conclusion: 结论表明，通过诺特定理（Noether's theorem）推导的新关系能够有效限制可接受拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）的集合。将对称性要求直接整合到力学逆问题（inverse problem of mechanics）中，为构造具有特定对称性的拉格朗日量提供了系统方法。

Abstract: We present new relations derived from Noether's identity that reveal the compatibility between the components of the Hessian matrix of the Lagrangian, the infinitesimal symmetry transformation of the configuration variables and time, and a constant of motion. Using these relations, we develop two new methods to incorporate symmetry requirements directly into the inverse problem of mechanics, thereby restricting the set of acceptable Lagrangians. We accomplish this by combining these relations with Helmholtz's conditions, which allow us to construct Lagrangians whose actions exhibit specific symmetries from the outset. The theory is illustrated with one- and two-dimensional examples.

### [189] [Random walks in finite Abelian groups with Birkhoff subpolytopes of doubly stochastic matrices and their physical implementation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08431)
*A. Vourdas*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了有限阿贝尔群（finite Abelian group）上的随机游走，使用与群相关的伯克霍夫子多面体（Birkhoff subpolytope）中的双随机转移矩阵。证明了所有未来概率向量属于一个不依赖于转移矩阵的多面体，该多面体随时间演化而收缩。应用包括加法群ℤ(d)和海森堡-外尔群（Heisenberg-Weyl group）HW(d)/ℤ(d)，并讨论了基于非选择性测量的物理实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究有限阿贝尔群上随机游走的概率演化特性，探索概率向量在多面体结构中的动态行为。旨在建立一般理论框架，并将其应用于具体群结构，同时探讨量子测量背景下的物理实现。

Method: 采用马尔可夫链方法，使用与群G相关的伯克霍夫子多面体（Birkhoff subpolytope）ℬ(G)中的双随机转移矩阵（doubly stochastic transition matrices）。应用多种量化工具描述概率向量：主序关系（majorization preorder）、洛伦兹值（Lorenz values）和基尼指数（Gini index）、熵量（entropic quantities）以及全变差距离（total variation distance）。

Result: 证明了所有未来概率向量属于一个不依赖于转移矩阵的多面体，且该多面体随时间演化而收缩。将一般结果应用于加法群ℤ(d)和海森堡-外尔群HW(d)/ℤ(d)。提出了两种物理实现：基于非选择性投影测量（non-selective projective measurements）的ℤ(d)随机游走，以及基于相干态非选择性POVM测量（non-selective POVM measurements with coherent states）的HW(d)/ℤ(d)随机游走。

Conclusion: 建立了有限阿贝尔群上随机游走的统一理论框架，揭示了概率向量在多面体结构中的收缩特性。通过具体群实例和应用展示了理论的普适性，并为量子测量背景下的物理实现提供了具体方案。

Abstract: Random walks in a finite Abelian group $G$ are studied. They use Markov chains with doubly stochastic transition matrices, in a Birkhoff subpolytope ${\cal B}(G)$ associated with the group $G$. It is shown that all future probability vectors belong to a polytope which does not depend on the transition matrices, and which shrinks during time evolution. Various quantities are used to describe the probability vectors: the majorization preorder, Lorenz values and the Gini index, entropic quantities, and the total variation distance. The general results are applied to the additive group ${\mathbb Z}(d)$, and to the Heisenberg-Weyl group $HW(d)/{\mathbb Z}(d)$. A physical implementation of random walks in ${\mathbb Z}(d)$ that involves a sequence of non-selective projective measurements, is discussed. A physical implementation of random walks in the Heisenberg-Weyl group $HW(d)/{\mathbb Z}(d)$ using a sequence of non-selective POVM measurements with coherent states, is also presented.

</details>


### [190] [Local Robustness of Bound States in the Continuum through Scattering-Matrix Eigenvector Continuation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08489)
*Ya Yan Lu,Jiaxin Zhou*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了周期性结构中连续谱束缚态（BICs）的拓扑特性，通过建立参数到散射系数的映射关系，为BICs的局部鲁棒性提供了拓扑解释，并提出了基于映射度的数值检测方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续谱束缚态（bound states in the continuum, BICs）作为准周期场，在连续谱频率下保持L²有界，其扰动可产生超强共振，在光子学中具有重要应用价值。然而，BICs的相位奇异性及其局部鲁棒性需要更深入的理论解释。

Method: 采用隐函数定理（implicit function theorem）分析系统参数变化时BICs如何连续变形为传播场。通过建立从参数到入射系数的映射$\mathcal{P}$，将BICs对应为该映射的零点，并利用映射度（mapping degree）理论分析BICs的拓扑特性。

Result: 当BICs对应的零点是孤立的且映射的定义域与值域维度相同时，BICs可与映射$\mathcal{P}$在小邻域内的映射度相关联。这一视角阐明了BICs的相位奇异性，并为BICs相对于给定参数的局部鲁棒性提供了普适的拓扑解释。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅从拓扑角度解释了BICs的局部鲁棒性，还提出了通过计算映射$\mathcal{P}$的映射度来检测和验证BICs的实用数值判据，为光子学应用提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We consider the diffraction of time-harmonic plane waves by a periodic structure, governed by the Helmholtz equation. Bound states in the continuum (BICs) are quasi-periodic fields that remain $L^{2}$-bounded over one period and occur at frequencies embedded in the continuous spectrum. Perturbations that break a BIC can lead to ultra-strong resonances, enabling various applications in photonics. Employing the implicit function theorem, we demonstrate how a simple BIC continuously deforms into a propagating field as system parameters vary in a neighborhood, with the frequency adjusting accordingly. In this setting, the incident coefficients of the field persist as an eigenvector of the scattering matrix with a fixed eigenvalue. By introducing a mapping $\mathcal{P}$ from the parameters to these coefficients, the zeros of $\mathcal{P}$ correspond precisely to BICs. When such a zero is isolated and the dimensions of the domain and range coincide, the BIC can be related to the mapping degree of $\mathcal{P}$ in a small neighborhood. This perspective clarifies the phase singularity associated with BICs and provides a general topological interpretation of their local robustness with respect to the given parameters. Moreover, it yields a practical numerical criterion for detecting and verifying BICs via computation of the mapping degree of $\mathcal{P}$.

### [193] [Study of the cosmological tensions and DESI-DR2 in the framework of the Little Rip model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07398)
*Safae Dahmani,Imad El Bojaddaini,Amine Bouali,Ahmed Errahmani,Taoufik Ouali*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过暗能量模型解决H₀和S₈张力问题，特别是探索小撕裂（Little Rip）模型这一具有未来突发事件的晚期宇宙模型。

Method: 采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法进行统计分析，使用最新观测数据，包括宇宙微波背景（CMB）、重子声学振荡（BAO）、PantheonPlus（PP）超新星数据以及DESI-DR2结合CMB和近期SNIa测量。

Result: 在（H₀, β）平面观察到正相关；使用早期测量（CMB）及结合BAO数据时，哈勃张力小于3σ，但结合晚期测量（PantheonPlus）后不再如此；模型倾向于quintessence场；贝叶斯因子显示LR模型仅对CMB数据提供改进拟合。

Abstract: We present an analysis that investigates the $H_0$ and $S_8$ tensions by considering a dark energy model. The latter is a late-time model characterized by a future abrupt event known as the Little Rip (LR) model and characterised by one extra parameter, $β$, compared to the standard model, $Λ$CDM. To test this approach, we perform a statistical analysis by the MCMC method using the most recent observational data. We obtain a positive correlation in ($H_0$, $β$) plane. We also note that the Hubble tension is less than $3σ$ when using early measurements, i.e., Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) data, and when combining it with Baryon Acoustic Oscillation (BAO) data, but it is no longer so when we combine early and late measurements (i.e. PantheonPlus (PP)). In addition, we test the model with DESI-DR2 combined with CMB and recent SNIa measurements. We notice that our model shifts toward the quintessence field. For a complete statistical analysis, we use the Akaike Information Criteria and Bayesian analysis of the evidence. According to Bayes factors, we find that the LR model provides an improved fit only to CMB data.

### [194] [First Optical Observation of Negative Ion Drift at Surface Pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06837)
*F. D. Amaro,R. Antonietti,E. Baracchini,L. Benussi,C. Capoccia,M. Caponero,L. G. M. de Carvalho,G. Cavoto,I. A. Costa,A. Croce,M. D'Astolfo,G. D'Imperio,G. Dho,F. Di Giambattista,E. Di Marco,J. M. F. dos Santos,D. Fiorina,F. Iacoangeli,Z. Islam,H. P. Lima,G. Maccarrone,R. D. P. Mano,D. J. G. Marques,G. Mazzitelli,P. Meloni,A. Messina,C. M. B. Monteiro,R. A. Nobrega,I. F. Pains,E. Paoletti,F. Petrucci,S. Piacentini,D. Pierluigi,D. Pinci,A. A. Prajapati,F. Renga,A. Russo,G. Saviano,P. A. O. C. Silva,N. J. C. Spooner,R. Tesauro,S. Tomassini,S. Torelli,D. Tozzi*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 首次在Gran Sasso实验室表面压力下观测到He:CF₄:SF₆混合气体中的负离子漂移（NID），通过光学读出时间投影室（TPC）实现了多物种负离子漂移操作，为大规模低扩散光学TPC用于稀有事件探测开辟了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索在表面压力条件下实现负离子漂移（negative ion drift）的可能性，这是CYGNO/INITIUM项目的一部分。目标是为稀有事件探测（rare event searches）开发大规模、低扩散的光学时间投影室（optical TPC）。

Method: 采用光学读出的时间投影室（optically read out Time Projection Chamber）在Gran Sasso实验室进行实验，使用He:CF₄:SF₆混合气体，表面压力为900±7 mbar。首次对负离子漂移区域进行光电倍增管波形分析（PMT waveform analysis），通过结合径迹几何和电荷输运的模型解释时间光模式。

Result: 观测到的漂移速度对应O(cm² V⁻¹ s⁻¹)量级的迁移率（mobilities），与负离子输运一致。时间扩展均值与漂移距离的线性比例关系揭示了除主要SF₆⁻物种外，还存在更快的少数电荷载流子群体，其漂移速度比主要物种高约25%。

Conclusion: 该研究首次在表面压力条件下实现了He:CF₄:SF₆混合气体中的多物种负离子漂移操作，为开发大规模、低扩散光学TPC用于稀有事件探测提供了具体的技术路径。

Abstract: We report the first observation of Negative Ion Drift (NID) at surface pressure of $900 \pm 7$ mbar at Laboratori Nazionali del Gran Sasso in a He:CF$_4$:SF$_6$ mixture using an optically read out Time Projection Chamber (TPC) within the CYGNO/INITIUM project. We present the first PMT waveform analysis in the NID regime, interpreting the temporal light pattern through a model that combines track geometry and charge transport. The inferred drift velocities correspond to mobilities of O(cm$^2$ V$^{-1}$ s$^{-1}$), consistent with negative ion transport. The observed linear scaling of the time extension mean with drift distance reveals the presence of a faster minority charge carrier population in addition to the dominant SF$_6^-$ species, drifting at a $\sim$25\% higher velocity under external inputs. These results demonstrate multi-species negative ion drift operation at surface pressure in a He:CF$_4$:SF$_6$ mixture and open a concrete path toward large scale, low diffusion optical TPCs for rare event searches.

</details>

Method: 基于慕尼黑工业大学（Technical University of Munich）的NUCLEUS测试调试结果及先前表征活动，使用配备两个跃迁边缘传感器（transition-edge sensors）的蓝宝石探测器，在不同实验条件下测量本底率，进行综合分析。

Abstract: The NUCLEUS experiment aims to detect coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering of reactor antineutrinos using low-threshold, gram-scale cryogenic calorimeters. Similar to other low-threshold experiments, NUCLEUS observes a sharp rise in the event rate below a few hundred eV, referred to as the low energy excess (LEE), whose origin remains yet unidentified. Building on results from the NUCLEUS testing and commissioning at the Technical University of Munich and from previous characterization campaigns, we present a comprehensive study of the background rate measured with a sapphire detector equipped with two transition-edge sensors under various experimental conditions. We find no evidence for a dependence of the LEE rate on the particle background level, whereas the results indicate that slower cooling-down procedures lead to lower initial LEE rates. The behavior of the LEE rate during the same cooldown is comparable across the measurements and is best described by a power law with a common exponent across datasets of $(-0.59 \pm 0.06)$, when time is expressed from the moment the detector reaches the 4 K temperature. These findings provide valuable guidance for future LEE mitigation strategies in the NUCLEUS experiment.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 这种调谐方法避免了向谐振体积内插入元件，特别适用于轴子晕镜实验中的高品质因数超导腔体，并可应用于能在多特斯拉磁场中运行的REBCO基实现方案。

Abstract: We demonstrate a novel broad-frequency tuning mechanism for superconducting microwave cavities designed for dark matter searches. Using a Nb$_3$Sn-coated cigar-shaped cavity operating at approximately 9\,GHz, we achieve continuous frequency tuning exceeding 1\,GHz by mechanically separating the two cavity halves: a "tuning-by-opening" technique. Finite-element method simulations predict that radiative losses do not degrade the quality factor even for large openings, as a closed cavity with an intrinsic quality factor of $10^7$ maintains this value for apertures up to 9\,mm, corresponding to a tuning range from 9.0 to 7.5\,GHz. Experimental validation using both copper ring spacers and a continuous sliding mechanism confirms $Q_0$ values exceeding the dark matter quality factor across the entire explored frequency range, despite mechanical imperfections and film non-uniformities. This tuning approach avoids inserting elements into the resonant volume, making it particularly suitable for high-Q superconducting cavities in axion haloscope experiments and readily applicable to REBCO-based implementations capable of operating in multi-tesla magnetic fields.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Conventional heat engines require two reservoirs; their efficiency is bounded by the Carnot limit. In a well-defined theoretical framework where the working fluid undergoes phase change in the presence of asymmetric constraints, that limit does not apply: the appropriate description is constraint-reshaped entropy distributions $P_{\infty}(S;λ)$. We give \emph{one} complete \emph{theoretical} design: micro temperature difference (1--2\,$^\circ$C), subcooled liquid, liquid-only compression, and asymmetric constraint phase change (R134a). The cycle absorbs heat from a \textbf{single} heat source (the environment; $q_{\mathrm{in}} = 0.9\,\mathrm{kJ}/\mathrm{kg}$ per cycle), delivers net useful work ($w_{\mathrm{net}} = +0.514\,\mathrm{kJ}/\mathrm{kg}$), and uses only standard components. The analysis is rigorous: energy and mass balance are closed; all property data are from NIST and are reproducible at the cited URL. We show that, within this framework, this constitutes single-heat-source power generation.

### [199] [Offer of a reward does not always promote trust in spatial games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07328)
*Haidong Zhang,Chaoqian Wang,Shuo Liu,Charo I. del Genio,Stefano Boccaletti,Xin Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究在空间信任博弈（spatial trust game）中引入角色间奖励机制（inter-role reward mechanism），发现适度奖励能打破不信任的主导地位，但过度奖励反而会抑制信任的演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 信任是人类社会的基石之一，其演化压力机制可能源于对可信行为的激励。然而在空间信任博弈中，这类奖励机制受到的关注相对较少，而该模型常用于演化博弈论（evolutionary game theory）建模。

Method: 在空间信任博弈中引入角色间奖励机制，使投资方（trustor）能够选择支付额外成本来奖励可信的受托方（trustworthy trustee）。通过大量数值模拟（extensive numerical simulations）进行研究。

Result: 研究发现奖励并不总是促进信任：适度奖励能打破不信任的主导地位，有利于投资；但过度奖励会刺激不回报策略（nonreturn strategy），最终抑制信任演化。较低奖励成本不一定促进信任，而成本较高但不过度的奖励能增强原始投资的优势。

Conclusion: 该模型揭示了复杂社会中信任与奖励关系的反直觉（counterintuitive）本质：适度奖励能促进信任，但过度奖励反而会抑制信任演化，且奖励成本与信任促进效果之间存在非线性关系。

Abstract: Trust is one of the cornerstones of human society. One of the evolutionary pressure mechanisms that may have led to its emergence is the presence of incentives for trustworthy behavior. However, this type of reward has received relatively little attention in the context of spatial trust games, which are often used to build models in evolutionary game theory. To fill this gap, we introduce an inter-role reward mechanism in the spatial trust game, so that an investing trustor can choose to pay an extra cost to reward a trustworthy trustee. With extensive numerical simulations, we find that this type of reward does not always promote trust. Rather, while moderate rewards break the dominance of mistrust, thereby favoring investment, excessive rewards eventually stimulate a nonreturn strategy, ultimately suppressing the evolution of trust. Additionally, lower reward costs do not necessarily promote trust. Instead, more costly, but not excessive, rewards enhance the advantage of the original investment, consolidating the clusters of rewarders and improving trust. Our model thus provides evidence about the counterintuitive nature of the relationship between trust and rewards in a complex society.

</details>


### [200] [Fisher Curvature Scaling at Critical Points: An Exact Information-Geometric Exponent from Periodic Boundary Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07651)
*Max Zhuravlev*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了临界点附近晶格自旋模型的费希尔信息度量（Fisher information metric）在微观耦合参数流形上的标量曲率（scalar curvature）标度行为。研究发现曲率绝对值随系统尺寸呈幂律增长，其标度指数 $d_R$ 可由临界指数 $\nu$ 和 $\eta$ 解析表达，并在二维/三维伊辛（Ising）模型和二维波茨（Potts）模型中通过精确计算和蒙特卡洛模拟得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索临界点附近统计模型的几何结构，特别是费希尔信息度量在微观耦合参数流形上的曲率性质。通过分析标量曲率的标度行为，旨在揭示临界现象与信息几何（information geometry）之间的深层联系，并建立曲率指数与已知临界指数之间的解析关系。

Method: 研究方法结合了理论推导与数值计算。理论方面，推导了 $d$ 维周期边界晶格系统中费希尔流形标量曲率的标度指数 $d_R$ 与临界指数 $\nu$、$\eta$ 的解析关系：$d_R = (d\nu+ 2\eta)/(d\nu+ \eta)$。数值方面，采用精确转移矩阵（transfer-matrix）计算（$L=6$--$9$）和多种子蒙特卡洛（multi-seed MCMC）模拟（至 $L=24$）验证二维伊辛模型；使用 MCMC 模拟三维伊辛模型（至 $L=10$）；对二维波茨模型 $q=3,4$ 则采用快速傅里叶变换蒙特卡洛（FFT-MCMC）模拟（至 $L=40$）。

Result: 研究结果证实了理论预测的标度关系。对于二维伊辛模型（$\nu=1$, $\eta=1/4$），预测 $d_R=10/9$，数值结果为 $d_R = 1.1115 \pm 0.0002$，高度吻合。三维伊辛模型（$\nu=0.630$, $\eta=0.0363$）预测 $d_R=1.019$，幂律拟合得 $d_R=1.040$，基本一致。二维波茨模型 $q=3$ 预测 $33/29 \approx 1.138$，有效指数 $d_\mathrm{eff}$ 在 $\sim 1.20$ 附近非单调振荡，与 $O(1/(\ln L)^2)$ 对数修正一致；$q=4$ 模型则表现出更强的对数修正振荡。此外，所有模型中里奇分解恒等式（Ricci decomposition identity）$R_3 = -R_1/2$, $R_4 = -R_2/2$ 在 5-6 位有效数字内成立。

Conclusion: 结论指出，费希尔流形标量曲率的标度指数 $d_R$ 构成了一个新的临界指数，它不同于鲁佩纳热力学曲率（Ruppeiner thermodynamic curvature），反映了增长中的费希尔流形的集体几何性质。该研究为理解临界现象的信息几何结构提供了新视角，并提出了可用于检验其他普适类（universality classes）的证伪标准和预测。

Abstract: We study the scalar curvature of the Fisher information metric on the microscopic coupling-parameter manifold of lattice spin models at criticality. For a $d$-dimensional lattice with periodic boundary conditions and $n = L^d$ sites, the Fisher manifold has $m = d \cdot n$ dimensions (one per bond), and we find $|\mathcal{R}(J_c)| \sim n^{d_R}$ with $d_R = (dν+ 2η)/(dν+ η)$, where $ν$ and $η$ are the correlation-length and anomalous-dimension critical exponents. For 2D Ising ($ν= 1$, $η= 1/4$), this predicts $d_R = 10/9$, confirmed by exact transfer-matrix computations ($L = 6$--$9$: $d_R = 1.1115 \pm 0.0002$) and multi-seed MCMC through $L = 24$. For 3D Ising ($ν= 0.630$, $η= 0.0363$), the prediction $d_R = 1.019$ is consistent with MCMC on $L^3$ tori up to $L = 10$ (power-law fit: $d_R = 1.040$). For 2D Potts $q = 3$ (predicted $33/29 \approx 1.138$), FFT-MCMC through $L = 40$ shows $d_\mathrm{eff}$ oscillating non-monotonically around $\sim 1.20$, consistent with $O(1/(\ln L)^2)$ logarithmic corrections. For $q = 4$ (predicted $22/19$), effective exponents oscillate with strong logarithmic corrections. The Ricci decomposition identity $R_3 = -R_1/2$, $R_4 = -R_2/2$ holds to 5--6 digits for all models. This exponent is distinct from Ruppeiner thermodynamic curvature and reflects the collective geometry of the growing Fisher manifold. We provide falsification criteria and predictions for additional universality classes.

</details>


### [201] [Percolation on multifractal, scale-free weighted planar stochastic porous lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08044)
*Proshanto Kumar,Md. Kamrul Hassan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出加权平面随机多孔晶格（WPSPL），通过迭代细分单位正方形生成几何无序基底。该晶格具有多重分形特性，其双晶格形成幂律度分布复杂网络。研究WPSPL上的键渗流，发现临界指数随参数q连续变化，构成不同普适类家族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于加权平面随机多孔晶格（Weighted Planar Stochastic Porous Lattice, WPSPL）的特殊性质：多重分形特性、统计自相似性及其双晶格形成的幂律度分布复杂网络。这些特性促使研究者探索该多孔晶格上的渗流行为及其临界现象。

Method: 方法包括：1）通过迭代细分单位正方形生成WPSPL，每次选择概率正比于面积的块，以概率q（1-q）保留（移除）子块；2）解析证明WPSPL无限多非平凡守恒量的多重分形特性；3）数值验证不同时间快照的统计自相似性；4）研究WPSPL上的键渗流（bond percolation），确定渗流阈值并估计临界指数α、β、γ。

Result: 结果显示：1）WPSPL具有多重分形（multifractality）特性；2）双晶格（dual lattice）形成幂律度分布（power-law degree distribution）的复杂网络；3）渗流临界指数随参数q连续变化，反映晶格全局维度（global dimension）依赖q的不同普适类家族；4）Rushbrooke不等式近乎等式满足；5）非多孔情况（q=1）虽具有全局维度2，但不同于传统二维晶格普适类。

Conclusion: 结论强调几何无序（geometric disorder）、多重分形、无标度配位数无序（scale-free coordination number disorder）和多孔性如何产生非常规临界行为。WPSPL为研究几何无序系统中的相变提供了新范例，其连续变化的临界指数揭示了传统普适类分类的局限性。

Abstract: We introduce the Weighted Planar Stochastic Porous Lattice (WPSPL), a geometrically disordered substrate generated by iteratively subdividing a unit square. At each step a block is selected with probability proportional to its area, divided into four parts, and one sub-block is retained (removed) with probability $q$ ($1-q$). We show analytically that the WPSPL exhibits multifractality for each of its infinitely many nontrivial conserved quantities and demonstrate numerically that its snapshots at different times are statistically self-similar. The dual of the lattice forms a complex network with a power-law degree distribution. Motivated by these properties of this porous lattice, we study bond percolation on the WPSPL, determine the percolation threshold, and estimate the critical exponents $α$, $β$, and $γ$ associated with the specific heat, order parameter, and susceptibility, respectively. The exponents vary continuously with $q$, reflecting a family of distinct universality classes as the global dimension of the lattice depends on $q$. Remarkably, the Rushbrooke inequality, $α+ 2β+ γ\ge 2$, is satisfied in near equality. Notably, the nonporous case ($q=1$) has a global dimension $2$ but lies outside the universality class of conventional two-dimensional lattices. Our results highlight how geometric disorder, multifractality, scale-free coordination number disorder, and porosity produce unconventional critical behavior.

</details>


### [202] [Synchronization of higher-dimensional Kuramoto oscillators on networks: from scalar to matrix-weighted couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08352)
*Anna Gallo,Renaud Lambiotte,Timoteo Carletti*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了Kuramoto模型在d维空间中的推广，其中振子表示为(d-1)-球面上的单位向量，并通过矩阵加权网络（matrix-weighted network, MWN）相互作用。通过主稳定性函数（Master Stability Function）方法推导了全局同步的必要条件，并证明同步解在任何正耦合强度K下对任何连通网络都是局部稳定的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kuramoto模型是研究耦合振子系统同步的典范模型，但其经典形式仅限于单位圆上的标量相位。本研究旨在将这一模型推广到更高维度，探索振子表示为(d-1)-球面上单位向量并通过矩阵加权网络相互作用时的同步行为。

Method: 采用主稳定性函数（Master Stability Function）方法分析全局同步条件。通过引入适当的变量变换，将完整的Nd维问题简化为一系列d维特征值问题，每个问题由标量加权拉普拉斯矩阵（scalar weighted Laplacian）的特征值参数化。

Result: 研究发现，同步解的存在要求所有节点具有相同的频率矩阵（frequency matrices），且在矩阵加权网络情况下需要网络结构满足一致性条件（coherence condition）。分析表明，对于任何连通网络，只要耦合强度K为正，同步解就是局部稳定的。

Conclusion: 本文成功将Kuramoto模型推广到高维空间，建立了矩阵加权网络框架下的同步理论。理论分析结合数值模拟验证了同步解的稳定性条件，为研究复杂网络中的高维同步现象提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: The Kuramoto model is the paradigmatic model to study synchronization in coupled oscillator systems. In its classical formulation, the oscillators move on the unit circle, each characterized by a scalar phase and a natural frequency, by interacting through a sinusoidal coupling. In this work, we propose a d-dimensional generalization in which oscillators are represented as unit vectors on the (d-1)-sphere and interact through a matrix-weighted network (MWN), a recently introduced framework where links are endowed with a matrix weight instead of a scalar one. We derive necessary conditions for global synchronization via a Master Stability Function approach: the existence of a synchronous solution requires identical frequency matrices across nodes and, in the MWN case, a coherence condition on the network structure. Through a suitable change of variables, the stability analysis reduces the full Nd-dimensional problem to a family of d-dimensional eigenvalue problems, each one parametrized by the eigenvalue of a suitable scalar weighted Laplacian, showing that the synchronous solution is locally stable for any positive coupling strength K on any connected network. Analytical results are complemented by numerical simulations.

</details>


### [203] [The quantum square-well fluid: a thermodynamic geometric view](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08690)
*J. L. López-Picón,L. F. Escamilla-Herrera,Alejandro Gil-Villegas,José Torres-Arenas*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究采用基于路径积分-项链类比（path-integral-necklace analogy）的三阶微扰理论框架，分析了具有方势阱相互作用的量子流体的热力学几何性质。研究比较了量子流体与经典对应物在三种相互作用范围下的热力学和几何特性，重点考察了标量曲率行为、临界性以及从曲率和多种热力学响应函数导出的维德姆线（Widom lines）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究量子效应对热力学系统几何信息的影响，以及相互作用范围在塑造超临界热力学行为中的关键作用。通过比较量子流体与经典对应物的热力学几何性质，旨在揭示量子效应如何平滑标量曲率的超临界异常并改变其极值位置。

Method: 研究方法基于路径积分-项链类比（path-integral-necklace analogy）的三阶微扰理论框架，分析具有方势阱相互作用的量子流体。研究比较了相互作用范围λ*=1.3、1.5和1.7时量子流体与经典对应物的热力学和几何特性。

Result: 量子效应平滑了标量曲率的超临界异常，并改变了短程相互作用下曲率极值的位置。曲率及其热容的临界指数与平均场预测一致。对于短程相互作用，与温度相关响应函数和曲率标量相关的维德姆线（Widom lines）表现出显著的经典-量子差异；而从等温压缩率导出的维德姆线仅显示微小变化。

Conclusion: 研究结论强调了量子效应对热力学系统几何信息的敏感性，以及相互作用范围在塑造超临界热力学行为中的关键作用。这些发现为理解量子流体与经典流体在热力学几何性质上的差异提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We investigate several aspects of the thermodynamic geometry for a quantum fluid with square-well interactions using a third-order perturbation theory framework based on the path-integral-necklace analogy. A comparison is made between the thermodynamic and geometric properties of the quantum fluid and its classical counterpart for the interaction ranges $λ^{*}= 1.3$, 1.5, and 1.7. In particular, we analyze the scalar curvature behavior, criticality, and the corresponding Widom lines derived from curvature and several thermodynamic response functions. Quantum effects are shown to smooth supercritical anomalies of the scalar curvature and to shift its extrema for short-range interactions, while leaving the critical exponents of both the curvature and its heat capacity consistent with mean-field predictions. Widom lines associated with temperature-dependent response functions and with the curvature scalar exhibit pronounced classical-quantum differences for short interaction ranges; in contrast, those derived from the isothermal compressibility exhibit only minor variations. Overall, these results highlight the sensitivity of geometric information of thermodynamic systems due to quantum effects and the crucial role of the interaction range in shaping supercritical thermodynamic behavior.

Method: 采用量子调和分析（quantum harmonic analysis）框架，对具有平方可积不可约酉表示的局部紧群，研究指示函数与固定密度算子卷积的特征值分布。通过构造算子序列，分析特征值在1附近小邻域内的渐近数量。

Conclusion: 研究建立了群结构性质（幺模性与Følner序列存在性）与卷积算子特征值渐近行为之间的等价关系，为量子调和分析中算子谱理论提供了新的理论框架，并统一了包括海森堡群在内的多个重要特例。

Abstract: Within the framework of quantum harmonic analysis, for a locally compact group $G$ with a square-integrable, irreducible unitary representation, we analyze the eigenvalue distributions of convolutions between indicator functions on $G$ and a fixed density operator on the representation space, a concept which generalizes localization operators. In particular, we consider a sequence of such operators and the asymptotic number of eigenvalues that lie within a small distance of $1$. We show that a previously postulated type of asymptotic behavior occurs if and only if the group is unimodular and the sets underlying the indicator functions form a Følner sequence. Applying this, we obtain positive results for nilpotent and homogeneous Lie groups, recovering an established result for the Heisenberg group as a special case.

### [205] [Why does entropy drive evolution equations?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07653)
*Mark A. Peletier*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 该论文提出熵（entropy）作为演化方程驱动力的统一解释：熵表征了底层随机过程的稳态测度（invariant measure），这一原理可解释熵在不同确定性及随机演化方程中的多种表现形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 熵作为驱动力出现在许多确定性及随机演化方程中，且呈现不同形式。论文旨在揭示这些看似不同的实例背后的共同原理，解释熵为何以及如何驱动这些演化方程。

Method: 通过将熵解释为底层随机过程的稳态测度表征，为不同演化方程中的熵提供统一理解框架。该方法从随机过程、梯度流（gradient flows）和GENERIC系统等实例进行说明。

Result: 研究结果表明，熵驱动演化的共同原理在于其表征了底层随机过程的稳态测度。这一解释阐明了熵在不同方程中的出现原因、多种形式及其驱动机制。

Conclusion: 熵作为演化方程驱动力的统一解释框架得以建立，该框架通过稳态测度的概念连接了随机过程、梯度流和GENERIC系统等不同领域的演化方程。

Abstract: `Entropy' appears as driving force in many different evolution equations, both deterministic and stochastic, and in these equations this `entropy' also takes different forms. We show how all these examples can be understood as different instances of a common principle: Entropy drives evolutions because it characterizes the invariant measure of an underlying stochastic process. This interpretation explains the appearance of entropy, the different forms that entropy takes in these equations, and how entropy `drives' these evolution equations. We illustrate this common structure with examples from stochastic processes, gradient flows, and GENERIC systems.

### [206] [Fundamental Limits of Quantum Sensors for Gravitational Wave Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06772)
*Sergio Gaudio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨量子传感技术（如光学钟、量子磁力计）能否直接探测或增强引力波探测，发现耦合机制是关键决定因素。分析显示内部原子耦合增益极低，质心耦合灵敏度不足，而光传播耦合机制使激光干涉仪和原子干涉仪可行，量子增强效果受探测器噪声架构限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子传感技术的最新进展（如系统不确定度达5.5×10⁻¹⁹的光学钟、突破标准量子极限的频率依赖压缩、接近基本灵敏度极限的量子磁力计）引发了一个自然问题：这些技术能否直接探测引力波，或将现有探测器的能力提升至当前水平之上？

Method: 从费米法线坐标（Fermi normal coordinates）中的潮汐哈密顿量出发，在线性化广义相对论和非相对论量子力学框架内，识别了三种物理上不同的耦合机制，并推导了它们的换能器增益（transducer gains）。

Result: 内部原子耦合（电子波函数的潮汐畸变）的换能器增益GA=2.4×10⁻²⁰，所有J=0钟态的一阶能量移动为零，相对于激光干涉仪存在约10³⁵的不足。质心耦合（测地线运动的多普勒频移）达到约10⁻¹⁸的应变灵敏度，仍比LISA要求高10⁴倍。光传播耦合（宏观基线上的相位积累）提供了巨大的换能器增益，使激光干涉仪和原子干涉仪成为可能。

Conclusion: 对于利用第三种机制的探测器，量子传感器能提供的改进程度受探测器噪声架构限制：LISA的噪声预算约91%为经典噪声，将组合量子增强限制在ε≈1.04，而处于散粒噪声主导区域的地基探测器可实现ε=1.8-2.4。原子干涉仪利用相同的光传播机制，独特地覆盖0.01-10 Hz频段。

Abstract: Recent advances in quantum sensing -- optical clocks at $5.5\times 10^{-19}$ systematic uncertainty, frequency-dependent squeezing below the standard quantum limit, quantum magnetometers approaching fundamental sensitivity limits -- raise a natural question: can these technologies detect gravitational waves directly, or enhance existing detectors beyond current capabilities? We show that the answer is primarily determined by the \emph{coupling mechanism} between the gravitational wave and the sensor. Starting from the tidal Hamiltonian in Fermi normal coordinates, we identify three physically distinct coupling mechanisms and derive their transducer gains within linearized general relativity and non-relativistic quantum mechanics. Internal atomic coupling (tidal distortion of electronic wavefunctions) yields a transducer gain $G_A = 2.4\times 10^{-20}$, with vanishing first-order energy shifts for all $J=0$ clock states -- a $\sim\!10^{35}$ deficit relative to laser interferometry that exceeds any projected quantum enhancement. Center-of-mass coupling (Doppler shifts from geodesic motion) reaches strain sensitivities of $\sim\!10^{-18}$, still $10^4$ above LISA requirements. Light propagation coupling (phase accumulation over macroscopic baselines) provides the enormous transducer gain that makes laser interferometry -- and atom interferometry -- viable. For detectors exploiting this third mechanism, we quantify how much improvement quantum sensors can provide through the detector's noise architecture: LISA's noise budget is $\sim\!91\%$ classical, limiting combined quantum enhancement to $\mathcal{E} \approx 1.04$, while ground-based detectors in the shot-noise-dominated regime achieve $\mathcal{E} = 1.8$--$2.4$. Atom interferometers exploit the same light-propagation mechanism to uniquely access the 0.01--10~Hz band.

</details>


### [207] [Spectral sirens cosmology from binary black holes populations with sharper mass features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06792)
*Tom Bertheas,Vasco Gennari,Danièle Steer,Nicola Tamanini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种仅利用引力波数据即可提取宇宙学参数的新方法——光谱警报推断（spectral-sirens inference），无需电磁对应体或星系目录。通过引入新的参数化质量函数分析GWTC-4.0数据，将哈勃常数（Hubble constant）的测量精度提高了约50%，达到23%精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力波宇宙学方法通常依赖电磁对应体（electromagnetic counterparts）或星系目录（galaxy catalogs）来确定红移，这限制了观测样本的数量和精度。本研究旨在开发一种仅基于引力波数据本身就能提取宇宙学参数的方法，从而充分利用引力波观测的潜力。

Method: 研究引入了新的参数化质量函数（parametric mass functions）来描述双黑洞（binary black hole）群体的质量分布，这些函数能够捕捉质量谱中的显著结构。使用这些改进的群体模型分析最新的引力波瞬变目录GWTC-4.0，并测试了包括修正引力波传播（modified gravitational-wave propagation）在内的替代宇宙学模型。

Result: 仅使用幂律群体模型（powerlaws-only population models）就将哈勃常数约束到23%精度：$H_0 = 53.3^{+14.0}_{-10.8} ~\rm km \,s^{-1} \,Mpc^{-1}$（68%置信水平）。这比LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组相应的纯双黑洞分析提高了约50%精度，达到他们包含中子星和星系目录的联合分析相当的水平。对修正引力波传播参数也建立了有竞争力的约束。

Conclusion: 光谱警报推断方法展示了仅利用引力波数据提取宇宙学参数的强大能力。研究结果强调了黑洞质量分布与推断宇宙学参数之间的强烈相互作用，表明需要合适的群体模型来充分开发引力波数据的潜力。对未来O5观测运行的预测显示，更大数据集将显著改善哈勃常数和修正传播参数的约束。

Abstract: Spectral-sirens inference enables the extraction of cosmological parameters from gravitational-wave data alone, without electromagnetic counterparts or galaxy catalogs. We introduce new parametric mass functions for the binary black hole population that capture significant structure across the mass spectrum and are moderately favoured by Bayesian evidence over simpler models. Analysing the latest gravitational-wave transient catalog, GWTC-4.0, we show that powerlaws-only population models constrain the Hubble constant to $23\%$ precision, $H_0 = 53.3^{+14.0}_{-10.8} ~\rm km \,s^{-1} \,Mpc^{-1}$ at $68\%$ confidence level. This represents a $\sim 50\%$ improvement over the corresponding binary black hole-only analysis by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA collaboration, achieving precision comparable to their joint analyses including neutron stars and galaxy catalogs. We further test alternative cosmological models, establishing competitive constraints on modified gravitational-wave propagation, while bounds on the dark energy equation-of-state parameters remain uninformative. Projecting to future O5 observing run, we forecast substantial improvements in $H_0$ and modified propagation parameters with larger datasets at higher redshifts. Our results highlight the strong interplay between the black hole mass distribution and inferred cosmology, underscoring the need for suitable population models to fully exploit gravitational-wave data.

</details>


### [208] [Stationary Particle Creation and Entanglement in the Rotating Teo Wormhole: A Quantum Mode-Mixing Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06822)
*Ramesh Radhakrishnan,Gerald Cleaver,William Julius*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转可穿越虫洞（rotating traversable wormhole）中无质量标量扰动的量子场论处理，通过Bogoliubov变换计算了真空模式混合，揭示了旋转和参考系拖拽（frame dragging）导致的几何不对称性如何产生粒子创生和量子放大效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旋转可穿越虫洞允许在没有事件视界（event horizon）的情况下研究参考系拖拽和旋转效应。本文旨在发展旋转Teo时空（rotating Teo spacetime）中无质量标量扰动的量子场论处理方法，以探索几何不对称性如何影响量子真空模式混合。

Method: 采用Bogoliubov变换形式体系（Bogoliubov transformation formalism），在两个渐近平坦区域（asymptotically flat regions）上构造"in"和"out"模式解，并计算量化真空模式混合的Bogoliubov系数。通过势垒穿透指数（barrier-penetration exponent）解析评估由旋转和参考系拖拽诱导的有效径向势垒的反射和透射振幅。

Result: 获得了Bogoliubov系数、平均粒子数和双模纠缠熵（two-mode entanglement entropy）作为旋转参数的闭式表达式。放大效应源于量子Bogoliubov模式混合和真空压缩（vacuum squeezing），而非经典超辐射通量增强。共转和反转载波经历不等价散射，使过程具有内在非互易性。

Conclusion: 该机制被识别为不对称动态卡西米尔效应（Asymmetric Dynamical Casimir Effect, ADCE）的稳态几何类比。在旋转Teo几何中，旋转和参考系拖拽扮演了动态卡西米尔效应中移动边界（moving boundaries）的角色，成为不对称真空模式混合的源。

Abstract: Rotating traversable wormholes allow the effects of frame dragging and rotation to be studied in the absence of event horizons. We develop a quantum field theoretic treatment of massless scalar perturbations in the rotating Teo spacetime. This spacetime is an exact, stationary, horizonless wormhole connecting two asymptotically flat regions. Using the Bogoliubov transformation formalism, we construct ``in'' and ``out'' mode solutions defined on the two asymptotic regions and compute the Bogoliubov coefficients that quantify vacuum mode mixing.
  The effective radial potential induced by rotation and frame dragging forms an asymmetric scattering barrier. This geometric asymmetry allows an exact analytic evaluation of reflection and transmission amplitudes via the barrier-penetration exponent. This results in closed-form expressions for the Bogoliubov coefficients, the mean particle number, and the two-mode entanglement entropy as functions of the rotation parameter. The resulting amplification arises at the level of quantum Bogoliubov mode mixing and vacuum squeezing, rather than classical superradiant flux enhancement.
  Since this spacetime is stationary, particle creation originates from geometric asymmetry and boundary conditions, and not from explicit time dependence. Co-rotating and counter-rotating modes experience inequivalent scattering. This renders the process intrinsically non-reciprocal. We identify this mechanism as a stationary, geometric analogue of the Asymmetric Dynamical Casimir Effect (ADCE). In the rotating Teo geometry, rotation and frame dragging play the role that moving boundaries play in the dynamical Casimir effect, acting as the source of asymmetric vacuum mode mixing.

</details>


### [209] [Constraint Analysis and Quantization of Anomalous 2-D Thomas-Whitehead Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06995)
*Eric Biedke,Salvatore Quaid,Vincent Rodgers*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了托马斯-怀特黑德引力（Thomas-Whitehead gravity）框架下的约束分析和哈密顿量量子化问题。通过引入微分同胚场（diffeomorphism field）作为动力学变量，解决了传统二维有效波利亚科夫作用量（Polyakov action）中哈密顿量消失的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维有效波利亚科夫作用量（Polyakov action）通常作为弦理论和费米子与引力耦合的异常贡献出现。然而，由于重参数化不变性（reparameterization invariance），该有效作用量在不同规范（如动力学光锥规范和ADM形式）下均产生消失的哈密顿量作为约束条件。

Method: 采用托马斯-怀特黑德引力（Thomas-Whitehead gravity）形式，将有效波利亚科夫作用量扩展，使轨道定义的余伴随元素成为动力学场，即微分同胚场（diffeomorphism field）。在动力学光锥规范和ADM形式下进行约束分析，并在闵可夫斯基背景（Minkowski background）中重复分析，同时考虑来自托马斯-怀特黑德作用量的微分同胚场动力学作用。

Result: 为微分同胚场添加动力学后，成功消除了消失的哈密顿量问题。这表明通过引入额外的动力学自由度，可以解决传统二维引力理论中的约束问题。

Conclusion: 托马斯-怀特黑德引力框架通过引入动力学微分同胚场，为二维引力理论的哈密顿量约束问题提供了解决方案。该方法将几何作用在维拉索罗代数（Virasoro algebra）余伴随轨道上的自然实现进行了扩展，使得约束分析和量子化成为可能。

Abstract: The two-dimensional effective Polyakov action is often realized as the anomalous contributions of string theories and fermions coupled to gravity in two-dimensions. However, as a result of the reparameterization invariance, one finds that the effective action produces vanishing Hamiltonians as constraints even in disparate gauges such as the dynamical light-cone and the ADM formalism of the metric. On the other hand, two-dimensional gravitational theories naturally arise as geometric actions on the coadjoint orbits of the Virasoro algebra. The Thomas-Whitehead gravity formalism extends the effective Polyakov action in such a way that the defining coadjoint element for the orbit becomes a dynamical field, viz the diffeomorphism field. In this work, we examine the constraint analysis and quantization of the Hamiltonian in the context of Thomas-Whitehead gravity using both the dynamical light-cone and the ADM formalisms of the metric. Constraint analysis is then repeated in a Minkowski background and with a dynamical action for the diffeomorphisms field arising from the Thomas-Whitehead action. Adding dynamics to the diffeomorphism field subsequently removes the vanishing Hamiltonians.

</details>


### [210] [Black hole solutions surrounded by an anisotropic fluid in a Kalb--Ramond two--form background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07052)

Abstract: We investigate static, spherically symmetric black hole spacetimes induced by the spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking of a Kalb--Ramond (KR) two-form field non--minimally coupled to gravity, coexisting with an anisotropic fluid. By adopting a general equation of state where the radial pressure relates to the energy density via $w_1 = -1$ and the tangential pressure via an arbitrary parameter $w_2$, we derive exact analytical solutions representing black holes surrounded by diverse matter fields, including dust ($w_2=0$), radiation ($w_2=1/3$), and dark energy-like distributions ($w_2=-1/2$). A rigorous analysis of curvature invariants confirms a genuine core singularity, while the global geometry and adherence to standard energy conditions are shown to be highly sensitive to the interplay between the KR coupling ($\ell$), the fluid density parameter ($K$), and $w_2$. Furthermore, we analyse null geodesics in detail to determine the photon sphere and shadow radii. Using the Gibbons--Werner geometrical approach and the Gauss-Bonnet theorem applied to the optical metric, we compute the weak deflection angle of light, demonstrating that both the KR field and the anisotropic fluid significantly enhance light bending, particularly in dark-energy-like backgrounds. Finally, we evaluate strong deflection limit (SDL) observables for the supermassive black holes Sgr A$^*$ and M87$^*$, revealing quantifiable deviations from standard Schwarzschild geometries. These results offer novel astrophysical signatures for constraining string-inspired KR gravity and anisotropic dark matter halos using current and future observations.

### [211] [Frozen Motion: Why Single Carrollian Scalars Cannot Propagate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07081)
*Andrew James Bruce*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一类在卡罗尔平面（Carrollian plane）上固有定义的一阶标量场理论，这些理论与卡罗尔联络（Carrollian connection）最小耦合，而非通过洛伦兹理论的极限获得。研究发现超平移对称性（supertranslations）迫使能量密度静态且动量密度为零，从而排除了场的传播，因此需要超越最小耦合的单场理论才能获得传播理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于构建固有定义在卡罗尔平面上的标量场理论，这些理论不依赖于洛伦兹理论的极限过程。通过探索卡罗尔几何（Carrollian geometry）与场理论的直接耦合，旨在理解扩展卡罗尔变换（extended Carrollian transformations）下的理论特性。

Method: 研究方法采用构建与卡罗尔联络最小耦合的一阶标量场理论，这些理论在卡罗尔平面上固有定义。理论构建基于扩展卡罗尔变换的对称性要求，包括超平移对称性，仅要求拉格朗日量（Lagrangians）与时空坐标无关。

Result: 研究发现超平移对称性（包含作为线性超平移的boost）迫使能量密度保持静态且动量密度为零，这排除了场在壳传播（on-shell propagation）的可能性。因此，最小耦合的单场理论无法支持传播现象。

Conclusion: 结论表明，要获得具有传播特性的理论，必须超越与几何最小耦合的单场理论框架。这为卡罗尔几何中构建传播场理论指明了新的研究方向。

Abstract: We investigate a class of first-order scalar field theories minimally coupled to a Carrollian connection that are defined intrinsically on the Carrollian plane, i.e., the theories are not defined via limits of Lorentzian theories. The theories built are invariant under the extended Carrollian transformations which include supertranslations. The symmetry allows for a large class of Lagrangians, independence of spacetime coordinates is all that is required. However, invariance under supertranslations (which include boosts as linear supertranslations) forces the energy density to be static and the momentum density to vanish -- this precludes on-shell propagation of fields. Thus, to have propagating theories, one must move beyond single field theories that are minimally coupled to the geometry.

### [212] [Bounding the number of spacetime dimensions from precessing black hole binaries with the third-generation gravitational-wave detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07102)
*Xu-Jie Zhu,Ji-Yu Song,Tao Zhu,Xin Zhang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究生成了一年内可被探测器网络探测到的进动双黑洞并合信号数据集。采用费希尔信息矩阵方法进行参数估计，并结合暗警报方法在层次贝叶斯框架下从星系目录中获取红移信息。

Result: 结果显示，双星系统的进动能显著提高光度距离的精度并缩小其红移范围，从而对额外维度产生更严格的约束。在68%置信水平下，约束结果为时空维度数D=3.99^{+0.07}_{-0.06}，额外维度的屏蔽尺度log₁₀(R_c/Mpc)>3.76。

Conclusion: 该结果比基于GWTC-3的分析提高了约一个数量级的精度，为未来第三代引力波观测探索额外维度效应提供了理论基础和预期灵敏度。

Abstract: In the theories with extra dimensions, gravitational waves can leak into extra dimensions, resulting in a reduction in the amplitude of the observed gravitational waves. Such an effect modifies the standard luminosity distance of gravitational wave sources, which enables constraining extra dimensions by measuring both the luminosity distance and redshift from gravitational wave events. The main purpose of this paper is to assess the capacity of the third-generation gravitational wave detector network, Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer, to constrain the theory of extra dimensions through observations of precessing binary black hole mergers. To this end, we generate a dataset of signals of precessing binary black hole mergers detectable by the detector network with one year of observations. We then employ the Fisher information matrix method for parameter estimation, together with a dark siren approach that obtains the redshift information from the galaxy catalog within a hierarchical Bayesian framework. Our results show that the precession in the binary system can significantly improve the precision of the luminosity distances and narrow their redshift ranges, thus leading to a tighter constraint on the extra dimensions. Based on this approach, we constrain the number of spacetime dimensions $D$ and the screening scale $R_{\rm c}$ of the extra dimensions, obtaining $D = 3.99^{+0.07}_{-0.06}$ and $\log_{10}(R_c/\mathrm{Mpc}) > 3.76$ at $68\%$ credible level. This result improves previous ones from an analysis with GWTC-3 by about one order of magnitude. This work provides theoretical foundations and projected sensitivities for future third-generation gravitational wave observations in exploring the effects of extra dimensions.

Abstract: We study the general black hole solutions of dimensionally reduced five-dimensional Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. The reduced theory contains gravity, electromagnetism and a scalar field, with nonlinear corrections to the action and nontrivial couplings. The solutions can be classified through mass and electric and magnetic charge. They present peculiar features with respect to the solutions of the standard Kaluza-Klein theory without Gauss-Bonnet corrections, like the existence of an extremal mass even in the neutral case. Also the thermodynamics is affected, for example, extremal black holes display nonvanishing temperature and entropy.

### [214] [Periodic Orbits and Gravitational Radiation from Extreme Mass-Ratio Inspirals as Probes of Black Hole Quantum Hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07168)
*Yiru Zhang,Meirong Tang,Zhaoyi Xu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了量子毛发（quantum hair）参数γ如何影响极端质量比旋近（EMRIs）的轨道动力学和引力波发射，发现γ会显著改变关键轨道半径和角动量，导致可观测的相位失配，为区分量子修正黑洞与经典黑洞提供了动力学特征。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究分析了量子毛发参数γ对极端质量比旋近（extreme mass-ratio inspirals, EMRIs）中测试体周期性轨道动力学的影响，基于有理数q分类探讨了量子修正对轨道行为的影响，并采用数值近似（Numerical Kludge）方法进行引力波计算。

Result: γ显著改变了两个关键圆形轨道的特征半径和角动量：边际束缚轨道（marginally bound orbit, MBO）和最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO），导致能量-角动量（E-L）相空间允许区域发生偏移。量子修正倾向于增强缩放-旋转（zoom-whirl）轨道行为，并改变有效时空势能，产生基本轨道频率的微小漂移，最终导致长时间信号中出现可观测的相位失配（phase dephasing）。

Conclusion: 这些结果为区分量子修正黑洞与经典史瓦西（Schwarzschild）黑洞提供了动力学特征，并为利用未来空间引力波天文台测试量子引力效应提供了理论动机。

Abstract: The classical no-hair theorem states that stationary black holes in general relativity can be completely described by only a small set of global parameters. Within this framework, no additional geometric structures are expected to persist outside the event horizon. However, quantum vacuum polarization may introduce small modifications to the near-horizon geometry, effectively giving rise to what is known as quantum hair. Such corrections may provide a possible window into the microscopic structure and thermodynamic properties of black holes. In this work, we examine how the quantum hair parameter γ influences the periodic orbital dynamics of test bodies in extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) and their associated gravitational-wave emission. We find that γ significantly modifies the characteristic radii and angular momenta of two important circular orbits, namely the marginally bound orbit (MBO) and the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO), leading to a shift in the allowed region of the energy-angular momentum (E-L) phase space. Based on the rational number q classification, we further show that quantum corrections tend to enhance the zoom-whirl orbital behavior.Gravitational-wave calculations using the Numerical Kludge approach indicate that quantum hair alters the effective spacetime potential, produces small drifts in the fundamental orbital frequencies, and consequently leads to observable phase dephasing in longduration signals. These results provide a dynamical signature for distinguishing quantum-corrected black holes from classical Schwarzschild ones and offer theoretical motivation for testing quantum gravity effects with future space-based gravitational-wave observatories.

Abstract: We adopt a general relativistic ray-tracing approach to study the shadows and polarization images of spherically symmetric Gauss-Bonnet (GB) black holes enveloped by geometrically thick accretion flows. Specifically, we adopt a phenomenological RIAF-like model and an analytical Hou disk model. In the RIAF-like model, increasing the GB coupling parameter $λ$ reduces both the size and brightness of the higher-order image, while increasing $θ$ alters the shape of the higher-order image and obscures the horizon's outline. The main difference between isotropic and anisotropic emission is that the latter produce distortion of the high-order image in the vertical direction, leading to an elliptical morphology. For the Hou disk model, due to specific regions being geometrically thinner with the conical approximation, the high-order images are narrower with the increase in $λ$ than the RIAF model. While increasing $θ$ enhances the brightness of the direct images outside the higher-order images, but hardly changes the size of the higher-order images, which is in sharp contrast to the RIAF model. Meanwhile, the Hou disk produces polarization patterns that trace the brightness configuration and are affected by $λ$ and $θ$, reflecting the intrinsic structure of spacetime. These results illustrate that intensity and polarization in thick-disk models provide probes of GB black holes and near-horizon accretion dynamics.

Conclusion: 该方法为高维引力理论中精确解的构造提供了系统框架，通过将真空爱因斯坦场方程简化为手征方程和Killing方程，并利用参数化技术和交换性假设，实现了从已知解生成新解的机制。

Abstract: In this work, we introduce a method for finding exact solutions to the vacuum Einstein field equations in higher dimensions from a given solution to the chiral equation. When considering a $n + 2$-dimensional spacetime with $n$ commutative Killing vectors, the metric tensor can take the form $\hat g = f ( ρ, ζ) ( d ρ^2 + d ζ^2 ) + g_{μν} ( ρ, ζ) d x^μd x^ν$. Then, the Einstein field equations in vacuum reduce to a chiral equation, $( ρg_{, z} g ^{-1} )_{, \bar z} + ( ρg_{, \bar z} g ^{-1} )_{, z} = 0$, and two differential equations, $( \ln f ρ^{1-1/n} )_{, Z} = \fracρ{2} \operatorname{tr} ( g_{, _Z} g^{-1} )^2$, where $g \in SL( n, \mathbb{R} )$ is the normalized matrix representation of $g_{μν}$, $z = ρ+ i ζ$ and $Z = z, \bar z$. We use the ansatz $g = g ( ξ^a )$, where the parameters $ξ^a$ depend on $z$ and $\bar z$ and satisfy a generalized Laplace equation, $( ρξ^a _{, z} )_{, \bar z} + ( ρξ^a _{, \bar z} )_{, z} = 0$. The chiral equation to the Killing equation, $A_{a , ξ^b} + A_{b , ξ^a} = 0$, where $A_a = g_{, ξ^a} g^{-1}$. Furthermore, we assume that the matrices $A_a$ commute with each other; in this way, they fulfill the Killing equation.

### [217] [Can Oscillatory and Persistent Nonlinearities Be Bridged in Black Hole Ringdown?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07469)
*Jun-Xi Shi,Zhen-Tao He,Jiageng Jiao,Jing-Qi Lai,Caiying Shao,Yu Tian,Hongbao Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了二次准正则模（QQNMs）与Christodoulou记忆效应之间的数学联系，通过依赖于残余黑洞参数的桥系数（bridge coefficients）建立桥梁，为未来空间引力波探测器测试广义相对论非线性区域提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二次准正则模（quadratic quasinormal modes, QQNMs）和Christodoulou记忆效应是引力波物理中的关键非线性现象，前者描述扰动黑洞的近区非线性响应，后者是出射辐射在零无穷远（null infinity）留下的非线性残余。这自然引发了一个问题：两者是否以及如何能够联系起来。

Method: 研究通过引入依赖于残余黑洞参数的桥系数（bridge coefficients）来建立两者之间的联系，主要关注在铃荡（ringdown）阶段残余黑洞参数的作用。

Result: 研究表明二次准正则模与Christodoulou记忆效应确实通过桥系数相互关联，这些系数主要取决于铃荡阶段的残余黑洞参数。未来空间引力波探测器有望探测这一关系。

Conclusion: 这些结果为测试引力理论提供了新途径，并为理解广义相对论（general relativity）的非线性区域提供了新视角，特别是通过桥系数连接了黑洞近区响应与无穷远记忆效应。

Abstract: Quadratic quasinormal modes (QQNMs) and Christodoulou memory effect are key nonlinear phenomena in gravitational wave physics. QQNMs characterize the near zone nonlinear response of a perturbed black hole, whereas the memory effect is a nonlinear remnant imprinted at null infinity by outgoing radiation. This naturally raises the question of whether and in what sense the two can be bridged. We show that they are related through bridge coefficients which depend primarily on remnant black hole parameters during ringdown. Future space-based gravitational-wave detectors can probe this relation. These results provide a new avenue for testing gravity and a fresh perspective on the nonlinear regime of general relativity.

</details>

### [219] [Josephson Effects in Slowly Rotating Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07553)
*Nurmukhammed Aytimbetov,Reggie C. Pantig,Ali Övgün,Bobomurat Ahmedov,Javlon Rayimbaev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在缓慢旋转的稳态时空中分析约瑟夫森效应（Josephson effect），明确区分了引力红移（gravitational redshift）和旋转框架拖曳（frame dragging）的不同作用。研究发现，在线性旋转近似下，红移效应与非旋转情况一致，而旋转效应仅通过位移矢量（shift vector）影响对空间相位传输或全局时间坐标同步敏感的系统配置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于深入理解引力红移和旋转框架拖曳在约瑟夫森物理中的不同作用，特别是在缓慢旋转的稳态时空中。这项工作受到先前研究[10.1007/JHEP02(2026)006]的启发，旨在为稳态时空中的超导电路提供一致的理论框架。

Method: 采用基于规范不变相位动力学和守恒电流的协变表述，在3+1分解框架内进行分析。研究限制在线性旋转参数a的一阶近似，并在欧拉/ZAMO（zero angular momentum observer）参考系中工作，采用缓慢旋转切片方法。

Result: 在采用的缓慢旋转切片中，流逝函数（lapse function）在$\mathcal{O}(a^2)$阶内保持其静态形式，而旋转效应通过位移矢量进入。约瑟夫森频率和直流临界电流的红移效应在线性阶内与非旋转情况相同。交流约瑟夫森关系在适当电压表述下保持红移结构，而在渐近（Killing时间）可观测量表述下简化为标准平直时空形式。

Conclusion: 研究结果清晰分离了流逝函数驱动的红移效应和位移矢量驱动的旋转贡献。旋转效应仅在对空间相位传输或全局时间坐标同步敏感的系统配置中变得相关，特别是射频驱动的干涉仪设置可获得与框架拖曳相关的萨格纳克型相位偏移，而直流通量量子约束在当前近似下在线性阶内保持不变。

Abstract: We investigate Josephson phenomena in a slowly rotating stationary spacetime, emphasizing the distinct roles of gravitational redshift and rotational frame dragging motivated by [10.1007/JHEP02(2026)006]. Using a covariant formulation based on gauge-invariant phase dynamics and conserved currents within a $3+1$ decomposition, we analyze both AC and DC Josephson effects and interferometric configurations. Restricting attention to linear order in the rotation parameter $a$, and working in the Eulerian/ZAMO frame, we show that in the slow-rotation slicing adopted here the lapse function agrees with its static (Schwarzschild-type) form up to $\mathcal{O}(a^2)$, while rotational effects enter through the shift vector. Consequently, redshift effects on Josephson frequencies and DC critical currents remain unchanged relative to the non-rotating case at $\mathcal{O}(a)$. The AC Josephson relation retains its redshifted structure when expressed in terms of proper voltages and reduces to the standard flat-spacetime form when formulated in terms of asymptotic (Killing-time) observables. Likewise, the DC critical current measured at infinity scales with a single power of the lapse function and is unaffected by rotation at linear order in the absence of azimuthal condensate momentum. Rotational effects become relevant only in configurations sensitive to spatial phase transport or to synchronization with respect to the global time coordinate. In particular, RF-driven interferometric setups can acquire Sagnac-type phase offsets associated with frame dragging, whereas the DC fluxoid constraint remains unshifted at linear order in the present approximation. Our results provide a clean separation between lapse-driven redshift effects and shift-driven rotational contributions in Josephson physics and furnish a consistent framework for superconducting circuits in stationary spacetimes.

### [220] [Black Hole Topologies and Geodesic Structures in Symmetric Teleparallel f(Q) Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07576)
*G. G. L. Nashed,A. Eid*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法采用$f(Q)$模型的幂律形式，分析(2+1)维静态圆对称时空，包括带电和不带电情况。通过计算曲率和非度量性标量（non-metricity scalar）来研究几何性质，并进行基于欧拉特征的拓扑分析（topological analysis）和测地线完备性（geodesic completeness）检验。

Result: 研究发现曲率和非度量性标量揭示了比广义相对论更强的中心奇点（central singularities）。视界半径随电荷参数增加而增大，而非度量性系数$c_4$或宇宙常数$Λ$的较高值倾向于合并或消除视界，减少其总数并改变时空的近原点结构。根据电荷存在与否，奇点可能或不可能通过测地线到达。

Conclusion: 研究结论确认了通过温度、熵和热容量计算得到的热力学稳定性。该研究突出了$f(Q)$引力在低维设置中的丰富结构，并为修正引力理论中奇点和黑洞拓扑性质提供了新见解。

Abstract: Black hole solutions are studied here within the symmetric teleparallel formulation of gravity, employing the $f(Q)$ model in which the gravitational dynamics are governed by the non-metricity scalar $Q$. We focus on static, circularly symmetric spacetimes in $(2+1)$-dimensions, analyzing both charged and uncharged cases. By adopting a power-law form for $f(Q)$, we derive exact black hole solutions and explore their thermodynamic and geometric properties. Curvature and non-metricity scalars reveal central singularities stronger than those in general relativity. we find that the horizon radii increase with the charge parameter while higher values of the non-metricity coefficient, $c_{4}$, or the cosmological constant $Λ$ tend to merge or eliminate horizons, reducing their total number and altering the near-origin structure of the spacetime. We perform a detailed topological analysis based on the Euler characteristic and examine the geodesic completeness of the spacetime. Our findings show that, depending on the presence of electric charge, the singularity may or may not be reachable by geodesics. The thermodynamic stability is confirmed via temperature, entropy, and heat capacity calculations. This study highlights the rich structure of $f(Q)$ gravity in lower-dimensional settings and offers new insights into the nature of singularities and black hole topologies in modified gravity theories.

### [221] [Non-minimally coupled Einstein-Yang-Mills black holes: periodic orbits and gravitational wave radiation in extreme mass ratio systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07610)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究系统分析了非最小耦合EYM黑洞时空中EMRIs的周期轨道特征和引力波辐射性质，通过轨道分类绘制典型周期轨道，并考察磁荷参数Q和非最小耦合常数ξ对轨道动力学的影响。

Conclusion: 这些结果为通过未来引力波观测区分不同黑洞模型提供了理论预测，表明非最小耦合EYM黑洞的轨道特性和引力波特征与标准黑洞模型存在可观测差异。

Abstract: Extreme mass ratio inspirals (EMRIs), as a core target for future space-based gravitational wave detection, offer crucial observational grounds for testing strong-field gravitational theories and classifying black holes through their orbital dynamics and gravitational wave radiation characteristics. This study systematically investigates the periodic orbit characteristics and gravitational wave radiation properties of EMRIs in the spacetime of a non-minimally coupled Einstein-Yang-Mills (EYM) black hole. The results show that as the magnetic charge parameter \(Q\) and the non-minimal coupling constant \(ξ\) increase, the radii of the marginally bound orbit (\(r_{\text{MBO}}\)) and the innermost stable circular orbit (\(r_{\text{ISCO}}\)) decrease significantly, with corresponding reductions in the orbital energy \(E\) and angular momentum \(L\). Furthermore, the allowable parameter space of energy and angular momentum (\(E\)-\(L\)) for bound orbits shifts towards the left. We then plot typical periodic orbits through orbit classification, finding that the non-minimal coupling effect suppresses the orbital contraction induced by the magnetic charge, leading to degeneracy of orbits with different \(Q\) values towards the Schwarzschild case, as well as phase shifts, amplitude enhancement, and period shortening in the gravitational waveforms with increasing \(Q\) and \(ξ\). These results provide theoretical predictions for distinguishing different black hole models through future gravitational wave observations.

Conclusion: 暖膨胀的弱耗散机制为引力波背景探测提供了更有利的条件，强调了膨胀场景特征在引力波产生中的关键作用。该研究为通过引力波观测检验统一暖膨胀和暗区（dark sector）的宇宙模型提供了新的理论依据。

Abstract: Previous work on the gravitational-wave background generated in a two-scalar-field cosmological model, in which warm inflation and the dark sector are unified within a single framework, has shown that the resulting spectrum could be potentially detectable by planned next-generation gravitational-wave observatories. In this work, we extend this analysis to the weak dissipation regime of warm inflation, highlighting how the features of the inflationary scenario play a crucial role in the production of gravitational waves. The full gravitational-wave energy spectrum is calculated using the formalism of continuous Bogoliubov coefficients. By comparing our results with those obtained in the strong dissipation regime and with the sensitivity curves of future detectors, we find that the weak dissipation regime improves the prospects for observational detection.
