### [223] [Scattering from compact objects: Debye series and Regge-Debye poles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07714)
*Mohamed Ould El Hadj*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了弯曲时空中无质量标量波在静态球对称均匀密度天体上的弹性散射，通过精确的德拜级数分解分析散射矩阵，确定了相关的Regge-Debye极点谱，并发现中子星类天体与超致密天体的极点谱存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解无质量标量波在弯曲时空中与无视界致密天体的弹性散射过程。通过引入精确的德拜级数分解，旨在分离直接表面反射与内部传输贡献，为散射过程提供自然的轨迹解释。

Method: 研究方法基于德拜级数分解，将散射矩阵分解为直接表面反射和涉及内部传输的贡献。该方法确定了复角动量平面中的Regge-Debye极点谱，并针对中子星类天体（R>3M）和超致密天体（R<3M）分别分析其极点谱特征。

Result: 研究结果显示，对于中子星类天体，极点谱包含两个分支：与表面匹配条件相关的表面波分支和与内部正则条件相关的宽共振分支。对于超致密天体，表面波分支持续存在，而内部共振部分分裂为宽共振和窄共振分支。德拜级数重建的散射振幅与直接分波计算结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在中子星类区域，Regge-Debye极点求和与分支切割贡献之间存在真正的竞争，高频下的彩虹状增强主要来自第一个内部传输贡献并由内部共振Regge-Debye极点主导。而在超致密区域，德拜振幅主要由极点主导。

Abstract: We investigate elastic scattering by a compact, horizonless body in curved spacetime, considering a massless scalar wave incident on a static, spherically symmetric, uniform-density star of radius $R$ and mass $M$ with a Schwarzschild exterior. We introduce an exact Debye-series decomposition of the scattering matrix, in the spirit of Debye expansions in Mie scattering. This decomposition separates direct surface reflection from contributions involving transmission into the interior and subsequent propagation, and admits a natural trajectory interpretation. We then determine the associated Regge-Debye pole spectrum in the complex angular-momentum plane. For neutron-star-like tenuities ($R>3M$), the spectrum exhibits two pole families: a surface-wave branch associated with the surface matching condition and a broad-resonance branch associated with the interior regularity condition. For ultracompact objects ($R<3M$), the surface-wave branch persists, while the interior-resonance sector splits into broad- and narrow-resonance branches.
  We next reconstruct the scattering amplitude from the Debye partial-wave contributions and find excellent agreement with direct partial-wave calculations. Finally, we develop complex angular-momentum representations order by order in the Debye series, making explicit how the pole families and non-pole sectors contribute to each Debye term. In the neutron-star-like regime, we find a genuine competition between Regge-Debye pole sums and branch-cut contributions, and show that, at high frequency, the rainbow-like enhancement already arises from the first interior-transmission contribution and is dominated by the interior-resonance Regge-Debye poles. By contrast, in the ultracompact regime, the Debye amplitudes are overwhelmingly pole dominated.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 针对两种不同世界线进行计算：类时圆形测地线（timelike circular geodesic）和静态世界线（static worldline），开发了多种数值和解析方法（numerical and analytical methods）来求解引力场微扰的格林函数。

Result: 格林函数在非焦散点（away from caustics）呈现4重奇点结构，在焦散点（at caustics）呈现2重奇点结构；引力场微扰在奇点附近出现物理振荡（physical oscillations），这是标量场微扰中不存在的现象。

Conclusion: 引力场微扰的格林函数具有与标量场不同的奇点结构和物理振荡特性，这些结果通过数值和解析方法的结合得以实现，为理解弯曲时空中引力扰动的传播提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We present a calculation of the full retarded Green functions of the Regge-Wheeler and Teukolsky equations obeyed by gravitational field perturbations of Schwarzschild spacetime. We perform the calculations for spacetime points along: (i) a timelike circular geodesic (where null-separated points are not at caustics); and (ii) a static worldline (where null-separated points are at caustics). These Green functions show a 4-fold singularity structure away from caustics, and 2-fold at caustics (similarly to the case of scalar field perturbations, which we also reproduce). Physical oscillations near the singularities appear in the gravitational case, which were not present in the scalar case. We obtain our results by developing various numerical and analytical methods.

### [225] [Evolution of density perturbations in fractional Newtonian cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07781)
*S. M. M. Rasouli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在分数牛顿宇宙学框架下分析密度扰动，推导并解析求解了物质主导时期的密度扰动增长方程，发现物理相关参数空间无动力学不稳定性。研究通过观测关系获得了分数参数α的观测上限约束，该约束比背景动力学和理论扰动考虑得出的限制更严格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索分数牛顿宇宙学（fractional Newtonian cosmology）框架下的密度扰动行为，旨在理解分数参数α如何影响宇宙结构形成，并检验该模型与标准宇宙学模型的区别。

Method: 采用流体流动方法（fluid-flow approach）研究物质主导时期（matter-dominated era），推导密度扰动增长方程并进行解析求解。利用观测关系，特别是萨克斯-沃尔夫方程（Sachs-Wolfe equation），获得分数参数α的观测约束。

Result: 密度扰动增长方程及其解明确依赖于分数参数α，在α=1的特殊极限下退化为标准牛顿和相对论对应形式。确认了增长和衰减扰动模式的存在，并聚焦于增长模式。获得了比背景动力学和理论扰动考虑更严格的α观测上限约束。

Conclusion: 分数宇宙学模型的背景演化可能接近ΛCDM模型，但其密度扰动通常携带独特的分数特征，原则上可通过观测进行检验。结合背景分析得到的独立约束，分数参数α被限制在狭窄且物理可行的参数空间区域内。

Abstract: In this work, density perturbations are investigated within the framework of a fractional Newtonian cosmology. Focusing on the matter-dominated era and employing the fluid-flow approach, the growth equation for density perturbations is derived and solved analytically. No dynamical instability arises in the physically relevant parameter space. It is shown that both the growth equation and its solutions depend explicitly on the fractional parameter $α$, and reduce to their standard Newtonian and relativistic counterparts in the special limit $α= 1$. The existence of both growing and decaying perturbative modes is confirmed, and, in accordance with current cosmological observations, the analysis is restricted to the growing mode. Using observational relations, in particular the Sachs--Wolfe equation, an observational upper bound on the parameter $α$ is obtained, which is more restrictive than the bounds inferred from background dynamics and theoretical perturbative considerations. When combined with the independent constraints arising from the background analysis, these results confine the fractional parameter $α$ to a narrow and physically viable region of parameter space. Overall, the present study indicates that, although the background evolution of the fractional model may closely mimic that of $Λ$CDM, the associated density perturbations generically carry a distinct fractional signature that can, in principle, be tested observationally.

</details>


### [226] [Threshold Temperature for Neutron-Star Emergence in a Gravitational Thermodynamic Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07951)
*Wen-Xiang Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究基于涌现引力（emergent gravity）的熵泛函框架，将中子星形成重新表述为体引力-热力学阈值问题，推导出静态致密天体的四个特征温度标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于涌现引力（emergent gravity）的熵泛函表述，其中时空被赋予热力学熵，通过极值化可导出爱因斯坦场方程。作者旨在将中子星形成重新概念化为体引力-热力学阈值问题。

Method: 方法结合了Jacobson-Padmanabhan的引力作为状态方程（equation of state）视角、Tolman红移（Tolman redshift）、Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff（TOV）流体静力学平衡，以及体结合能与热能平衡。研究提供了数学扩展推导、显式TOV和费米气体（Fermi-gas）公式及热力学一致性关系。

Result: 研究推导出静态致密天体的四个特征温度标度：牛顿位力阈值（Newtonian virial threshold）、无穷远处观测的红移阈值（redshifted threshold）、简并物质阈值（degenerate-matter threshold）和表面屏幕温度（surface screen temperature）。

Conclusion: 该工作通过引力-热力学框架重新表述中子星形成，建立了四个关键温度标度，为理解致密天体形成提供了新的热力学视角，并提供了完整的数学推导和一致性关系。

Abstract: Motivated by the entropy-functional formulation of emergent gravity, in which spacetime is endowed with a thermodynamic entropy that, upon extremization, yields the Einstein field equations, we reformulate the onset of a neutron star as a bulk gravitational-thermodynamic threshold problem. By combining the Jacobson-Padmanabhan perspective of gravity as an equation of state with Tolman redshift, Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff hydrostatics, and a bulk binding versus thermal energy balance, we derive four characteristic temperature scales for a static compact object: the Newtonian virial threshold, the redshifted threshold as observed at infinity, the degenerate-matter threshold, and the surface screen temperature.The paper supplies a mathematically expanded derivation, explicit TOV and Fermi-gas formulae, and thermodynamic consistency relations.

### [227] [The Interior of the Scalar Hairy Black Hole with Inverted Higgs Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08067)
*Xiao Yan Chew,Kok-Geng Lim,Dong-han Yeom*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值方法探索了具有非正定标量势的爱因斯坦-克莱因-戈登理论中渐近平坦毛状黑洞的内部结构，发现标量场和度规函数在视界内单调增加并在r→0时发散，确认了真正的曲率奇点存在，且未发现柯西视界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管毛状黑洞的外部特性（包括由倒置希格斯类势支持的HBHs的阴影成像）已被广泛研究，但其内部结构在很大程度上仍未被探索。在许多引力理论中，经典场的反作用可以显著消除柯西视界，这引发了关于强宇宙监督猜想有效性的重要问题。

Method: 通过从外视界向内数值积分场方程来检查毛状黑洞的内部结构。该方法涉及对爱因斯坦-克莱因-戈登理论中具有非正定标量势的渐近平坦毛状黑洞进行数值分析。

Result: 研究发现标量场和度规函数在视界内单调增加，并在r→0时发散。Ricci和Kretschmann标量在r=0处也发散，确认了真正的曲率奇点存在。未观察到度规函数的额外根，表明所考虑的电中性毛状黑洞中不存在柯西视界。

Conclusion: 弱能量条件在整个内部区域被违反，且违反程度随着视界处标量场的增加而变得更加显著。这些结果为毛状黑洞的全局结构及其对宇宙监督的影响提供了新的见解。

Abstract: We investigate the interior structure of asymptotically flat hairy black holes (HBHs) arising in the Einstein-Klein-Gordon theory with nonpositive-definite scalar potentials, where nontrivial scalar hair exists at the event horizon. While exterior properties, including shadow imaging for HBHs supported by an inverted Higgs-like potential have been extensively investigated, their interior structure remains largely unexplored. In many gravitational theories, backreaction of classical fields can significantly eliminate the Cauchy horizon, which is known to be highly unstable due to the mass inflation effect, raising important questions regarding the validity of the Strong Cosmic Censorship conjecture. These considerations motivate us to examine the interior structure of HBHs by numerically integrating the field equations inward from the outer horizon. We find that the scalar field and the metric functions increase monotonically inside the horizon and diverge as $r \rightarrow 0$. The Ricci and Kretschmann scalars also diverge at $r=0$, confirming the presence of a genuine curvature singularity. No additional root of the metric function is observed, indicating the absence of a Cauchy horizon in the electrically neutral HBHs considered here. Furthermore, the weak energy condition is violated throughout the interior region, and the degree of violation becomes more pronounced as the scalar field at the horizon increases. These results provide new insight into the global structure of HBHs and their implications for cosmic censorship.

### [228] [Phase Transitions, Geodesic Structure, and Thermodynamic Properties Measurement of Einstein-Maxwell-Power Yang-Mills Black Hole Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08222)
*Abdelmalek Bouzenada,Allan. R. P. Moreira,Shi-Hai Dong,Guo-Hua Sun,Muhammad Sharif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-幂律杨-米尔斯黑洞模型，分析其几何结构、热力学性质及非线性杨-米尔斯参数对时空几何、粒子动力学和相变临界点的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索通过包含幂律杨-米尔斯不变量（power-law Yang-Mills invariant）对标准爱因斯坦-杨-米尔斯理论进行非线性推广的黑洞模型，分析电磁荷和非线性杨-米尔斯参数对黑洞性质的影响。

Method: 首先通过度规函数f(r)分析时空几何，研究电磁荷和非线性杨-米尔斯参数对视界结构、因果结构和引力势的修正。随后通过零测地线和类时测地线研究光子和有质量粒子的动力学，确定有效势、光子球半径及相关黑洞阴影。使用李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）量化圆形光子轨道的稳定性，计算有质量粒子的最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）。从热力学角度计算黑洞质量、霍金温度、贝肯斯坦-霍金熵、热容和吉布斯自由能等主要热力学量。

Result: 非线性杨-米尔斯参数显著影响时空几何、粒子动力学和热力学相结构，改变稳定性区域和相变临界点的位置。热容的发散指示二阶相变的发生，而吉布斯自由能分析识别不同热力学构型之间可能的一阶相变。

Conclusion: 研究表明，非线性杨-米尔斯参数强烈影响爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-幂律杨-米尔斯黑洞的几何结构、粒子动力学和热力学相结构，为理解非线性杨-米尔斯理论中的黑洞物理提供了重要见解。

Abstract: In this work, we test the geometrical structure and thermodynamic properties of the Einstein-Maxwell-Power-Yang-Mills black hole (BH) models, which constitute a nonlinear generalization of the standard Einstein-Yang-Mills theory through the inclusion of a power-law Yang-Mills invariant. Also, we begin by analyzing the spacetime geometry via the metric function $f(r)$ and examine the modifications induced by the electromagnetic charge and nonlinear Yang-Mills parameter on the horizon structure, causal structure, and gravitational potential. Subsequently, the dynamics of photons and massive particles are explored through the study of null and timelike geodesics, allowing the determination of the effective potential, photon sphere radius, and associated BH shadow. Also, the stability of circular photon orbits is quantified using the Lyapunov exponent, which characterizes the timescale of orbital instability and provides a direct link to observable photon ring features. For massive particles, the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) is calculated, illustrating the influence of BH parameters on the dynamics of accretion disks. From the thermodynamic viewpoint, we compute the principal thermodynamic quantities, including the BH mass, Hawking temperature, Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, heat capacity, and Gibbs free energy, to assess both local and global stability of the system. The divergence of the heat capacity signals the occurrence of second-order phase transitions, whereas the Gibbs free energy analysis identifies possible first-order phase transitions between distinct thermodynamic configurations. In this context, our results demonstrate that the nonlinear Yang-Mills parameter strongly affects the spacetime geometry, particle dynamics, and thermodynamic phase structure, shifting the location of stability regions and critical points associated with phase transitions.

### [229] [Gravitational waves in metric-affine bumblebee gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08310)
*A. A. Araújo Filho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在度规-仿射（metric-affine）大黄蜂模型框架下，分析了引力波的传播与发射特性，其中自发洛伦兹对称性破缺源于矢量场获得非零真空期望值。研究推导了修正的色散关系，分析了极化特性，构建了推迟格林函数，并评估了双黑洞系统的引力辐射，为通过引力波观测约束洛伦兹破缺参数提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索洛伦兹对称性破缺（Lorentz symmetry breaking）对引力波（gravitational waves）传播与发射的影响。具体而言，旨在分析度规-仿射（metric-affine）大黄蜂模型（bumblebee model）中，由矢量场真空期望值引发的自发洛伦兹破缺如何修正引力波的传播特性，并评估其对引力波观测的潜在影响。

Method: 研究方法基于线性化理论的几何光学极限（geometric-optics limit）。首先推导了控制引力子模式（graviton modes）的修正色散关系（modified dispersion relation），该关系依赖于波矢相对于背景矢量的方向。随后分析了类时（timelike）和类空（spacelike）洛伦兹破缺真空构型下的极化特性。通过构建与修正波动算子相关的推迟格林函数（retarded Green function），确定了局域源产生的辐射区（radiation-zone）场。

Result: 研究结果表明，在类时和类空构型下，仅有两个独立的张量模式传播，但其传播特性和张量结构依赖于背景场的方向。类时构型中，洛伦兹破缺效应表现为修正的传播速度和整体振幅重整化（amplitude renormalization），导致推迟时间偏移，但保持了波形的四极矩结构。类空构型则引入了对四极矩振幅的各向异性修正，以及一个与四极矩矩三阶时间导数成正比的额外贡献。通过对双黑洞系统引力辐射的评估，利用GW170817/GRB 170817A的多信使（multimessenger）界限和引力波观测的波形一致性要求，可以估计对洛伦兹破缺组合参数ξb²的观测约束。

Conclusion: 该研究系统分析了度规-仿射大黄蜂模型中洛伦兹对称性破缺对引力波传播与发射的影响。研究揭示了类时和类空真空构型下引力波传播特性的不同修正模式，为利用引力波观测（特别是多信使事件和波形一致性分析）约束洛伦兹破缺参数提供了具体的理论预测和可观测特征。

Abstract: We study the propagation and emission of gravitational waves in the metric-affine formulation of the bumblebee model, where spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking arises from a vector field acquiring a nonvanishing vacuum expectation value. Working in the geometric-optics limit of the linearized theory, we derive the modified dispersion relation governing the graviton modes and show that it depends on the orientation of the wave vector relative to the background vector. The polarization sector is examined for timelike and spacelike configurations of the Lorentz-violating vacuum. In both cases only two independent tensor modes propagate, although their propagation properties and tensor structure depend on the orientation of the background field. We then construct the retarded Green function associated with the modified wave operator and determine the radiation-zone produced by localized sources. In the timelike configuration the Lorentz-violating effects appear through a modified propagation speed and an overall amplitude renormalization, leading to a shifted retarded time while preserving the quadrupole structure of the waveform. In contrast, the spacelike sector introduces anisotropic corrections to the quadrupole amplitude together with an additional contribution proportional to the third time derivative of the quadrupole moment. As an astrophysical application, the gravitational radiation emitted by a circular binary black hole system is evaluated, allowing observational constraints on the Lorentz-violating combination $ξb^{2}$ to be estimated using multimessenger bounds from GW170817/GRB~170817A and waveform consistency requirements from gravitational wave observations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将霍恩德斯基理论扩展至帕拉蒂尼形式，其中度规张量和对称联络先验独立。研究动机在于探索度规和联络的变换不变性，以及该理论框架在引力理论中的潜在应用。

Method: 采用帕拉蒂尼方法，引入度规的变形变换（disformal transformation）和联络的新变换，构建形式不变的作用量泛函。通过引入不变度规和联络，将理论约化为纯度量形式，并在第二部分考虑简单宇宙学模型。

Result: 理论在壳上约化为霍恩德斯基引力的度量子类——动力学引力编织。不变度规和联络的构建导致纯度量理论。宇宙学模型显示存在能再现晚期宇宙加速膨胀的模型，渐近趋向德西特相（de Sitter phase）。

Conclusion: 扩展的帕拉蒂尼霍恩德斯基理论可约化为度量理论，其宇宙学应用显示与k-本质型理论（k-essence-type theories）的潜在联系，并能再现晚期宇宙加速膨胀，为后续研究提供动机。

Abstract: In this paper, we extend Horndeski's theory into the Palatini approach, assuming that the metric tensor and the (symmetric) connection are a priori independent objects. We introduce an additional transformation of the connection and write down the action functional being form-invariant under both the disformal transformation of the metric and the new transformation of the connection. We show that such a theory reduces on-shell to a metric subclass of Horndeski's gravity called kinetic gravity braiding. We also introduce an invariant metric and connection, and demonstrate that quantities defined in such a way lead to a metric theory. In the second part of the paper, we consider a simple cosmological model within the theory and explore its potential links with $ k$-essence-type theories, with a non-trivial coupling between the scalar field and the matter part of the action in the Einstein frame. We show that there exists a model that reproduces late-time cosmic acceleration, approaching asymptotically the de Sitter phase, motivating further study of the theories.

### [231] [Local Origin of Hidden Symmetry in Rotating Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08408)
*Hyeong-Chan Kim*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究证明Kerr几何的隐藏对称性和可分离性源于爱因斯坦场方程对旋转时空的局部必然结果，无需假设可分离性或全局边界条件，仅通过局部平衡条件即可推导出Kerr型解的核心运动学结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 混合场方程强制径向和角向扇区之间的刚性投影对齐，一致性要求导致Schwarzian导数的相等，从而将局部解普遍分类为Möbius、指数和三角分支。全局正则性一般排除三角分支，精确留下Kerr型扇区并涌现Petrov D型结构。

Abstract: We show that the hidden symmetry and separability characteristic of Kerr geometry arise as an inevitable \emph{local} consequence of the Einstein equations for rotating spacetimes. Without assuming separability, algebraic speciality, Killing-Yano symmetry, or global boundary conditions, we analyze general stationary and axisymmetric geometries in a locally non-rotating orthonormal frame. Imposing a minimal physical requirement, the local equilibrium condition, we find that the mixed Einstein equations enforce a rigid projective alignment between the radial and angular sectors. This result does not rely on vacuum: the mixed equations are insensitive to the detailed form of a comoving stress-energy tensor. Consistency then requires equality of Schwarzian derivatives, leading to a universal classification of local solutions into Möbius, exponential, and trigonometric branches. Global regularity generically excludes the trigonometric branch, leaving precisely the Kerr-type sector and the emergence of Petrov type D structure. This provides a structural precursor to Kerr uniqueness, demonstrating that the kinematical core of Kerr geometry is encoded locally within the Einstein equations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate a simple $f(R, T_φ)$ gravity model coupled to a scalar field and demonstrate that the theory admits classical degenerate metric solutions, analogous to those known in general relativity. In particular, we identify a class of solutions that exhibits a smooth transition from a Euclidean to a Lorentzian domain, thus yielding a classical dynamical realization of signature change.

### [233] [Black hole shadows in nonminimally coupled Weyl connection gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08441)
*Cláudio Gomes,Margarida Lima,Francisco S. N. Lobo,Luís F. D. da Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析非最小耦合Weyl联络引力理论中的黑洞阴影，利用事件视界望远镜对Sgr A*的观测约束，对描述时空非度量性的Weyl参数设置了观测界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索超越黎曼框架的引力理论，特别是非最小耦合Weyl联络引力理论，该理论通过Weyl矢量场描述时空非度量性（non-metricity）。研究旨在利用黑洞阴影观测数据来约束这类扩展引力理论中的参数。

Method: 方法包括：在非最小耦合Weyl联络引力理论框架下，计算修正的Schwarzschild-like和Reissner-Nordström-like解对应的阴影半径；将这些计算结果与事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）对Sgr A*的观测约束进行对比；假设观测者距离$r_O = 4.1\times 10^{10}M$，在$2σ$置信水平下要求理论预测与观测一致。

Result: 研究结果为Weyl参数设置了观测界限：模型I要求$ω\gtrsim 10^{11.7}M$，模型II要求$ω\gtrsim 10^{10.5}M$，模型III显示$ω\sim 10^{12}M$。这些结果表明，当前视界尺度的成像观测已经能够对时空非度量性设定有意义的限制。

Conclusion: 结论强调黑洞阴影观测作为扩展引力动力学探针的强大能力，并建立了基于Weyl的理论与当前天体物理数据之间的直接联系。该工作展示了如何利用观测数据约束超越广义相对论的引力理论参数。

Abstract: We study black hole shadows in nonminimally coupled Weyl connection gravity, a metric-affine extension of general relativity in which spacetime is described by a metric and a Weyl vector field encoding non-metricity. Despite going beyond the Riemannian framework, the presence of a non-dynamical Weyl vector ensures second-order field equations. The theory admits Schwarzschild- and Reissner--Nordström-like solutions modified by a Weyl integration constant that parametrizes deviations from General Relativity. By computing the corresponding shadow radii and confronting them with the Event Horizon Telescope constraints on Sgr A*, we place observational bounds on the Weyl parameter. Assuming an observer distance $r_O = 4.1\times 10^{10}M$ and requiring consistency at the $2σ$ level, we obtain $ω\gtrsim 10^{11.7}M$ (model I), $ω\gtrsim 10^{10.5}M$ (model II), and $ω\sim 10^{12}M$ (model III). Our results show that present horizon-scale imaging already sets meaningful limits on spacetime non-metricity. This work highlights the power of black hole shadow observations as probes of extended gravitational dynamics and establishes a direct link between Weyl-based theories and current astrophysical data.

</details>


### [234] [A dynamical approach to General Relativity based on proper time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08568)
*Jaume de Haro*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究将不变间隔$ds^2$置于引力相互作用的核心，将其解释为具有直接物理意义的固有时微分而非纯几何对象。从费马原理推广到有质量粒子出发，结合伽利略自由落体普适性，推导出静态引力场中的$ds^2$形式，并通过洛伦兹不变性扩展到运动物质系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在重新诠释引力相互作用的基础，将不变间隔$ds^2$从纯几何对象转变为具有直接物理意义的固有时微分。这一视角转变旨在为广义相对论提供更物理化的基础，避免将其场方程视为纯粹的几何假设。

Method: 方法基于费马原理（Fermat's principle）向有质量粒子的推广，即自由落体沿固有时极值轨迹运动（类时运动对应局部极大值）。结合伽利略自由落体（Galilean free fall）的普适性，推导静态引力场中的$ds^2$形式，再通过洛伦兹不变性（Lorentz invariance）扩展到运动物质系统。

Result: 通过此程序推导的不变量与谐和规范（harmonic gauge）下广义相对论（General Relativity）的弱场极限相匹配。在线性化区域中，理论结构已包含其非线性完备的种子：任何向强引力场的动力学一致扩展必然涉及里奇张量（Ricci tensor）。

Conclusion: 爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein's field equations）并非作为假设的几何定律出现，而是确保能动量守恒（energy momentum conservation）和引力相互作用自洽性所需的唯一协变闭合。这一视角为广义相对论提供了基于物理原理而非纯几何假设的基础。

Abstract: This work places the invariant $ds^2$ at the center of the gravitational interaction, interpreting it not as a purely geometric object but as the differential of proper time, endowed with direct physical meaning. Starting from the extension of Fermat's principle to massive particles--namely, the requirement that freely falling bodies follow trajectories that extremize proper time, which for timelike motion corresponds to a local maximum--and invoking the universality of Galilean free fall, we derive the form of $ds^2$ in a static gravitational field. Lorentz invariance then provides the natural framework to extend this result to systems involving moving matter. The invariant derived through this procedure matches the weak-field limit of General Relativity formulated in the harmonic gauge.
  Within this linearized regime, we show that the structure of the theory already contains the seeds of its non-linear completion: any dynamically consistent extension to strong gravitational fields necessarily involves the Ricci tensor. From this viewpoint, Einstein's field equations appear not as a postulated geometric law, but as the unique covariant closure required to ensure energy momentum conservation and the self consistency of the gravitational interaction.

</details>

TL;DR: 该论文指出Harada最近宣布的Kerr-Schild解实际上是已知NUT解的一个等距变换版本。

Conclusion: Harada声称的新解实际上是已有NUT解的一个等距版本，并非真正的新解。

Abstract: Harada's recently announced Kerr-Schild solution of Einstein's equations in general relativity [Phys. Rev. D {\bf 112}, 024020 92025)] is identified as isometric with one of the well-known NUT solutions.

### [236] [Secondary gravitational waves against a strong gravitational wave in the Bianchi VI universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08628)
*Konstantin E. Osetrin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种构建动态引力波场模型的固有时方法，用于在Bianchi VI宇宙真空精确波解背景下构造次级引力波的解析模型，并证明了存在使微扰解稳定的引力波参数连续统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在发展一种构建动态引力波场模型的固有时方法（proper-time method），以解决在精确引力波解背景下构造次级引力波解析模型的问题。

Method: 采用固有时方法，在特权波坐标系（privileged wave coordinate system）中，以Bianchi VI宇宙真空爱因斯坦方程的精确波解为背景，将次级引力波构造为线性化场方程的微扰解。利用测试粒子在强引力波背景下的固有时关系，从场方程的相容性条件获得次级引力波度规分量的解析形式。

Result: 从场方程获得了包含在次级引力波度规小修正中的函数的常微分方程显式形式及其解。证明了存在一个引力波参数连续统（continuum of gravitational wave parameters），使得微扰解保持稳定。

Conclusion: 固有时方法成功构建了次级引力波的解析模型，并在Bianchi VI宇宙背景下证明了稳定微扰解的存在性，为动态引力波场建模提供了有效的解析框架。

Abstract: A proper-time method for constructing models of dynamic gravitational-wave fields is presented. Using the proper-time method, analytical (not numerical) models of secondary gravitational waves are constructed as perturbative solutions of linearized field equations against the background of the exact wave solution of Einstein's equations for the vacuum in the Bianchi VI universe in a privileged wave coordinate system. Relations for the proper time of test particles against the background of a strong gravitational wave are used. The analytical form of the metric components for secondary gravitational waves is found from compatibility conditions for the field equations. From the field equations, an explicit form of ordinary differential equations and their solutions is obtained for functions included in small corrections to the metric for secondary gravitational waves. It is shown that there exists a continuum of gravitational wave parameters for which the perturbative solutions are stable.

</details>


### [237] [A Deep Learning Framework for Amplitude Generation of Generic EMRIs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08635)
*Yan-bo Zeng,Jian-dong Zhang,Yi-Ming Hu,Jianwei Mei*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于卷积编码器-解码器架构的快速全局拟合方法，用于高效生成极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）的Teukolsky振幅，通过迁移学习策略和渐进训练实现了毫秒级波形生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间引力波探测器的主要目标之一是探测极端质量比旋进（Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals, EMRIs），其数据分析需要既准确又快速的波形模型。主要挑战在于为通用（偏心且倾斜的）Kerr轨道快速生成Teukolsky振幅，传统方法在四维参数空间中建模约10^5个谐波模式时计算成本过高。

Method: 引入卷积编码器-解码器（convolutional encoder-decoder）架构，用于Teukolsky振幅的快速端到端全局拟合。采用迁移学习（transfer learning）策略减少训练数据集规模，模型从最简单的Schwarzschild圆轨道逐步训练到通用Kerr轨道。

Result: 基于半解析后牛顿（Post-Newtonian）数据集获得代理模型（surrogate model），完整谐波振幅可在毫秒内生成。通用轨道的模式分布误差中位数约为10^{-3}，表明该框架适用于构建高效的EMRI波形模型。

Conclusion: 该框架能够有效构建极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）的高效波形模型，解决了传统方法在计算成本方面的限制，为空间引力波探测的数据分析提供了可行的技术方案。

Abstract: One of the main targets for space-borne gravitational wave detectors is the detection of Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs). The data analysis of EMRIs requires waveform models that are both accurate and fast. The major challenge for the fast generation of such waveforms is the generation of the Teukolsky amplitudes for generic (eccentric and inclined) Kerr orbits. The requirement for the modeling of $\sim10^5$ harmonic modes across a four-dimensional parameter space makes traditional approaches, including direct computation or dense interpolation, computationally prohibitive. To overcome this issue, we introduce a convolutional encoder-decoder architecture for a fast and end-to-end global fitting of the Teukolsky amplitudes. We also adopt a transfer learning strategy to reduce the size of the training dataset, and the model is trained gradually from the simplest Schwarzschild circular orbits to generic Kerr orbits step by step. Within this framework, we obtain a surrogate model based on a semi-analytical Post-Newtonian dataset, and the full harmonic amplitudes can be generated within milliseconds, while the median mode-distribution error for generic orbits is approximately $\sim10^{-3}$. This result indicates that the framework is viable for constructing efficient waveform models for EMRIs.

</details>


### [238] [Circular stable orbits in $f(R)$ realistic static and spherically-symmetric spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08637)
*Néstor Rivero González,Álvaro de la Cruz Dombriz,Gonzalo J. Olmo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在二次Starobinsky模型$f(R)=aR^2$（$a<0$）的度量$f(R)$引力理论中，中子星时空的测地线结构。研究发现，大质量粒子存在离散的稳定圆形轨道带，而光子轨道在参数范围内不存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究度量$f(R)$引力理论中，特别是二次Starobinsky模型下，中子星时空的测地线结构。该研究关注修正引力理论对致密天体周围轨道动力学的影响。

Method: 通过数值求解修正的Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff（TOV）系统，获得多种现实状态方程下的中子星解。使用有效势方法分析测地线结构，并通过强制执行完整的连接条件（junction conditions）将内部解与外部真空几何匹配。

Result: 研究发现稳定圆形轨道以离散的径向带形式出现，被禁带区域分隔。主稳定带对恒星中心压强、状态方程和参数$|a|$的大小敏感。在稳定带外，大质量粒子存在束缚但不稳定的进动轨迹以及无界运动。对于零测地线，在研究的参数范围内未发现中子星外存在光子球（photon spheres）。

Conclusion: 在二次Starobinsky模型的度量$f(R)$引力中，中子星时空表现出独特的测地线结构：大质量粒子轨道呈现离散的稳定带特征，而光子轨道行为与广义相对论预测存在差异。这些特征对参数$a$、状态方程和恒星结构敏感。

Abstract: We investigate the geodesic structure of realistic static and spherically symmetric spacetimes embedding neutron stars in metric $f(R)$ gravity, focusing on the quadratic Starobinsky model $f(R)=aR^2$ with $a<0$. Neutron-star solutions are obtained by numerically solving the modified Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff system for several realistic equations of state. Such solutions are then matched consistently to the exterior vacuum geometry by enforcing the full set of junction conditions required in metric $f(R)$ theories. Using an effective potential approach, we show that stable circular orbits appear in discrete radial bands separated by forbidden regions, with a dominant principal band of stability that depends sensitively on the stellar central pressure, the equation of state, and the magnitude of the parameter $|a|$. Outside the stable bands, massive particles can have bound but unstable precessing trajectories as well as unbounded motions. On the other hand, for null geodesics, we find no evidence for photon spheres outside the neutron star within the parameter range studied.

</details>

Abstract: This article is devoted to the investigation of the observational properties of the Schwarzschild black hole (BH) surrounded by a dark matter (DM) halo. Our study commences with a brief review of spacetime, including the horizon structure and curvature invariants, which are the Ricci scalar, the square of the Ricci tensor, and the Kretschmann scalar. Subsequently, we explore the massive and massless particle dynamics around the Schwarzschild BH surrounded by a dark matter halo, including the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) and photon sphere radii. It was found that the radius of the ISCO increases under the influence of the spacetime parameters. Additionally, we investigate the weak gravitational lensing with the assumption that the BH is surrounded by a uniform and non-uniform plasma. Finally, we examine the impact of a plasma on the BH shadow and employ Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) observational data to constrain the BH's parameters.

Abstract: Black holes are the most efficient scramblers in nature. ### [241] [Enhancing superconductivity using thermal bosons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06796)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索超导体与热玻色子强耦合对超导临界温度的增强机制，解决传统方法中密度涨落与玻色子诱导吸引力之间的竞争问题，为高温超导材料设计提供理论指导。

Result: 研究预测了临界温度在广泛相互作用范围内的稳健提升，发现了临界温度对玻色子质量的非平凡依赖关系，并建立了由凝聚态或热态玻色子驱动的增强超导性相图。

Conclusion: 该工作为增强超导临界温度提供了理论框架，指出了在冷原子系统和范德华材料异质结构中的电子-激子混合物等可能的实验实现途径。

Abstract: We investigate how the strong coupling of a superconductor to thermal bosons can enhance its superconducting critical temperature. To tackle this problem, we use a renormalization group approach that allows us to describe the competition between density fluctuations and the build-up of boson-induced attraction between fermions. Capturing the mutual influence of bosonic and fermionic sectors, the self-consistent renormalization group framework predicts a robust increase of the critical temperature across a wide range of interactions. We find a nontrivial dependence of the critical temperature on the boson mass and we establish a phase diagram for enhanced superconductivity driven by bosons being either in the condensed or thermal state. We outline possible experimental realizations in cold atomic systems and discuss implementations using electron-exciton mixtures in van der Waals material heterostructures.

### [242] [A Compact XOR Gate Implemented With a Single Straintronic Magnetic Tunnel Junction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06818)
*Supriyo Bandyopadhyay*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于单个应变电子磁隧道结（straintronic MTJ）的XOR逻辑门设计，显著减小了器件尺寸，具有非易失性、低功耗（~225 aJ）和快速开关（~200 ps）特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: XOR逻辑门在加密、二进制加法、错误检测等应用中广泛使用，但传统实现需要多个逻辑开关或门电路，导致器件尺寸大、逻辑密度低。需要开发更紧凑、高效的XOR门设计。

Method: 采用单个应变电子磁隧道结（straintronic magnetic tunnel junction）构建XOR门，通过1 MTJ-1 CMOS架构实现级联。CMOS器件不参与门动态，仅提供增益以实现逻辑电平恢复、扇出和输入输出隔离。

Result: 该设计实现了约200 ps的开关时间和约225 aJ的每门操作能耗。与传统全晶体管XOR设计相比，能耗降低了一个数量级，同时显著减小了器件尺寸。

Conclusion: 单应变电子磁隧道结XOR门设计具有非易失性，适用于非冯·诺依曼架构和内存处理器等应用。其紧凑的1 MTJ-1 CMOS架构在能耗和尺寸方面相比传统设计具有显著优势。

Abstract: The XOR Boolean logic gate is widely used in many applications such as encryption (XOR ciphers), binary addition (half- and full-adders), error detection (parity bits), etc. but is challenging to construct because of its demanding conditional dynamics. It typically requires multiple logic switches or other types of gates, which results in a large gate footprint and low logic density. Here, we present the design of an XOR gate with a single straintronic magnetic tunnel junction which reduces the footprint dramatically. Such a gate is non-volatile and hence suitable for non-von-Neumann architectures, processor-in-memory, etc. The switching time of the gate is ~200 ps and the energy dissipation per gate operation is ~225 aJ. Cascading of successive stages is accomplished via a CMOS device which plays no role in the gate dynamics but is needed for gain to provide logic level restoration, fan-out and isolation between input and output. This 1 MTJ-1 CMOS design has an energy dissipation that is an order of magnitude smaller than what has been reported for traditional all-transistor XOR designs.

</details>

Abstract: We present a theory of a flux-tunable superconducting qubit, the "Fraunhofer qubit," based on the Fraunhofer interference in a wide ballistic Josephson junction. As magnetic flux threads the junction, the Josephson potential is effectively averaged over a phase window proportional to flux. For perfectly transmitting junctions, as flux approaches one flux quantum h/2e, the flux averaging transforms the potential near its minimum from a quadratic to a triangular shape, resulting in significantly enhanced anharmonicity. This enhancement persists for junctions with lower transparency conducting channels. Microscopic tight-binding simulations that include inhomogeneous electrostatic potential and disorder confirm the enhancement of anharmonicity. These results establish a framework for flux control in hybrid superconducting circuits, providing an operating point where anharmonicity and charge-noise protection can be optimally balanced.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统微磁模型（micromagnetic models）通常无法以网格无关（grid independent）的方式再现超快退磁（ultrafast demagnetization）过程，这限制了数值模拟的准确性。当磁性材料受到飞秒（femtosecond）激发时，其磁化动力学（magnetization dynamics）处于远离平衡态（far-from-equilibrium）的状态，需要新的建模方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种非平衡热场（non-equilibrium thermal field），其特性取决于原子自旋翻转概率（atomic spin flip probabilities）。在假设每个自旋翻转（spin flip）相当于一个角动量量子（quantum of angular momentum）的前提下，该方法能够实现数千开尔文量级的等效温度（equivalent temperatures）。

Result: 该方法能够在多种晶胞尺寸（cell sizes）下定量再现退磁（demagnetization）过程。提出的方法可以进一步优化和扩展，实现网格无关（grid independent）和多尺度（multiscale）的超快磁化动力学（ultrafast magnetization dynamics）建模。

Conclusion: 基于非平衡热场（non-equilibrium thermal field）的建模方法成功解决了传统微磁模型（micromagnetic models）在超快退磁（ultrafast demagnetization）模拟中的网格依赖性问题，为实现网格无关（grid independent）的多尺度磁化动力学建模提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Far-from-equilibrium magnetization dynamics can be accessed when a magnetic material is subject to a femtosecond excitation, such as an optical laser or an electric current. Numerically, the demagnetization of magnetic materials is typically modeled by atomistic spin dynamics. Micromagnetic models generally fail to reproduce ultrafast demagnetization in a grid independent manner. Here, we propose a non-equilibrium thermal field whose features depend on atomic spin flip probabilities. Under the assumption that each spin flip is equivalent to a quantum of angular momentum, equivalent temperatures on the order of thousands of Kelvin are achieved. Demagnetization is quantitatively reproduced for several cell sizes. The presented approach can be further refined and extended towards a grid-independent and multiscale modeling of ultrafast magnetization dynamics.

Abstract: Altermagnets with compensated spin structures and nonrelativistic spin splitting have emerged as a new class of magnetic materials. Magnetic measurements show that the crystals are isotropically paramagnetic. Interestingly, resistivity is rather pressure sensitive: at 44 GPa, a clear metal-insulator transition occurs. Hybrid functional calculations reveal that applying pressure significantly increases the Hubbard U value, driving a phase transition from a paramagnetic metal to an altermagnetic metal, and eventually to an altermagnetic insulator. These findings suggest that tuning external pressure effectively modulates the magnetic ground state of OsO2, providing a pathway to realize altermagnetism in this material.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析系统在低频辐射下的Drude吸收加热效应，研究稳态平衡的双稳态特性，考察温度、电流及激子或三子发光强度等可观测量在两态间的跃变行为。

Conclusion: 过渡金属二硫化物单层中的三子-激子系统在低频辐射加热下表现出双稳态行为，这种动态平衡特性可通过温度、电流和发光强度等物理量的跃变来观测，为相关光电应用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the dynamic equilibrium between trions and excitons in monolayers of transition metal dichalcogenides in the presence of resident charge carriers and continuous photogeneration of excitons. We show that heating of the system via Drude absorption of low-frequency radiation leads to bistability of the steady-state equilibrium. The first is a low-temperature state, in which almost all resident charge carriers are bound into trions. The second state occurs at high temperatures, where most trions are dissociated; in this regime, the heating is more efficient due to the higher Drude conductivity of unbound charge carriers compared to trions. Switching between these two states occurs on a timescale of tens to hundreds of picoseconds and is accompanied by a jump in various observables such as temperature, current, and the intensity of exciton or trion luminescence.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现电子熵和比热展现出快速和慢速的磁热振荡以及显著的磁热效应。特别识别出$S_e$和$C_e$中的显著自相似性，追踪到心形比热轮廓和隧道状熵轮廓，这些模式在特定晶格依赖的磁通量下重复出现。

Abstract: Fractal electronic spectra arising from the competition between lattice periodicity and magnetic flux are a fundamental hallmark of two-dimensional quantum systems. While the spectral properties of Hofstadter butterflies are well documented, their thermodynamic response has remained remarkably unexplored. We present an original characterization of the electronic entropy $S_{e}$, and specific heat $C_{e}$, at half-filling, for square, honeycomb, and triangular lattices under a magnetic field. We demonstrate that these observables exhibit fast and slow magneto-thermo oscillations and pronounced magnetocaloric effects. We identify striking self-similarity in $S_e$ and $C_e$, tracing heart-shaped specific heat and tunnel-like entropy contours that repeat at specific lattice-dependent magnetic fluxes. Entropy minima at low temperatures play a remarkable role, acting as fingerprints for the butterfly spines, resolving the underlying fractal spectra. These findings may establish thermal measurements as high-resolution spectroscopic probes, providing a robust framework for recognizing fractal signatures through thermodynamics in diverse nanostructures.

### [249] [Spin-selective elliptic optical dichroism and perfectly spin-polarized third-order nonlinear photocurrent in altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07490)
*Motohiko Ezawa*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: It is shown that the low-energy theory of a $d$-wave altermagnet is characterized by anisotropic Dirac cones with up and down spins based on a recently proposed tight-binding model. Spin-selective perfect elliptic dichroism occurs in this system, where only up-spin or down-spin electrons are excited by elliptically polarized light. Then, we derive a formula for the third-order photocurrent induced by applying both elliptically polarized light and static electric field, which is described in terms of quantum metric and the Berry curvature. Based on it, we predict only up-spin polarized current is induced. It is the leading order of photocurrent because the second-order photocurrent such as the injection current and the shift current are prohibited due to inversion symmetry inherent to altermagnets. It is intriguing that nonzero photocurrent is induced only by the anisotropy of the Dirac cones. Our results will be useful for future photo-excited spintronics based on altermagnets.

To address the trade-off between the accuracy and complexity of resulting barrier configurations, regularization techniques are incorporated into the optimization process. Our approach demonstrates the potential for highly tunable electronic transport in graphene-based systems by exploiting evolution-inspired optimization techniques.

Motivation: 非厄米系统为探索非平衡现象提供了独特框架，而altermagnets作为一类新型磁性材料，具有受晶体对称性保护的非传统自旋劈裂能带。研究两者相互作用旨在探索通过可控非保守过程操纵自旋自由度的新途径。

Method: 研究聚焦于Edelstein效应，在d波交替磁体（d-wave altermagnets）和p波非常规磁体（p-wave unconventional magnets）中引入非厄米性，分析其对磁化率分量的影响。方法基于对称性分析，考察序参数对称性与非保守过程之间的相互作用。

Result: 非厄米性在交替磁体中开启了厄米对应物无法获得的新奇磁化率分量，这些通道对序参数的底层对称性高度敏感。系统的非保守特性导致特定自旋分量的选择性增益和损失，该现象可通过耗散与交替磁序的相互作用进行调控。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，非厄米交替磁体中的磁化率分量展现出严格依赖于奈尔矢量（Néel vector）取向的增益/损失分布特征，这为通过新兴磁性材料中的可控非保守过程操纵自旋自由度提供了新途径。

Abstract: The recent interest in non-Hermitian (NH) systems has significantly broadened their application across condensed matter physics, offering a unique framework to explore out-of-equilibrium phenomena. Simultaneously, altermagnets have emerged as a distinct magnetic class, characterized by unconventional spin-split bands protected by crystal symmetries. In this work, we investigate the interplay between non-Hermitian dynamics and spin transport in these materials, focusing on the Edelstein effect. We demonstrate that the introduction of non-Hermiticity in $d$-wave altermagnets and $p$-wave unconventional magnets opens novel susceptibility components that are inaccessible in Hermitian counterparts. Our analysis reveals that these susceptibility channels are highly sensitive to the underlying symmetry of the order parameter. Crucially, our results show that the non-conservative nature of the system leads to the selective gain and loss of specific spin components, a phenomenon that can be tuned by the interplay between dissipation and the altermagnetic order. These components exhibit a distinct gain/loss profile that depends strictly on the Néel vector orientation, providing a new route for manipulating spin degrees of freedom through controlled non-conservative processes in emerging magnetic materials

Abstract: Efficient transport of spin and orbital moments, and their electrical detection, are among the main challenges in spintronics and orbitronics. In magnetic insulators, these currents are mediated by magnons. In addition to carrying spin and orbital moment, the orbital motion of a magnon combined with its magnetic moment, generates an effective electric dipole moment. Here, we develop a theoretical framework for Seebeck- and Nernst-type transport of the magnon orbital moment (MOM) and its associated electric dipole moment (EDM). We show that a measurable transverse voltage generated by the EDM current provides a direct electrical detection scheme for magnon orbital transport. In this work, we propose and quantitatively analyze an experimental procedure, based on gate reflectometry, which enables this four-state discrimination in a single measurement. We provide an intuitive recipe to maximize the contrast between the quantum capacitances of the four basis states. Our results highlight a realistic opportunity to mitigate the overhead of readout ancilla qubits in a spin-based quantum computer.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在Rashba-Dresselhaus哈密顿量框架内，解析计算量子度量分量，分析其在持久自旋螺旋条件下的行为。进一步研究高阶立方自旋轨道相互作用（higher-order cubic spin-orbit interactions）对几何响应的正则化作用及量子度量标度行为的影响。

Conclusion: 量子几何（quantum geometry）为识别和表征持久自旋螺旋及相关对称性保护自旋纹理提供了强大框架，量子度量可作为此类系统的敏感几何探针。

Abstract: Persistent spin helices are a manifestation of symmetry-protected spin textures in systems with balanced spin-orbit coupling. They enable long-lived spin structures that are of interest for spintronics and coherent spin manipulation. The quantum metric has recently emerged as a promising tool for characterizing the geometric structure of quantum states. Here, we demonstrate that the quantum metric provides a sensitive geometric probe of the persistent spin helix. Within the Rashba-Dresselhaus Hamiltonian, we analytically evaluate the quantum metric components and uncover a divergent geometric contribution that emerges precisely at the persistent spin helix condition. We reveal that this divergence originates from a hidden line degeneracy that forms when the strengths of Rashba and Dresselhaus spin-orbit coupling become equal. We further study the role of higher-order cubic spin-orbit interactions and determine how these corrections regularize the geometric response and control the scaling behavior of the quantum metric. Our results establish quantum geometry as a powerful framework for identifying and characterizing persistent spin helices and related symmetry-protected spin textures.

### [258] [Layer-Dependent Orbital Magnetization in Graphene-Haldane Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08170)
*Sovan Ghosh,Bheema Lingam Chittari*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过紧束缚模型和现代轨道磁化理论，揭示了菱面体多层石墨烯（RMG）在Haldane衬底邻近耦合下的层数依赖磁响应特性。研究发现三层和四层石墨烯在空穴掺杂区存在偏压诱导的轨道磁化符号反转现象，而双层石墨烯则无此特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 菱面体多层石墨烯（rhombohedral multilayer graphene, RMG）与Haldane衬底邻近耦合为研究能带拓扑、层数和轨道磁性的电场控制之间的相互作用提供了平台。该研究旨在探索层数如何作为轨道磁性的关键调控参数。

Method: 采用紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）和现代轨道磁化理论（modern theory of orbital magnetization），研究双层、三层和四层石墨烯在Haldane邻近耦合下的层依赖磁响应。将总轨道磁化分解为自旋转（self-rotation, M_SR）和质心（center-of-mass, M_C）贡献。

Result: 单层石墨烯产生全局拓扑能隙并具有量子化的磁化斜率，而多层系统由于未受扰动的子晶格相关的受保护低能带而保持金属性。尽管缺乏全局能隙，有限的谷对比贝里曲率（valley-contrasting Berry curvature）产生非平凡的层依赖陈数（Chern numbers）。三层和四层石墨烯在空穴掺杂区显示出偏压诱导的轨道磁化符号反转，临界阈值分别为Δ≃-55 meV（3LG）和-50 meV（4LG），而双层石墨烯无此现象。

Conclusion: 拓扑邻近多层石墨烯为电场可操纵的轨道电子学（orbitronic）和谷电子学（valleytronic）器件提供了多功能平台。层数作为轨道磁性的关键调控参数，该效应在空穴和电子掺杂区均存在，展示了层数依赖的磁响应特性。

Abstract: Rhombohedral multilayer graphene (RMG) proximity-coupled to a Haldane substrate provides a platform to investigate the interplay between band topology, layer number, and electric-field control of orbital magnetism. Using a tight-binding model and the modern theory of orbital magnetization, we study the layer-dependent magnetic response in bilayer, trilayer, and tetralayer graphene under Haldane proximity. While monolayer graphene develops a global topological gap with quantized magnetization slope, multilayer systems remain metallic due to protected low-energy bands associated with unperturbed sublattices. Despite the absence of a global gap, finite valley-contrasting Berry curvature produces non-trivial layer-dependent Chern numbers. We decompose the total orbital magnetization into self-rotation ($M_{\mathrm{SR}}$) and center-of-mass ($M_C$) contributions, revealing their distinct behaviors across doping and applied interlayer bias. In bilayer graphene, magnetization remains negative and monotonic. Remarkably, trilayer and tetralayer graphene display a bias-induced sign reversal of orbital magnetization beyond critical thresholds ($Δ\simeq -55$ meV for 3LG, $-50$ meV for 4LG) in the hole-doped regime, a feature completely absent in the bilayer. The effect persists across both hole and electron doping, demonstrating that layer count serves as a key tuning parameter for orbital magnetism. Our findings establish topologically proximitized multilayer graphene as a versatile platform for electric-field-manipulable orbitronic and valleytronic devices.

### [259] [All-in-plane image sensors free from readout integrated circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08178)

Such access is especially challenging for ultra-miniaturized pixels, for heterogeneously integrated sensing and readout layers in long-wavelength detectors, and for novel light-sensing materials with unestablished integration to silicon chips. Here, we introduce and experimentally validate a novel imaging approach that does not require electrical connections to individual pixels. The sensor matrix involves photoresistive pixels connected neighbor-to-neighbor and packed into a rectangular lattice. The signal readout is based on electrical impedance tomography applied to the photoresistance: the photovoltage is measured at the matrix boundary at various positions of injected bias current, and the image is reconstructed algorithmically. We present experimental validations for moderate-size infrared imagers based on multilayer graphene (24 pixels) and amorphous vanadium oxide (264 pixels). The reconstruction procedure is mathematically stable, sustainable to variations of pixel resistivity and photosensitivity, and its complexity is that of linear system solution. The proposed method enables unprecedented architecture simplification of imaging devices.

</details>


### [260] [Bound Trions in Two-Dimensional Monolayers: A Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08346)
*Roman Ya. Kezerashvili*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文综述了二维半导体中三粒子激子（trion）的理论与实验进展，重点分析其结合能增强机制、计算方法以及与环境因素、外场的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三粒子激子（trion）作为二维半导体中的核心准粒子，其库仑束缚特性因介电屏蔽减弱和量子限制效应而显著增强。本综述旨在系统梳理该领域的理论与实验进展，为理解低维系统中三粒子激子的物理性质提供全面视角。

Method: 采用严格的少体（few-body）方法分析三粒子激子，重点考察介电环境（dielectric environment）、各向异性（anisotropy）以及外加电磁场的影响。利用二维构型空间（two-dimensional configuration spaces）中的计算方法描述其特性。

Result: 综述表明，降低的介电屏蔽和量子限制显著增强了三粒子激子的结合能，使其在实验中易于观测。同时，降低的维度性（reduced dimensionality）改变了其结构和稳定性，并与多体现象如屏蔽效应、朗道能级混合（Landau-level mixing）以及激子-极化子交叉（exciton-polaron crossover）存在关联。

Conclusion: 本综述系统总结了二维半导体中三粒子激子的物理特性，强调了少体方法的重要性，并指出了介电环境、维度和外场对其性质的关键影响，为未来相关研究提供了理论基础和方向指引。

Abstract: Trions -- Coulomb-bound three-particle excitations composed of two like-charge carriers and one oppositely charged carrier -- are central quasiparticles in two-dimensional semiconductors. Reduced dielectric screening and quantum confinement strongly enhance their binding energies, making them robust and experimentally accessible. This review surveys theoretical and experimental advances in trion physics, emphasizing rigorous few-body approaches and the role of dielectric environment, anisotropy, and external electric and magnetic fields. We analyze computational methods for describing trions in two-dimensional configuration spaces and discuss how reduced dimensionality modifies their structure and stability. Connections to many-body phenomena, including screening, Landau-level mixing, and exciton--polaron crossover, are also highlighted.

</details>


### [261] [Optical manipulation of valley coherence via Landau level transitions in black phosphorus and WTe2 monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08357)
*Xinyu Mu,Shihao Li,Xiaoying Zhou,Guangyi Jia*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该理论研究黑磷（BP）和WTe2单层材料中通过朗道能级（Landau level）间跃迁调控的谷量子干涉效应，发现各向异性环境可增强干涉强度20倍以上，干涉谱呈现C2旋转对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 谷相干性（valley coherence）对探索基础量子现象和发展下一代谷电子学（valleytronic）器件具有重要意义。研究旨在通过朗道能级间跃迁工程化调控谷量子干涉效应。

Method: 采用理论研究方法，分析黑磷（BP）和WTe2单层材料中不同朗道能级（Landau level）间跃迁（δn = n'- n = -4, -2, 0, +2, +4）引起的谷量子干涉。重点关注沿扶手椅（armchair）和锯齿（zigzag）方向的电子跃迁概率差异。

Result: 与非朗道量子化（non-Landau-quantized）体系相比，各向异性环境使谷量子干涉增强超过20倍甚至更强。黑磷因其更大的电子跃迁概率方向差异，能更有效地增强谷量子干涉响应。干涉条纹呈现不同光谱特征，但归一化干涉强度均遵循磁场和朗道能级指数的两个指数函数。

Conclusion: 黑磷和WTe2单层材料中的谷量子干涉可通过朗道能级间跃迁有效调控，各向异性环境显著增强干涉效应。干涉光谱表现出关于90°晶体学方位角的C2旋转对称性，为谷电子学器件设计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Valley coherence is of great significance for exploring fundamental quantum phenomena and developing next-generation valleytronic devices. Herein, we theoretically investigate the valley quantum interference engineered by inter-Landau level (LL) transitions in black phosphorus (BP) and WTe2 monolayers. In contrast to the non-Landau-quantized regime, valley quantum interference is enhanced by over 20-fold, or even significantly stronger, in virtue of striking anisotropic environment. Such anisotropy originates from the distinct electron transition probabilities along the armchair and zigzag directions of BP and WTe2 monolayers. Especially, BP is capable of more effectively strengthening the valley quantum interference response due to its greater directional disparity in electron transition probabilities. The interference fringes also present distinct spectral profiles (e.g., different dip and peak numbers in one interference period) owing to different transition selection rules in BP and WTe2 monolayers. In spite of these discrepancies, normalized interference intensities follow two exponential functions of magnetic field and Landau level index for all the transitions δn = n'- n = -4, -2, 0, +2, +4 (where n and n' indicate the LL indexes of valence and conduction bands, respectively), and the interference spectra exhibit C2 rotational symmetry about the crystallographic azimuthal angle of 90°.

</details>


### [262] [Non-local effects in charge and energy transport with dissipative electrodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08464)
*Rodolfo A. Jalabert*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过在静电自洽方案（electrostatically self-consistent scheme）中描述连接电极内的非弹性散射，并限制在准一维几何、弱激发和低温条件下，推导出电流密度和耗散功率的通用表达式。

Result: 获得了适用于能量无关平均自由程（energy-independent mean-free-path）或能量无关弛豫率（energy-independent relaxation-rate）不同情况下的通用表达式，并阐明了纳米器件两侧的耗散不对称性（dissipation asymmetry）和观测局部最大耗散功率加热点的条件。

Conclusion: 研究成功扩展了散射理论以包含非局域耗散效应，为理解纳米尺度热耗散行为提供了理论工具，这些结果可以用定义纳米器件及其环境的关键参数来表述。

Abstract: Recent advances in nano-thermometry motivate the extension of the Landauer-Büttiker scattering theory as to include the non-local dissipation associated with charge transport. Such a program is implemented by describing the inelastic scattering in the connecting electrodes within an electrostatically self-consistent scheme. The restriction to quasi-one-dimensional geometries, weak excitation and low temperature allows to obtain general expressions of the current density and the dissipated power, valid in different regimes, for the cases of an energy-independent mean-free-path or an energy-independent relaxation-rate. In particular, the dissipation asymmetry at both sides of a nano-device and the conditions for observing heating spots with a local maximum of the dissipated power are formulated in terms of the key parameters that define the nano-device and its environment.

### [263] [Microwave response of electrically driven spins in a three-qubit quantum processor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08577)
*Tanner M. Janda,Heun Mo Yoo,Connor Nasseraddin,Adam R. Mills,Zhaoyi Joy Zheng,Jason R. Petta*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过精确校准微波驱动幅度，发现Loss-DiVincenzo单自旋量子比特的Rabi频率与驱动幅度呈线性关系，表明先前观察到的非线性响应并非该类型量子比特的普遍特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电偶极自旋共振（EDSR）中，单自旋在微磁体产生的场梯度中被电驱动。虽然EDSR已在许多器件中实现高保真度门操作，但存在关于Rabi频率随微波驱动幅度呈现意外非线性关系的报告。

Method: 研究仔细测量了Loss-DiVincenzo（LD）单自旋量子比特对共振驱动以及同时施加共振和非共振驱动的响应，这种场景在实际量子处理器中会遇到。微波幅度经过仔细校准。

Result: 研究发现，在微波幅度精确校准后，Rabi频率与驱动幅度呈线性比例关系，即使所有三个自旋同时被驱动时也是如此。同时确定，非共振驱动引起的加热诱导共振频率偏移与典型的时间漂移相当。

Conclusion: 结果表明，先前观察到的非线性响应并非Loss-DiVincenzo自旋量子比特的普遍特征，为实际量子处理器中多量子比特同时操作提供了重要参考。

Abstract: In electric dipole spin resonance (EDSR), a single spin is electrically driven in the field gradient produced by a micromagnet. While EDSR has enabled high fidelity gate operations in many devices, there are reports of unexpected non-linearities in the Rabi frequency as a function of microwave drive amplitude. We carefully measure the response of Loss-DiVincenzo (LD) single spin qubits to resonant drives as well as simultaneous resonant and off-resonant drives, as would be encountered in a realistic quantum processor. With the microwave amplitude carefully calibrated, we find that the Rabi frequency scales linearly with drive amplitude, even when all three spins are driven simultaneously. We also determine that heating-induced resonance frequency shifts from off-resonant drives are comparable to typical temporal drifts. Our results indicate that the previously observed nonlinear response is not a general feature of LD spin qubits.

### [264] [Nonlinear Mode Coupling in Silicon Nitride Membrane Resonators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08689)
*Soumya Kanti Das,Nishta Arora,Hridhay A S,Akshay Naik,Chandan Samanta*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验观测和理论建模，揭示了高应力方形氮化硅薄膜谐振器中非线性模式耦合现象，建立了基于Kirchhoff-Love板理论的定量框架，为多模频率调谐和机械传感提供了可控资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 振动模式间的非线性相互作用对于理解纳米机械谐振器的动态响应至关重要。研究旨在探索高应力方形氮化硅薄膜谐振器中非线性模式耦合的实验观测和理论建模。

Method: 通过增加基模和高阶弯曲模式的振幅，量化张力介导的几何非线性引起的基模频率偏移。建立了基于Kirchhoff-Love板理论的定量理论框架，该框架同时包含固有Duffing非线性和非线性模式间耦合。

Result: 理论模型与实验测量在(1,1)-(2,1)和(1,1)-(2,2)模式对中显示出良好的一致性。进一步计算了跨模式族的非线性耦合矩阵，揭示了模式对称性和空间重叠在调控模式间相互作用中的作用。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了非线性模式耦合作为多模频率调谐和机械传感的可控资源，为纳米机械谐振器的动态响应理解提供了重要基础。

Abstract: Nonlinear interactions between vibrational modes play a crucial role in understanding the dynamical response of nanomechanical resonators. Here, we report the experimental observation and theoretical modeling of nonlinear mode coupling in a high-stress square silicon nitride membrane resonator. We quantify frequency shifts of the fundamental mode arising from tension-mediated geometric nonlinearity by increasing the amplitude of the fundamental mode and higher-order flexural modes. A quantitative theoretical framework based on Kirchhoff-Love plate theory is developed, which incorporates both intrinsic Duffing nonlinearity and nonlinear intermodal coupling and shows good agreement with experimental measurements for the (1,1)-(2,1) and (1,1)-(2,2) mode pairs. We further compute the nonlinear coupling matrix across mode families, revealing the role of mode symmetry and spatial overlap in governing intermodal interactions. These results establish nonlinear mode coupling as a controllable resource for multimode frequency tuning and mechanical transduction.

### [265] [Variational approach to nonholonomic and inequality-constrained mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2409.11063)
*A. Rothkopf,W. A. Horowitz*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 该论文为非完整系统构建了一个显式且通用的作用量（action）表述，通过变分原理恢复拉格朗日-达朗贝尔方程的正确动力学，并利用数值优化验证了该框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分原理在经典力学中占据核心地位，但非完整系统（受非完整速度约束或位置不等式约束）长期以来缺乏通用的极值作用量处理。本文旨在解决这一理论缺口，为非完整系统建立变分力学框架。

Method: 受量子Schwinger-Keldysh作用量形式（由Galley重新发现）的经典极限启发，构建了非完整运动的显式通用作用量。该方法通过标量作用量的极值化来恢复拉格朗日-达朗贝尔方程的正确动力学。

Result: 成功构建了非完整系统的通用作用量表述，并通过直接数值优化该新作用量（绕过运动方程）在典型示例上验证了方法的有效性。该框架扩展了变分力学的适用范围。

Conclusion: 该工作为非完整系统提供了首个通用变分作用量表述，成功恢复了拉格朗日-达朗贝尔动力学。该框架扩展了变分力学的应用范围，并为约束系统提供了新的分析和计算工具。

Abstract: Variational principles play a central role in classical mechanics, providing compact formulations of dynamics and direct access to conserved quantities. While holonomic systems admit well-known action formulations, non-holonomic systems -- subject to non-integrable velocity constraints or position inequality constraints -- have long resisted a general extremized action treatment. In this work, we construct an explicit and general action for non-holonomic motion, motivated by the classical limit of the quantum Schwinger-Keldysh action formalism, rediscovered by Galley. Our formulation recovers the correct dynamics of the Lagrange-d'Alembert equations via extremization of a scalar action. We validate the approach on canonical examples using direct numerical optimization of the novel action, bypassing equations of motion. Our framework extends the reach of variational mechanics and offers new analytical and computational tools for constrained systems.

</details>


### [266] [Physical properties of elementary particles: Inertia and Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08456)
*Martin Rivas*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于惯性中心与相互作用中心关系的经典自旋粒子描述方法。当相互作用中心以光速运动时，该模型能够完全确定质量中心的动力学行为，并在量子化后满足狄拉克方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为基本粒子提供一种新的经典描述框架，通过区分惯性中心（center of mass）与相互作用中心（center of interaction）来建立自旋粒子的经典模型。这种区分能够统一描述点粒子模型和自旋粒子模型。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于两个物理中心关系的分析方法：如果惯性中心与相互作用中心重合，则得到点粒子模型；如果两者不同，则得到自旋粒子模型。特别地，当相互作用中心以光速运动时，该模型能够完全确定质量中心的动力学行为。

Result: 研究结果表明，当相互作用中心以光速运动时，该经典模型在量子化后能够满足狄拉克方程（Dirac's equation）。这为狄拉克粒子提供了一种经典的描述方法，即经典自旋狄拉克粒子（classical description of the spinning Dirac particle）。

Conclusion: 该论文成功建立了一种基于惯性中心与相互作用中心关系的经典自旋粒子描述框架。当相互作用中心以光速运动时，该模型不仅能够确定质量中心的动力学，而且在量子化后与狄拉克方程一致，为自旋粒子的经典描述提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: Matter has two physical properties: Inertia and interaction. If we define the center of mass of an elementary particle in relation to its inertia, and a center of interaction in relation to its interactive properties, there are only two possibilities to describe this elementary particle: that both points are the same or that they are different. If they are the same, what we describe is the point particle model, while if we consider them to be different, what we obtain is the description of an elementary spinning particle. If the center of interaction or center of charge is moving at the speed of light, completely determines also the dynamics of the center of mass, and when quantizing this model satisfies Dirac's equation. We obtain the classical description of the spinning Dirac particle.

</details>


### [267] [Unimode material based low-frequency underwater acoustic isolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08162)
*Yu Wei,Binghao Zhao,Fen Du,Yi Chen,Gengkai Hu*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了互补极值材料（complementary extremal materials）概念，即一种材料的软模（soft mode）是另一种材料的硬模（hard mode）。通过研究各向同性单模（unimode）与双模（bimode）材料的界面，实现了纵波到横波的完美模式转换，并提出了低频水下声学绝缘体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极值材料（extremal materials）作为一类特殊的柯西材料（Cauchy materials），其弹性张量具有零特征值，对应零应变能的软模。这类材料已实现声子偏振器、瑞利波隔离器等功能，但两种极值材料界面的丰富波行为尚未充分探索。

Method: 提出互补极值材料概念，研究各向同性单模材料与各向同性双模材料之间的界面特性。通过设计超材料（metamaterials）并采用有效介质模型（effective-medium modeling）进行验证。

Result: 界面实现了纵波到横波的完美模式转换（perfect mode conversion）。基于互补极值材料提出了低频水下声学绝缘体（low-frequency underwater acoustic insulator）。

Conclusion: 互补极值材料在控制弹性波偏振（elastic wave polarization）和水声传播方面具有重要潜力，为波操控提供了新途径。

Abstract: Extremal materials are a specific class of Cauchy materials whose elasticity tensor has one or more zero eigenvalues. Each zero eigenvalue corresponds to a soft mode requiring zero strain energy, while non-zero eigenvalues correspond to hard modes that cost energy. According to the number, N, of zero eigenvalues, these materials can be referred to as unimode (N=1), bimode (N=2), etc. Extremal materials have enabled novel functions beyond conventional Cauchy media, e.g., phonon polarizers, Rayleigh wave isolators and underwater acoustic cloaks. These functions typically require a single extremal material. Interfaces between two extremal materials exhibit rich wave behaviors, yet have been seldom explored. Here, we proposed the concept of complementary extremal materials, i.e., the soft mode of one extremal material is a hard mode of the other. As one example, we study the interface between an isotropic unimode material and an isotropic bimode material. We show that the interface allows perfect mode conversion from longitudinal waves to transverse waves. A low-frequency underwater acoustic insulator based on complementary extremal materials is proposed. Our finding has been verified with designed metamaterials and using effective-medium modeling. This work demonstrates the potential of complementary extremal materials in controlling elastic wave polarization and waterborne sound.

</details>
